 <hr>
  <h3 align="center">Darby Bible: Psalms</h3> 
 <p><a name="an_1:1">1:1</a> Blessed is the man that walketh not in the counsel of the  wicked, and standeth not in the way of sinners, and sitteth not  in the seat of scorners;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:2">1:2</a> But his delight is in Jehovah's law, and in his law doth he  meditate day and night.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:3">1:3</a> And he [is] as a tree planted by brooks of water, which  giveth its fruit in its season, and whose leaf fadeth not; and  all that he doeth prospereth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:4">1:4</a> The wicked are not so; but are as the chaff which the wind  driveth away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:5">1:5</a> Therefore the wicked shall not stand in the judgment, nor  sinners in the assembly of the righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:6">1:6</a> For Jehovah knoweth the way of the righteous, but the way of  the wicked shall perish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:1">2:1</a> Why are the nations in tumultuous agitation, and [why] do  the peoples meditate a vain thing?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:2">2:2</a> The kings of the earth set themselves, and the princes plot  together, against Jehovah and against his anointed:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:3">2:3</a> Let us break their bonds asunder, and cast away their cords  from us!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:4">2:4</a> He that dwelleth in the heavens shall laugh, the Lord shall  have them in derision.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:5">2:5</a> Then will he speak to them in his anger, and in his fierce  displeasure will he terrify them:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:6">2:6</a> And *I* have anointed my king upon Zion, the hill of my  holiness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:7">2:7</a> I will declare the decree: Jehovah hath said unto me, Thou  art my Son; *I* this day have begotten thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:8">2:8</a> Ask of me, and I will give thee nations for an inheritance,  and for thy possession the ends of the earth:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:9">2:9</a> Thou shalt break them with a sceptre of iron, as a potter's  vessel thou shalt dash them in pieces.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:10">2:10</a> And now, O kings, be ye wise, be admonished, ye judges of  the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:11">2:11</a> Serve Jehovah with fear, and rejoice with trembling.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:12">2:12</a> Kiss the Son, lest he be angry, and ye perish in the way,  though his anger burn but a little. Blessed are all who have  their trust in him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:1">3:1</a> {A Psalm of David, when he fled from Absalom his son.}  Jehovah, how many are they that trouble me, many they that rise  up against me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:2">3:2</a> Many say of my soul, There is no salvation for him in God.  Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:3">3:3</a> But thou, Jehovah, art a shield about me; my glory, and the  lifter up of my head.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:4">3:4</a> With my voice will I call to Jehovah, and he will answer me  from the hill of his holiness. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:5">3:5</a> I laid me down and slept; I awaked, for Jehovah sustaineth  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:6">3:6</a> I will not fear for myriads of the people that have set  themselves against me round about.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:7">3:7</a> Arise, Jehovah; save me, my God! For thou hast smitten all  mine enemies upon the cheekbone, thou hast broken the teeth of  the wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:8">3:8</a> Salvation is of Jehovah; thy blessing is upon thy people.  Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:1">4:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A Psalm of  David.} When I call, answer me, O God of my righteousness: in  pressure thou hast enlarged me; be gracious unto me, and hear  my prayer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:2">4:2</a> Ye sons of men, till when is my glory [to be put] to shame?  [How long] will ye love vanity, will ye seek after a lie?  Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:3">4:3</a> But know that Jehovah hath set apart the pious [man] for  himself: Jehovah will hear when I call unto him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:4">4:4</a> Be moved with anger, and sin not; meditate in your own  hearts upon your bed, and be still. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:5">4:5</a> Offer sacrifices of righteousness, and confide in Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:6">4:6</a> Many say, Who shall cause us to see good? Lift up upon us  the light of thy countenance, O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:7">4:7</a> Thou hast put joy in my heart, more than in the time that  their corn and their new wine was in abundance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:8">4:8</a> In peace will I both lay me down and sleep; for thou,  Jehovah, alone makest me to dwell in safety.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:1">5:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Upon Nehiloth. A Psalm of David.}  Give ear to my words, O Jehovah; consider my meditation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:2">5:2</a> Hearken unto the voice of my crying, my king and my God; for  to thee will I pray.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:3">5:3</a> Jehovah, in the morning shalt thou hear my voice; in the  morning will I address myself to thee, and will look up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:4">5:4</a> For thou art not a ùGod that hath pleasure in wickedness;  evil shall not sojourn with thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:5">5:5</a> Insolent fools shall not stand before thine eyes; thou  hatest all workers of iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:6">5:6</a> Thou wilt destroy them that speak lies: Jehovah abhorreth a  man of blood and deceit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:7">5:7</a> But as for me, in the greatness of thy loving-kindness will  I enter thy house; I will bow down toward the temple of thy  holiness in thy fear.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:8">5:8</a> Lead me, Jehovah, in thy righteousness, because of my foes;  make thy way plain before me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:9">5:9</a> For there is no certainty in their mouth; their inward part  is perversion, their throat is an open sepulchre; they flatter  with their tongue.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:10">5:10</a> Bring guilt upon them, O God; let them fall by their own  counsels: drive them out in the multitude of their  transgressions, for they have rebelled against thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:11">5:11</a> And all that trust in thee shall rejoice: for ever shall  they shout joyously, and thou wilt protect them; and they that  love thy name shall exult in thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:12">5:12</a> For thou, Jehovah, wilt bless the righteous [man]; with  favour wilt thou surround him as [with] a shield.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:1">6:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On stringed instruments, upon  Sheminith. A Psalm of David.} Jehovah, rebuke me not in thine  anger, and chasten me not in thy hot displeasure.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:2">6:2</a> Be gracious unto me, Jehovah, for I am withered; Jehovah,  heal me, for my bones tremble.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:3">6:3</a> And my soul trembleth exceedingly: and thou, Jehovah, till  how long?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:4">6:4</a> Return, Jehovah, free my soul; save me for thy  loving-kindness' sake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:5">6:5</a> For in death there is no remembrance of thee; in Sheol who  shall give thanks unto thee?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:6">6:6</a> I am wearied with my groaning; all the night make I my bed  to swim; I dissolve my couch with my tears.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:7">6:7</a> Mine eye wasteth away through grief; it hath grown old  because of all mine oppressors.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:8">6:8</a> Depart from me, all ye workers of iniquity; for Jehovah hath  heard the voice of my weeping.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:9">6:9</a> Jehovah hath heard my supplication; Jehovah receiveth my  prayer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:10">6:10</a> All mine enemies shall be ashamed and tremble exceedingly;  they will turn, they will be ashamed suddenly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:1">7:1</a> {Shiggaion of David, which he sang to Jehovah, concerning  the words of Cush the Benjaminite.} Jehovah my God, in thee  have I trusted: save me from all my pursuers, and deliver me;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:2">7:2</a> Lest he tear my soul like a lion, crushing it while there is  no deliverer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:3">7:3</a> Jehovah my God, if I have done this, if there be iniquity in  my hands;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:4">7:4</a> If I have rewarded evil to him that was at peace with me;  (indeed I have freed him that without cause oppressed me;)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:5">7:5</a> Let the enemy pursue after my soul, and take [it], and let  him tread down my life to the earth, and lay my glory in the  dust. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:6">7:6</a> Arise, Jehovah, in thine anger; lift thyself up against the  raging of mine oppressors, and awake for me: thou hast  commanded judgment.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:7">7:7</a> And the assembly of the peoples shall encompass thee; and  for their sakes return thou on high.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:8">7:8</a> Jehovah shall minister judgment to the peoples. Judge me,  Jehovah, according to my righteousness, and according to mine  integrity which is in me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:9">7:9</a> Oh let the wrong of the wicked come to an end, and establish  thou the righteous [man]; even thou that triest the hearts and  reins, the righteous God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:10">7:10</a> My shield is with God, who saveth the upright in heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:11">7:11</a> God is a righteous judge, and a ùGod who is indignant all  the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:12">7:12</a> If one turn not, he will sharpen his sword; he hath bent  his bow and made it ready,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:13">7:13</a> And he hath prepared for him instruments of death; his  arrows hath he made burning.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:14">7:14</a> Behold, he travaileth with iniquity, yea, he hath conceived  mischief, and brought forth falsehood:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:15">7:15</a> He digged a pit, and hollowed it out, and is fallen into  the hole that he made.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:16">7:16</a> His mischief shall return upon his own head, and his  violence shall come down upon his own pate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:17">7:17</a> I will praise Jehovah according to his righteousness, and  will sing forth the name of Jehovah the Most High.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:1">8:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Upon the Gittith. A Psalm of David.}  Jehovah our Lord, how excellent is thy name in all the earth!  who hast set thy majesty above the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:2">8:2</a> Out of the mouth of babes and sucklings hast thou  established praise because of thine adversaries, to still the  enemy and the avenger.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:3">8:3</a> When I see thy heavens, the work of thy fingers, the moon  and stars, which thou hast established;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:4">8:4</a> What is man, that thou art mindful of him? and the son of  man, that thou visitest him?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:5">8:5</a> Thou hast made him a little lower than the angels, and hast  crowned him with glory and splendour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:6">8:6</a> Thou hast made him to rule over the works of thy hands; thou  hast put everything under his feet:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:7">8:7</a> Sheep and oxen, all of them, and also the beasts of the  field;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:8">8:8</a> The fowl of the heavens, and the fishes of the sea,  [whatever] passeth through the paths of the seas.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:9">8:9</a> Jehovah our Lord, how excellent is thy name in all the  earth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:1">9:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Upon Muthlabben. A Psalm of David.}  I will praise Jehovah with my whole heart; I will recount all  thy marvellous works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:2">9:2</a> I will be glad and rejoice in thee; I will sing forth thy  name, O Most High.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:3">9:3</a> When mine enemies turned back, they stumbled and perished at  thy presence:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:4">9:4</a> For thou hast maintained my right and my cause. Thou sittest  on the throne, judging righteously.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:5">9:5</a> Thou hast rebuked the nations, thou hast destroyed the  wicked; thou hast put out their name for ever and ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:6">9:6</a> O enemy! destructions are ended for ever. -- Thou hast also  destroyed cities, even the remembrance of them hath perished.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:7">9:7</a> But Jehovah sitteth for ever; he hath ordained his throne  for judgment.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:8">9:8</a> And it is he that will judge the world with righteousness;  he shall execute judgment upon the peoples with equity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:9">9:9</a> And Jehovah will be a refuge to the oppressed one, a refuge  in times of distress.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:10">9:10</a> And they that know thy name will confide in thee; for thou,  Jehovah, hast not forsaken them that seek thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:11">9:11</a> Sing psalms to Jehovah who dwelleth in Zion; tell among the  peoples his doings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:12">9:12</a> For when he maketh inquisition for blood, he remembereth  them; the cry of the afflicted ones hath he not forgotten.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:13">9:13</a> Be gracious unto me, O Jehovah; consider mine affliction  from them that hate me, lifting me up from the gates of death:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:14">9:14</a> That I may declare all thy praise in the gates of the  daughter of Zion. I will be joyful in thy salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:15">9:15</a> The nations are sunk down in the pit [that] they made; in  the net that they hid is their own foot taken.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:16">9:16</a> Jehovah is known [by] the judgment he hath executed: the  wicked is ensnared in the work of his own hands. Higgaion.  Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:17">9:17</a> The wicked shall be turned into Sheol, all the nations that  forget God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:18">9:18</a> For the needy one shall not be forgotten alway; the hope of  the meek shall not perish for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:19">9:19</a> Arise, Jehovah; let not man prevail: let the nations be  judged in thy sight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:20">9:20</a> Put them in fear, Jehovah: that the nations may know  themselves to be but men. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:1">10:1</a> Why, Jehovah, standest thou afar off? [Why] hidest thou  thyself in times of distress?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:2">10:2</a> The wicked, in his pride, doth hotly pursue the afflicted.  They shall be taken in the devices that they have imagined.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:3">10:3</a> For the wicked boasteth of his soul's desire, and he  blesseth the covetous; he contemneth Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:4">10:4</a> The wicked [saith], in the haughtiness of his countenance,  He doth not search out: all his thoughts are, There is no God!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:5">10:5</a> His ways always succeed; thy judgments are far above out of  his sight; [as for] all his adversaries, he puffeth at them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:6">10:6</a> He saith in his heart, I shall not be moved; from  generation to generation I shall be in no adversity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:7">10:7</a> His mouth is full of cursing, and deceit, and oppression;  under his tongue is mischief and iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:8">10:8</a> He sitteth in the lurking-places of the villages; in the  secret places doth he slay the innocent: his eyes watch for the  wretched.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:9">10:9</a> He lieth in wait secretly, like a lion in his thicket; he  lieth in wait to catch the afflicted: he doth catch the  afflicted, drawing him into his net.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:10">10:10</a> He croucheth, he boweth down, that the wretched may fall  by his strong ones.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:11">10:11</a> He saith in his heart, ùGod hath forgotten, he hideth his  face, he will never see [it].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:12">10:12</a> Arise, Jehovah; O ùGod, lift up thy hand: forget not the  afflicted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:13">10:13</a> Wherefore doth the wicked contemn God? He hath said in his  heart, Thou wilt not require [it].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:14">10:14</a> Thou hast seen [it], for thou thyself beholdest trouble  and vexation, to requite by thy hand. The wretched committeth  himself unto thee; thou hast been the helper of the fatherless.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:15">10:15</a> Break thou the arm of the wicked, and as for the evil man,  seek out his wickedness [till] thou find none.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:16">10:16</a> Jehovah is King for ever and ever: the nations have  perished out of his land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:17">10:17</a> Jehovah, thou hast heard the desire of the meek, thou hast  established their heart: thou causest thine ear to hear,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:18">10:18</a> To do justice to the fatherless and the oppressed one,  that the man of the earth may terrify no more.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:1">11:1</a> {To the chief Musician. [A Psalm] of David.} In Jehovah  have I put my trust: how say ye to my soul, Flee [as] a bird to  your mountain?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:2">11:2</a> For behold, the wicked bend the bow, they make ready their  arrow upon the string, that they may in darkness shoot at the  upright in heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:3">11:3</a> If the foundations be destroyed, what shall the righteous  do?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:4">11:4</a> Jehovah [is] in the temple of his holiness; Jehovah, -- his  throne is in the heavens: his eyes behold, his eyelids try the  children of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:5">11:5</a> Jehovah trieth the righteous one; but the wicked, and him  that loveth violence, his soul hateth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:6">11:6</a> Upon the wicked he shall rain snares, fire and brimstone;  and scorching wind shall be the portion of their cup.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:7">11:7</a> For righteous is Jehovah; he loveth righteousness, his  countenance doth behold the upright.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:1">12:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Upon Sheminith. A Psalm of David.}  Save, Jehovah, for the godly man is gone; for the faithful have  failed from among the children of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:2">12:2</a> They speak falsehood every one with his neighbour: [with]  flattering lip, with a double heart, do they speak.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:3">12:3</a> Jehovah will cut off all flattering lips, the tongue that  speaketh proud things,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:4">12:4</a> Who have said, With our tongue will we prevail, our lips  are our own: who [is] lord over us?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:5">12:5</a> Because of the oppression of the afflicted, because of the  sighing of the needy, now will I arise, saith Jehovah, I will  set [him] in safety, at whom they puff.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:6">12:6</a> The words of Jehovah are pure words, silver tried in the  furnace of earth, purified seven times.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:7">12:7</a> Thou, Jehovah, wilt keep them, thou wilt preserve them from  this generation for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:8">12:8</a> The wicked walk about on every side, when vileness is  exalted among the children of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:1">13:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David.} How long,  Jehovah, wilt thou forget me for ever? how long wilt thou hide  thy face from me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:2">13:2</a> How long shall I take counsel in my soul, with sorrow in my  heart daily? how long shall mine enemy be exalted over me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:3">13:3</a> Consider, answer me, O Jehovah my God! lighten mine eyes,  lest I sleep the [sleep of] death;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:4">13:4</a> Lest mine enemy say, I have prevailed against him! [lest]  mine adversaries be joyful when I am moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:5">13:5</a> As for me, I have confided in thy loving-kindness; my heart  shall be joyful in thy salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:6">13:6</a> I will sing unto Jehovah, for he hath dealt bountifully  with me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:1">14:1</a> {To the chief Musician. [A Psalm] of David.} The fool hath  said in his heart, There is no God. They have corrupted  themselves, they have done abominable works: there is none that  doeth good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:2">14:2</a> Jehovah looked down from the heavens upon the children of  men, to see if there were any that did understand, that did  seek God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:3">14:3</a> They have all gone aside, they are together become corrupt:  there is none that doeth good, not even one.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:4">14:4</a> Have all the workers of iniquity no knowledge, eating up my  people [as] they eat bread? They call not upon Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:5">14:5</a> There were they in great fear; for God is in the generation  of the righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:6">14:6</a> Ye have shamed the counsel of the afflicted, because  Jehovah [was] his refuge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:7">14:7</a> Oh that the salvation of Israel were come out of Zion! When  Jehovah turneth again the captivity of his people, Jacob shall  be glad, Israel shall rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:1">15:1</a> {A Psalm of David.} Jehovah, who shall sojourn in thy tent?  who shall dwell in the hill of thy holiness?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:2">15:2</a> He that walketh uprightly, and worketh righteousness, and  speaketh the truth from his heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:3">15:3</a> [He that] slandereth not with his tongue, doeth not evil to  his companion, nor taketh up a reproach against his neighbour;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:4">15:4</a> In whose eyes the depraved person is contemned, and who  honoureth them that fear Jehovah; who, if he have sworn to his  own hurt, changeth it not;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:5">15:5</a> [He that] putteth not out his money to usury, nor taketh  reward against the innocent. He that doeth these [things] shall  never be moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:1">16:1</a> {Michtam of David.} Preserve me, O ùGod: for I trust in  thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:2">16:2</a> Thou [my soul] hast said to Jehovah, Thou art the Lord: my  goodness [extendeth] not to thee; --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:3">16:3</a> To the saints that are on the earth, and to the excellent  [thou hast said], In them is all my delight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:4">16:4</a> Their sorrows shall be multiplied that hasten after  another: their drink-offerings of blood will I not offer, and I  will not take up their names into my lips.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:5">16:5</a> Jehovah is the portion of mine inheritance and of my cup:  thou maintainest my lot.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:6">16:6</a> The lines are fallen unto me in pleasant places; yea, I  have a goodly heritage.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:7">16:7</a> I will bless Jehovah, who giveth me counsel; even in the  nights my reins instruct me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:8">16:8</a> I have set Jehovah continually before me; because [he is]  at my right hand, I shall not be moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:9">16:9</a> Therefore my heart rejoiceth, and my glory exulteth; my  flesh moreover shall dwell in hope.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:10">16:10</a> For thou wilt not leave my soul to Sheol, neither wilt  thou allow thy Holy One to see corruption.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:11">16:11</a> Thou wilt make known to me the path of life: thy  countenance is fulness of joy; at thy right hand are pleasures  for evermore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:1">17:1</a> {A Prayer of David.} Hear the right, O Jehovah, attend unto  my cry; give ear unto my prayer, which is not out of feigned  lips.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:2">17:2</a> Let my judgment come forth from thy presence, let thine  eyes regard equity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:3">17:3</a> Thou hast proved my heart, thou hast visited me by night;  thou hast tried me, thou hast found nothing: my thought goeth  not beyond my word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:4">17:4</a> Concerning the works of men, by the word of thy lips I have  kept from the paths of the violent [man].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:5">17:5</a> When thou holdest my goings in thy paths, my footsteps slip  not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:6">17:6</a> I have called upon thee, for thou answerest me, O ùGod.  Incline thine ear unto me, hear my speech.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:7">17:7</a> Shew wondrously thy loving-kindnesses, O thou that savest  by thy right hand them that trust [in thee] from those that  rise up [against them].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:8">17:8</a> Keep me as the apple of the eye, hide me under the shadow  of thy wings,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:9">17:9</a> From the wicked that destroy me, my deadly enemies, who  compass me about.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:10">17:10</a> They are enclosed in their own fat; with their mouth they  speak proudly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:11">17:11</a> They have now encompassed us in our steps; their eyes have  they set, bowing down to the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:12">17:12</a> He is like a lion that is greedy of its prey, and as a  young lion lurking in secret places.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:13">17:13</a> Arise, Jehovah, anticipate him, cast him down: deliver my  soul from the wicked, thy sword;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:14">17:14</a> From men [who are] thy hand, O Jehovah, from men of this  age: their portion is in [this] life, and their belly thou  fillest with thy hid [treasure]; they have their fill of sons,  and leave the rest of their [substance] to their children.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:15">17:15</a> As for me, I will behold thy face in righteousness; I  shall be satisfied, when I awake, with thy likeness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:1">18:1</a> {To the chief Musician. [A Psalm] of David, the servant of  Jehovah, who spoke to Jehovah the words of this song in the day  that Jehovah had delivered him out of the hand of all his  enemies and out of the hand of Saul. And he said,} I will love  thee, O Jehovah, my strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:2">18:2</a> Jehovah is my rock, and my fortress, and my deliverer; my  ùGod, my rock, in whom I will trust; my shield, and the horn of  my salvation, my high tower.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:3">18:3</a> I will call upon Jehovah, who is to be praised: so shall I  be saved from mine enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:4">18:4</a> The bands of death encompassed me, and torrents of Belial  made me afraid.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:5">18:5</a> The bands of Sheol surrounded me, the cords of death  encountered me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:6">18:6</a> In my distress I called upon Jehovah, and I cried out to my  God; he heard my voice out of his temple, and my cry came  before him, into his ears.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:7">18:7</a> Then the earth shook and quaked, and the foundations of the  mountains trembled and shook, because he was wroth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:8">18:8</a> There went up a smoke out of his nostrils, and fire out of  his mouth devoured: coals burned forth from it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:9">18:9</a> And he bowed the heavens, and came down; and darkness was  under his feet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:10">18:10</a> And he rode upon a cherub and did fly; yea, he flew fast  upon the wings of the wind.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:11">18:11</a> He made darkness his secret place, his tent round about  him: darkness of waters, thick clouds of the skies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:12">18:12</a> From the brightness before him his thick clouds passed  forth: hail and coals of fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:13">18:13</a> And Jehovah thundered in the heavens, and the Most High  uttered his voice: hail and coals of fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:14">18:14</a> And he sent his arrows, and scattered [mine enemies]; and  he shot forth lightnings, and discomfited them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:15">18:15</a> And the beds of the waters were seen, and the foundations  of the world were uncovered at thy rebuke, Jehovah, at the  blast of the breath of thy nostrils.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:16">18:16</a> He reached forth from above, he took me, he drew me out of  great waters:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:17">18:17</a> He delivered me from my strong enemy, and from them that  hated me; for they were mightier than I.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:18">18:18</a> They encountered me in the day of my calamity, but Jehovah  was my stay.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:19">18:19</a> And he brought me forth into a large place; he delivered  me, because he delighted in me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:20">18:20</a> Jehovah hath rewarded me according to my righteousness;  according to the cleanness of my hands hath he recompensed me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:21">18:21</a> For I have kept the ways of Jehovah, and have not wickedly  departed from my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:22">18:22</a> For all his ordinances were before me, and I did not put  away his statutes from me;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:23">18:23</a> And I was upright with him, and kept myself from mine  iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:24">18:24</a> And Jehovah hath recompensed me according to my  righteousness, according to the cleanness of my hands in his  sight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:25">18:25</a> With the gracious thou dost shew thyself gracious; with  the upright man thou dost shew thyself upright;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:26">18:26</a> With the pure thou dost shew thyself pure; and with the  perverse thou dost shew thyself contrary.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:27">18:27</a> For it is thou that savest the afflicted people; but the  haughty eyes wilt thou bring down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:28">18:28</a> For it is thou that makest my lamp to shine: Jehovah my  God enlighteneth my darkness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:29">18:29</a> For by thee I have run through a troop; and by my God have  I leaped over a wall.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:30">18:30</a> As for ùGod, his way is perfect; the word of Jehovah is  tried: he is a shield to all that trust in him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:31">18:31</a> For who is +God save Jehovah? and who is a rock if not our  God?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:32">18:32</a> The ùGod who girdeth me with strength, and maketh my way  perfect,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:33">18:33</a> Who maketh my feet like hinds' [feet], and setteth me upon  my high places;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:34">18:34</a> Who teacheth my hands to war, and mine arms bend a bow of  brass;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:35">18:35</a> And thou didst give me the shield of thy salvation, and  thy right hand held me up; and thy condescending gentleness  hath made me great.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:36">18:36</a> Thou didst enlarge my steps under me, and mine ankles have  not wavered.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:37">18:37</a> I pursued mine enemies, and overtook them; and I turned  not again till they were consumed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:38">18:38</a> I crushed them, and they were not able to rise: they fell  under my feet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:39">18:39</a> And thou girdedst me with strength to battle; thou didst  subdue under me those that rose up against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:40">18:40</a> And mine enemies didst thou make to turn their backs unto  me, and those that hated me I destroyed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:41">18:41</a> They cried, and there was none to save; -- unto Jehovah,  and he answered them not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:42">18:42</a> And I did beat them small as dust before the wind; I did  cast them out as the mire of the streets.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:43">18:43</a> Thou hast delivered me from the strivings of the people;  thou hast made me the head of the nations: a people I knew not  doth serve me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:44">18:44</a> At the hearing of the ear, they obey me: strangers come  cringing unto me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:45">18:45</a> Strangers have faded away, and they come trembling forth  from their close places.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:46">18:46</a> Jehovah liveth; and blessed be my rock; and exalted be the  God of my salvation,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:47">18:47</a> The ùGod who hath avenged me, and hath subjected the  peoples to me;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:48">18:48</a> Who hath delivered me from mine enemies: yea, thou hast  lifted me up above them that rose up against me; from the man  of violence hast thou delivered me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:49">18:49</a> Therefore will I give thanks to thee, Jehovah, among the  nations, and will sing psalms to thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:50">18:50</a> [It is he] who giveth great deliverances to his king, and  sheweth loving-kindness to his anointed, to David, and to his  seed for evermore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:1">19:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David.} The heavens  declare the glory of ùGod; and the expanse sheweth the work of  his hands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:2">19:2</a> Day unto day uttereth speech, and night unto night sheweth  knowledge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:3">19:3</a> There is no speech and there are no words, yet their voice  is heard.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:4">19:4</a> Their line is gone out through all the earth, and their  language to the extremity of the world. In them hath he set a  tent for the sun,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:5">19:5</a> And he is as a bridegroom going forth from his chamber; he  rejoiceth as a strong man to run the race.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:6">19:6</a> His going forth is from the end of the heavens, and his  circuit unto the ends of it; and there is nothing hid from the  heat thereof.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:7">19:7</a> The law of Jehovah is perfect, restoring the soul; the  testimony of Jehovah is sure, making wise the simple;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:8">19:8</a> The precepts of Jehovah are right, rejoicing the heart; the  commandment of Jehovah is pure, enlightening the eyes;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:9">19:9</a> The fear of Jehovah is clean, enduring for ever; the  judgments of Jehovah are truth, they are righteous altogether:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:10">19:10</a> They are more precious than gold, yea, than much fine  gold; and sweeter than honey and the dropping of the honeycomb.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:11">19:11</a> Moreover, by them is thy servant enlightened; in keeping  them there is great reward.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:12">19:12</a> Who understandeth [his] errors? Purify me from secret  [faults].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:13">19:13</a> Keep back thy servant also from presumptuous [sins]; let  them not have dominion over me: then shall I be perfect, and I  shall be innocent from great transgression.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:14">19:14</a> Let the words of my mouth and the meditation of my heart  be acceptable in thy sight, O Jehovah, my rock, and my  redeemer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:1">20:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David.} Jehovah answer  thee in the day of trouble; the name of the God of Jacob  protect thee;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:2">20:2</a> May he send thee help from the sanctuary, and strengthen  thee out of Zion;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:3">20:3</a> Remember all thine oblations, and accept thy  burnt-offering; Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:4">20:4</a> Grant thee according to thy heart, and fulfil all thy  counsels.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:5">20:5</a> We will triumph in thy salvation, and in the name of our  God will we set up our banners. Jehovah fulfil all thy  petitions!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:6">20:6</a> Now know I that Jehovah saveth his anointed; he answereth  him from the heavens of his holiness, with the saving strength  of his right hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:7">20:7</a> Some make mention of chariots, and some of horses, but we  of the name of Jehovah our God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:8">20:8</a> They are bowed down and fallen; but we are risen and stand  upright.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:9">20:9</a> Save, Jehovah! Let the king answer us in the day we call.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:1">21:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David.} The king shall  joy in thy strength, Jehovah; and in thy salvation how greatly  shall he rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:2">21:2</a> Thou hast given him his heart's desire, and hast not  withholden the request of his lips. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:3">21:3</a> For thou hast met him with the blessings of goodness; thou  hast set a crown of pure gold on his head.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:4">21:4</a> He asked life of thee; thou gavest [it] him, length of days  for ever and ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:5">21:5</a> His glory is great through thy salvation; majesty and  splendour hast thou laid upon him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:6">21:6</a> For thou hast made him to be blessings for ever; thou hast  filled him with joy by thy countenance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:7">21:7</a> For the king confideth in Jehovah: and through the  loving-kindness of the Most High he shall not be moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:8">21:8</a> Thy hand shall find out all thine enemies; thy right hand  shall find out those that hate thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:9">21:9</a> Thou shalt make them as a fiery furnace in the time of thy  presence; Jehovah shall swallow them up in his anger, and the  fire shall devour them:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:10">21:10</a> Their fruit shalt thou destroy from the earth, and their  seed from among the children of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:11">21:11</a> For they intended evil against thee; they imagined a  mischievous device, which they could not execute.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:12">21:12</a> For thou wilt make them turn their back; thou wilt make  ready thy bowstring against their face.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:13">21:13</a> Be thou exalted, Jehovah, in thine own strength: we will  sing and celebrate thy power.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:1">22:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Upon Aijeleth-Shahar. A Psalm of  David.} My ùGod, my ùGod, why hast thou forsaken me? [why art  thou] far from my salvation, from the words of my groaning?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:2">22:2</a> My God, I cry by day, and thou answerest not; and by night,  and there is no rest for me:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:3">22:3</a> And thou art holy, thou that dwellest amid the praises of  Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:4">22:4</a> Our fathers confided in thee: they confided, and thou didst  deliver them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:5">22:5</a> They cried unto thee, and were delivered; they confided in  thee, and were not confounded.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:6">22:6</a> But I am a worm, and no man; a reproach of men, and the  despised of the people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:7">22:7</a> All they that see me laugh me to scorn; they shoot out the  lip, they shake the head, [saying:]</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:8">22:8</a> Commit it to Jehovah -- let him rescue him; let him deliver  him, because he delighteth in him!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:9">22:9</a> But thou art he that took me out of the womb; thou didst  make me trust, upon my mother's breasts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:10">22:10</a> I was cast upon thee from the womb; thou art my ùGod from  my mother's belly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:11">22:11</a> Be not far from me, for trouble is near; for there is none  to help.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:12">22:12</a> Many bulls have encompassed me; Bashan's strong ones have  beset me round.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:13">22:13</a> They gape upon me with their mouth, [as] a ravening and a  roaring lion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:14">22:14</a> I am poured out like water, and all my bones are out of  joint: my heart is become like wax; it is melted in the midst  of my bowels.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:15">22:15</a> My strength is dried up like a potsherd, and my tongue  cleaveth to my palate; and thou hast laid me in the dust of  death.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:16">22:16</a> For dogs have encompassed me; an assembly of evil-doers  have surrounded me: they pierced my hands and my feet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:17">22:17</a> I may count all my bones. They look, they stare upon me;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:18">22:18</a> They part my garments among them, and cast lots upon my  vesture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:19">22:19</a> But thou, Jehovah, be not far [from me]; O my strength,  haste thee to help me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:20">22:20</a> Deliver my soul from the sword; my only one from the power  of the dog;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:21">22:21</a> Save me from the lion's mouth. Yea, from the horns of the  buffaloes hast thou answered me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:22">22:22</a> I will declare thy name unto my brethren, in the midst of  the congregation will I praise thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:23">22:23</a> Ye that fear Jehovah, praise him; all ye the seed of  Jacob, glorify him; and revere him, all ye the seed of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:24">22:24</a> For he hath not despised nor abhorred the affliction of  the afflicted; neither hath he hid his face from him: but when  he cried unto him, he heard.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:25">22:25</a> My praise is from thee, in the great congregation; I will  pay my vows before them that fear him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:26">22:26</a> The meek shall eat and be satisfied; they shall praise  Jehovah that seek him: your heart shall live for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:27">22:27</a> All the ends of the earth shall remember and turn unto  Jehovah, and all the families of the nations shall worship  before thee:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:28">22:28</a> For the kingdom is Jehovah's, and he ruleth among the  nations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:29">22:29</a> All the fat ones of the earth shall eat and worship; all  they that go down to the dust shall bow before him, and he that  cannot keep alive his own soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:30">22:30</a> A seed shall serve him; it shall be accounted to the Lord  for a generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:31">22:31</a> They shall come, and shall declare his righteousness unto  a people that shall be born, that he hath done [it].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:1">23:1</a> {A Psalm of David.} Jehovah is my shepherd; I shall not  want.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:2">23:2</a> He maketh me to lie down in green pastures; he leadeth me  beside still waters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:3">23:3</a> He restoreth my soul; he leadeth me in paths of  righteousness for his name's sake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:4">23:4</a> Yea, though I walk through the valley of the shadow of  death, I will fear no evil: for thou art with me; thy rod and  thy staff, they comfort me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:5">23:5</a> Thou preparest a table before me in the presence of mine  enemies; thou hast anointed my head with oil; my cup runneth  over.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:6">23:6</a> Surely, goodness and loving-kindness shall follow me all  the days of my life; and I will dwell in the house of Jehovah  for the length of the days.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:1">24:1</a> {Of David. A Psalm.} The earth is Jehovah's, and the  fulness thereof; the world, and they that dwell therein.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:2">24:2</a> For it was he that founded it upon seas, and established it  upon floods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:3">24:3</a> Who shall ascend into the mount of Jehovah? and who shall  stand in his holy place?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:4">24:4</a> He that hath blameless hands and a pure heart; who lifteth  not up his soul unto vanity, nor sweareth deceitfully:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:5">24:5</a> He shall receive blessing from Jehovah, and righteousness  from the God of his salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:6">24:6</a> This is the generation of them that seek unto him, that  seek thy face, O Jacob. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:7">24:7</a> Lift up your heads, ye gates, and be ye lifted up, ye  everlasting doors, and the King of glory shall come in.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:8">24:8</a> Who is this King of glory? Jehovah strong and mighty,  Jehovah mighty in battle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:9">24:9</a> Lift up your heads, ye gates; yea, lift up, ye everlasting  doors, and the King of glory shall come in.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:10">24:10</a> Who is he, this King of glory? Jehovah of hosts, he is the  King of glory. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:1">25:1</a> {[A Psalm] of David.} Unto thee, Jehovah, do I lift up my  soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:2">25:2</a> My God, I confide in thee; let me not be ashamed, let not  mine enemies triumph over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:3">25:3</a> Yea, none that wait on thee shall be ashamed: they shall be  ashamed that deal treacherously without cause.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:4">25:4</a> Make me to know thy ways, O Jehovah; teach me thy paths.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:5">25:5</a> Make me to walk in thy truth, and teach me: for thou art  the God of my salvation; on thee do I wait all the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:6">25:6</a> Remember, Jehovah, thy tender mercies and thy  loving-kindnesses; for they are from everlasting.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:7">25:7</a> Remember not the sins of my youth, nor my transgressions;  according to thy loving-kindness remember thou me, for thy  goodness' sake, Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:8">25:8</a> Good and upright is Jehovah; therefore will he instruct  sinners in the way:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:9">25:9</a> The meek will he guide in judgment, and the meek will he  teach his way.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:10">25:10</a> All the paths of Jehovah are loving-kindness and truth for  such as keep his covenant and his testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:11">25:11</a> For thy name's sake, O Jehovah, thou wilt indeed pardon  mine iniquity; for it is great.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:12">25:12</a> What man is he that feareth Jehovah? him will he instruct  in the way [that] he should choose.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:13">25:13</a> His soul shall dwell in prosperity, and his seed shall  inherit the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:14">25:14</a> The secret of Jehovah is with them that fear him, that he  may make known his covenant to them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:15">25:15</a> Mine eyes are ever toward Jehovah; for he will bring my  feet out of the net.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:16">25:16</a> Turn toward me, and be gracious unto me; for I am solitary  and afflicted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:17">25:17</a> The troubles of my heart are increased: bring me out of my  distresses;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:18">25:18</a> Consider mine affliction and my travail, and forgive all  my sins.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:19">25:19</a> Consider mine enemies, for they are many, and they hate me  [with] cruel hatred.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:20">25:20</a> Keep my soul, and deliver me: let me not be ashamed; for I  trust in thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:21">25:21</a> Let integrity and uprightness preserve me; for I wait on  thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:22">25:22</a> Redeem Israel, O God, out of all his troubles.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:1">26:1</a> {[A Psalm] of David.} Judge me, O Jehovah, for I have  walked in mine integrity, and I have confided in Jehovah: I  shall not slip.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:2">26:2</a> Prove me, Jehovah, and test me; try my reins and my heart:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:3">26:3</a> For thy loving-kindness is before mine eyes, and I have  walked in thy truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:4">26:4</a> I have not sat with vain persons, neither have I gone in  with dissemblers;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:5">26:5</a> I have hated the congregation of evil-doers, and I have not  sat with the wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:6">26:6</a> I will wash my hands in innocency, and will encompass thine  altar, O Jehovah,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:7">26:7</a> That I may cause the voice of thanksgiving to be heard, and  declare all thy marvellous works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:8">26:8</a> Jehovah, I have loved the habitation of thy house, and the  place where thy glory dwelleth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:9">26:9</a> Gather not my soul with sinners, nor my life with men of  blood;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:10">26:10</a> In whose hands are evil devices, and their right hand is  full of bribes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:11">26:11</a> But as for me, I will walk in mine integrity. Redeem me,  and be gracious unto me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:12">26:12</a> My foot standeth in an even place; in the congregations  will I bless Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:1">27:1</a> {[A Psalm] of David.} Jehovah is my light and my salvation;  whom shall I fear? Jehovah is the strength of my life; of whom  shall I be afraid?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:2">27:2</a> When evil-doers, mine adversaries and mine enemies, came  upon me to eat up my flesh, they stumbled and fell.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:3">27:3</a> If a host encamp against me, my heart shall not fear; if  war rise against me, in this will I be confident.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:4">27:4</a> One [thing] have I asked of Jehovah, that will I seek  after: that I may dwell in the house of Jehovah all the days of  my life, to behold the beauty of Jehovah, and to inquire [of  him] in his temple.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:5">27:5</a> For in the day of evil he will hide me in his pavilion; in  the secret of his tent will he keep me concealed: he will set  me high upon a rock.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:6">27:6</a> And now shall my head be lifted up above mine enemies round  about me; and I will offer in his tent sacrifices of shouts of  joy: I will sing, yea, I will sing psalms unto Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:7">27:7</a> Hear, Jehovah; with my voice do I call; be gracious unto  me, and answer me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:8">27:8</a> My heart said for thee, Seek ye my face. Thy face, O  Jehovah, will I seek.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:9">27:9</a> Hide not thy face from me; put not thy servant away in  anger: thou hast been my help; cast me not off, neither forsake  me, O God of my salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:10">27:10</a> For had my father and my mother forsaken me, then had  Jehovah taken me up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:11">27:11</a> Teach me thy way, Jehovah, and lead me in an even path,  because of mine enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:12">27:12</a> Deliver me not over to the will of mine adversaries; for  false witnesses are risen up against me, and such as breathe  out violence.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:13">27:13</a> Unless I had believed to see the goodness of Jehovah in  the land of the living ...!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:14">27:14</a> Wait for Jehovah; be strong and let thy heart take  courage: yea, wait for Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:1">28:1</a> {[A Psalm] of David.} Unto thee, Jehovah, do I call; my  rock, be not silent unto me, lest, [if] thou keep silence  toward me, I become like them that go down into the pit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:2">28:2</a> Hear the voice of my supplications, when I cry unto thee,  when I lift up my hands toward the oracle of thy holiness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:3">28:3</a> Draw me not away with the wicked, and with the workers of  iniquity, who speak peace to their neighbours, and mischief is  in their heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:4">28:4</a> Give them according to their doing, and according to the  wickedness of their deeds; give them after the work of their  hands, render to them their desert.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:5">28:5</a> For they regard not the deeds of Jehovah, nor the work of  his hands: he will destroy them, and not build them up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:6">28:6</a> Blessed be Jehovah, for he hath heard the voice of my  supplications.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:7">28:7</a> Jehovah is my strength and my shield; my heart confided in  him, and I was helped: therefore my heart exulteth, and with my  song will I praise him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:8">28:8</a> Jehovah is their strength; and he is the stronghold of  salvation to his anointed one.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:9">28:9</a> Save thy people, and bless thine inheritance; and feed  them, and lift them up for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:1">29:1</a> {A Psalm of David.} Give unto Jehovah, ye sons of the  mighty ones, give unto Jehovah glory and strength;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:2">29:2</a> Give unto Jehovah the glory of his name; worship Jehovah in  holy splendour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:3">29:3</a> The voice of Jehovah is upon the waters: the ùGod of glory  thundereth, -- Jehovah upon great waters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:4">29:4</a> The voice of Jehovah is powerful; the voice of Jehovah is  full of majesty.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:5">29:5</a> The voice of Jehovah breaketh cedars; yea, Jehovah breaketh  the cedars of Lebanon:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:6">29:6</a> And he maketh them to skip like a calf, Lebanon and Sirion  like a young buffalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:7">29:7</a> The voice of Jehovah cleaveth out flames of fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:8">29:8</a> The voice of Jehovah shaketh the wilderness; Jehovah  shaketh the wilderness of Kadesh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:9">29:9</a> The voice of Jehovah maketh the hinds to calve, and layeth  bare the forests; and in his temple doth every one say, Glory!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:10">29:10</a> Jehovah sitteth upon the flood; yea, Jehovah sitteth as  king for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:11">29:11</a> Jehovah will give strength unto his people; Jehovah will  bless his people with peace.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:1">30:1</a> {A Psalm of David: dedication-song of the house.} I will  extol thee, Jehovah; for thou hast delivered me, and hast not  made mine enemies to rejoice over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:2">30:2</a> Jehovah my God, I cried unto thee, and thou hast healed me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:3">30:3</a> Jehovah, thou hast brought up my soul from Sheol, thou hast  quickened me from among those that go down to the pit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:4">30:4</a> Sing psalms unto Jehovah, ye saints of his, and give thanks  in remembrance of his holiness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:5">30:5</a> For a moment [is passed] in his anger, a life in his  favour; at even weeping cometh for the night, and at morn there  is rejoicing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:6">30:6</a> As for me, I said in my prosperity, I shall never be moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:7">30:7</a> Jehovah, by thy favour thou hadst made my mountain to stand  strong: thou didst hide thy face; I was troubled.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:8">30:8</a> I called to thee, Jehovah, and unto the Lord did I make  supplication:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:9">30:9</a> What profit is there in my blood, in my going down to the  pit? shall the dust praise thee? shall it declare thy truth?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:10">30:10</a> Hear, O Jehovah, and be gracious unto me; Jehovah, be my  helper.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:11">30:11</a> Thou hast turned for me my mourning into dancing; thou  hast loosed my sackcloth, and girded me with gladness;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:12">30:12</a> That [my] glory may sing psalms of thee, and not be  silent. Jehovah my God, I will praise thee for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:1">31:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David.} In thee,  Jehovah, do I trust; let me never be ashamed: deliver me in thy  righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:2">31:2</a> Incline thine ear to me, deliver me speedily; be a strong  rock to me, a house of defence to save me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:3">31:3</a> For thou art my rock and my fortress; and, for thy name's  sake, thou wilt lead me and guide me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:4">31:4</a> Draw me out of the net that they have hidden for me; for  thou art my strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:5">31:5</a> Into thy hand I commit my spirit: thou hast redeemed me,  Jehovah, [thou] ùGod of truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:6">31:6</a> I have hated them that observe lying vanities; and as for  me, I have confided in Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:7">31:7</a> I will be glad and rejoice in thy loving-kindness, for thou  hast seen mine affliction; thou hast known the troubles of my  soul,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:8">31:8</a> And hast not shut me up into the hand of the enemy: thou  hast set my feet in a large place.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:9">31:9</a> Be gracious unto me, Jehovah, for I am in trouble: mine eye  wasteth away with vexation, my soul and my belly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:10">31:10</a> For my life is spent with sorrow, and my years with  sighing; my strength faileth through mine iniquity, and my  bones are wasted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:11">31:11</a> More than to all mine oppressors, I am become exceedingly  a reproach, even to my neighbours, and a fear to mine  acquaintance: they that see me without flee from me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:12">31:12</a> I am forgotten in [their] heart as a dead man; I am become  like a broken vessel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:13">31:13</a> For I have heard the slander of many -- terror on every  side -- when they take counsel together against me: they plot  to take away my life.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:14">31:14</a> But I confided in thee, Jehovah; I said, thou art my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:15">31:15</a> My times are in thy hand: deliver me from the hand of mine  enemies, and from my persecutors.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:16">31:16</a> Make thy face to shine upon thy servant; save me in thy  loving-kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:17">31:17</a> Jehovah, let me not be ashamed; for I have called upon  thee: let the wicked be ashamed, let them be silent in Sheol.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:18">31:18</a> Let the lying lips become dumb, which speak insolently  against the righteous in pride and contempt.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:19">31:19</a> [Oh] how great is thy goodness, which thou hast laid up  for them that fear thee, [which] thou hast wrought for them  that trust in thee, before the sons of men!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:20">31:20</a> Thou keepest them concealed in the secret of thy presence  from the conspiracies of man; thou hidest them in a pavilion  from the strife of tongues.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:21">31:21</a> Blessed be Jehovah; for he hath shewn me wondrously his  loving-kindness in a strong city.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:22">31:22</a> As for me, I said in my haste, I am cut off from before  thine eyes; nevertheless thou heardest the voice of my  supplications when I cried unto thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:23">31:23</a> Love Jehovah, all ye his saints. Jehovah preserveth the  faithful, and plentifully requiteth the proud doer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:24">31:24</a> Be strong, and let your heart take courage, all ye that  hope in Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:1">32:1</a> {Of David. Instruction.} Blessed is he [whose]  transgression is forgiven, [whose] sin is covered!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:2">32:2</a> Blessed is the man unto whom Jehovah reckoneth not  iniquity, and in whose spirit there is no guile!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:3">32:3</a> When I kept silence, my bones waxed old, through my  groaning all the day long.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:4">32:4</a> For day and night thy hand was heavy upon me; my moisture  was turned into the drought of summer. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:5">32:5</a> I acknowledged my sin unto thee, and mine iniquity I  covered not; I said, I will confess my transgressions unto  Jehovah, and *thou* forgavest the iniquity of my sin. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:6">32:6</a> For this shall every one that is godly pray unto thee at a  time when thou mayest be found: surely in the floods of great  waters they will not reach him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:7">32:7</a> Thou art a hiding-place for me; thou preservest me from  trouble; thou dost encompass me with songs of deliverance.  Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:8">32:8</a> I will instruct thee and teach thee the way in which thou  shalt go; I will counsel [thee] with mine eye upon thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:9">32:9</a> Be ye not as a horse, as a mule, which have no  understanding: whose trappings must be bit and bridle, for  restraint, or they will not come unto thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:10">32:10</a> Many sorrows hath the wicked; but he that confideth in  Jehovah, loving-kindness shall encompass him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:11">32:11</a> Rejoice in Jehovah, and be glad, ye righteous; and shout  for joy, all ye upright in heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:1">33:1</a> Exult, ye righteous, in Jehovah: praise is comely for the  upright.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:2">33:2</a> Give thanks unto Jehovah with the harp; sing psalms unto  him with the ten-stringed lute.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:3">33:3</a> Sing unto him a new song; play skilfully with a loud sound.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:4">33:4</a> For the word of Jehovah is right, and all his work is in  faithfulness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:5">33:5</a> He loveth righteousness and judgment: the earth is full of  the loving-kindness of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:6">33:6</a> By the word of Jehovah were the heavens made, and all the  host of them by the breath of his mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:7">33:7</a> He gathereth the waters of the sea together as a heap; he  layeth up the deeps in storehouses.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:8">33:8</a> Let all the earth fear Jehovah; let all the inhabitants of  the world stand in awe of him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:9">33:9</a> For *he* spoke, and it was [done]; *he* commanded, and it  stood fast.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:10">33:10</a> Jehovah frustrateth the counsel of the nations; he maketh  the thoughts of the peoples of none effect.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:11">33:11</a> The counsel of Jehovah standeth for ever, the thoughts of  his heart from generation to generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:12">33:12</a> Blessed is the nation whose God is Jehovah, the people  that he hath chosen for his inheritance!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:13">33:13</a> Jehovah looketh from the heavens; he beholdeth all the  sons of men:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:14">33:14</a> From the place of his habitation he looketh forth upon all  the inhabitants of the earth;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:15">33:15</a> He who fashioneth the hearts of them all, who considereth  all their works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:16">33:16</a> The king is not saved by the multitude of [his] forces; a  mighty man is not delivered by much strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:17">33:17</a> The horse is a vain thing for safety; neither doth he  deliver by his great power.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:18">33:18</a> Behold, the eye of Jehovah is upon them that fear him,  upon them that hope in his loving-kindness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:19">33:19</a> To deliver their soul from death, and to keep them alive  in famine.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:20">33:20</a> Our soul waiteth for Jehovah: he is our help and our  shield.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:21">33:21</a> For in him shall our heart rejoice, because we have  confided in his holy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:22">33:22</a> Let thy loving-kindness, O Jehovah, be upon us, according  as we have hoped in thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:1">34:1</a> {[A Psalm] of David; when he changed his behaviour before  Abimelech, who drove him away, and he departed.} I will bless  Jehovah at all times; his praise shall continually be in my  mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:2">34:2</a> My soul shall make its boast in Jehovah: the meek shall  hear, and rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:3">34:3</a> Magnify Jehovah with me, and let us exalt his name  together.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:4">34:4</a> I sought Jehovah, and he answered me, and delivered me from  all my fears.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:5">34:5</a> They looked unto him, and were enlightened, and their faces  were not confounded.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:6">34:6</a> This afflicted one called, and Jehovah heard [him], and  saved him out of all his troubles.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:7">34:7</a> The angel of Jehovah encampeth round about them that fear  him, and delivereth them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:8">34:8</a> Taste and see that Jehovah is good: blessed is the man that  trusteth in him!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:9">34:9</a> Fear Jehovah, ye his saints; for there is no want to them  that fear him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:10">34:10</a> The young lions are in need and suffer hunger; but they  that seek Jehovah shall not want any good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:11">34:11</a> Come, ye sons, hearken unto me: I will teach you the fear  of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:12">34:12</a> What man is he that desireth life, [and] loveth days, that  he may see good?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:13">34:13</a> Keep thy tongue from evil, and thy lips from speaking  guile;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:14">34:14</a> Depart from evil, and do good; seek peace, and pursue it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:15">34:15</a> The eyes of Jehovah are upon the righteous, and his ears  are toward their cry;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:16">34:16</a> The face of Jehovah is against them that do evil, to cut  off the remembrance of them from the earth:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:17">34:17</a> [The righteous] cry, and Jehovah heareth, and delivereth  them out of all their troubles.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:18">34:18</a> Jehovah is nigh to those that are of a broken heart, and  saveth them that are of a contrite spirit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:19">34:19</a> Many are the adversities of the righteous, but Jehovah  delivereth him out of them all:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:20">34:20</a> He keepeth all his bones; not one of them is broken.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:21">34:21</a> Evil shall destroy the wicked; and they that hate the  righteous shall bear their guilt.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:22">34:22</a> Jehovah redeemeth the soul of his servants; and none of  them that trust in him shall bear guilt.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:1">35:1</a> {[A Psalm] of David.} Strive, O Jehovah, with them that  strive with me; fight against them that fight against me:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:2">35:2</a> Take hold of shield and buckler, and stand up for my help;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:3">35:3</a> And draw out the spear, and stop [the way] against my  pursuers: say unto my soul, I am thy salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:4">35:4</a> Let them be put to shame and confounded that seek after my  life; let them be turned backward and brought to confusion that  devise my hurt:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:5">35:5</a> Let them be as chaff before the wind, and let the angel of  Jehovah drive [them] away;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:6">35:6</a> Let their way be dark and slippery, and let the angel of  Jehovah pursue them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:7">35:7</a> For without cause have they hidden for me their net [in] a  pit; without cause they have digged [it] for my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:8">35:8</a> Let destruction come upon him unawares, and let his net  which he hath hidden catch himself: for destruction let him  fall therein.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:9">35:9</a> And my soul shall be joyful in Jehovah; it shall rejoice in  his salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:10">35:10</a> All my bones shall say, Jehovah, who is like unto thee,  who deliverest the afflicted from one stronger than he, yea,  the afflicted and the needy from him that spoileth him!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:11">35:11</a> Unrighteous witnesses rise up; they lay to my charge  things which I know not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:12">35:12</a> They reward me evil for good, [to] the bereavement of my  soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:13">35:13</a> But as for me, when they were sick, my clothing was  sackcloth; I chastened my soul with fasting, and my prayer  returned into mine own bosom:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:14">35:14</a> I behaved myself as though [he had been] a friend, a  brother to me; I bowed down in sadness, as one that mourneth  [for] a mother.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:15">35:15</a> But at my halting they rejoiced, and gathered together:  the slanderers gathered themselves together against me, and I  knew [it] not; they did tear [me], and ceased not:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:16">35:16</a> With profane jesters for bread, they have gnashed their  teeth against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:17">35:17</a> Lord, how long wilt thou look on? Rescue my soul from  their destructions, my only one from the young lions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:18">35:18</a> I will give thee thanks in the great congregation; I will  praise thee among much people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:19">35:19</a> Let not them that are wrongfully mine enemies rejoice over  me; let them not wink with the eye that hate me without cause.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:20">35:20</a> For they speak not peace; and they devise deceitful words  against the quiet in the land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:21">35:21</a> And they opened their mouth wide against me; they said,  Aha! aha! our eye hath seen [it].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:22">35:22</a> Thou hast seen [it], Jehovah: keep not silence; O Lord, be  not far from me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:23">35:23</a> Stir up thyself, and awake for my right, for my cause, my  God and Lord!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:24">35:24</a> Judge me, Jehovah my God, according to thy righteousness,  and let them not rejoice over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:25">35:25</a> Let them not say in their heart, Aha! so would we have it.  Let them not say, We have swallowed him up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:26">35:26</a> Let them be ashamed and brought to confusion together that  rejoice at mine adversity; let them be clothed with shame and  dishonour that magnify themselves against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:27">35:27</a> Let them exult and rejoice that delight in my  righteousness; and let them say continually, Jehovah be  magnified, who delighteth in the prosperity of his servant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:28">35:28</a> And my tongue shall talk of thy righteousness, [and] of  thy praise, all the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:1">36:1</a> {To the chief Musician. [A Psalm] of the servant of  Jehovah; of David.} The transgression of the wicked uttereth  within my heart, There is no fear of God before his eyes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:2">36:2</a> For he flattereth himself in his own eyes, [even] when his  iniquity is found to be hateful.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:3">36:3</a> The words of his mouth are wickedness and deceit: he hath  left off to be wise, to do good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:4">36:4</a> He deviseth wickedness up on his bed; he setteth himself in  a way that is not good: he abhorreth not evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:5">36:5</a> Jehovah, thy loving-kindness is in the heavens, and thy  faithfulness [reacheth] unto the clouds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:6">36:6</a> Thy righteousness is like the high mountains; thy judgments  are a great deep: thou, Jehovah, preservest man and beast.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:7">36:7</a> How precious is thy loving-kindness, O God! So the sons of  men take refuge under the shadow of thy wings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:8">36:8</a> They shall be abundantly satisfied with the fatness of thy  house; and thou wilt make them drink of the river of thy  pleasures.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:9">36:9</a> For with thee is the fountain of life: in thy light shall  we see light.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:10">36:10</a> Continue thy loving-kindness unto them that know thee, and  thy righteousness to the upright in heart;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:11">36:11</a> Let not the foot of pride come against me, and let not the  hand of the wicked drive me away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:12">36:12</a> There are the workers of iniquity fallen: they are cast  down, and are not able to rise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:1">37:1</a> {[A Psalm] of David.} Fret not thyself because of  evil-doers, and be not envious of them that work  unrighteousness;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:2">37:2</a> for they shall soon be cut down like the grass, and fade as  the green herb.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:3">37:3</a> Confide in Jehovah, and do good; dwell in the land, and  feed on faithfulness;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:4">37:4</a> and delight thyself in Jehovah, and he will give thee the  desires of thy heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:5">37:5</a> Commit thy way unto Jehovah, and rely upon him: he will  bring [it] to pass;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:6">37:6</a> and he will bring forth thy righteousness as the light, and  thy judgment as the noonday.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:7">37:7</a> Rest in Jehovah, and wait patiently for him: fret not  thyself because of him that prospereth in his way, because of  the man that bringeth mischievous devices to pass.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:8">37:8</a> Cease from anger, and forsake wrath; fret not thyself: it  [would be] only to do evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:9">37:9</a> For evil-doers shall be cut off; but those that wait on  Jehovah, they shall possess the land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:10">37:10</a> For yet a little while, and the wicked is not; and thou  considerest his place, but he is not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:11">37:11</a> But the meek shall possess the land, and shall delight  themselves in the abundance of prosperity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:12">37:12</a> The wicked plotteth against the righteous, and gnasheth  his teeth against him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:13">37:13</a> The Lord laugheth at him; for he seeth that his day is  coming.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:14">37:14</a> The wicked have drawn out the sword, and have bent their  bow, to cast down the afflicted and needy, to slay those that  are upright in [the] way:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:15">37:15</a> their sword shall enter into their own heart, and their  bows shall be broken.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:16">37:16</a> The little that the righteous hath is better than the  abundance of many wicked;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:17">37:17</a> for the arms of the wicked shall be broken, but Jehovah  upholdeth the righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:18">37:18</a> Jehovah knoweth the days of the perfect; and their  inheritance shall be for ever:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:19">37:19</a> they shall not be ashamed in the time of evil, and in the  days of famine they shall be satisfied.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:20">37:20</a> For the wicked shall perish, and the enemies of Jehovah  shall be as the fat of lambs: they shall consume, like smoke  shall they consume away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:21">37:21</a> The wicked borroweth, and payeth not again; but the  righteous is gracious and giveth:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:22">37:22</a> for those blessed of him shall possess the land, and they  that are cursed of him shall be cut off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:23">37:23</a> The steps of a man are established by Jehovah, and he  delighteth in his way:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:24">37:24</a> though he fall, he shall not be utterly cast down, for  Jehovah upholdeth his hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:25">37:25</a> I have been young, and now am old, and I have not seen the  righteous forsaken, nor his seed seeking bread:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:26">37:26</a> all the day he is gracious and lendeth, and his seed shall  be a blessing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:27">37:27</a> Depart from evil, and do good, and dwell for evermore;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:28">37:28</a> for Jehovah loveth judgment, and will not forsake his  saints: They are preserved for ever; but the seed of the wicked  shall be cut off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:29">37:29</a> The righteous shall possess the land, and dwell therein  for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:30">37:30</a> The mouth of the righteous proffereth wisdom, and his  tongue speaketh judgment;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:31">37:31</a> the law of his God is in his heart; his goings shall not  slide.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:32">37:32</a> The wicked watcheth the righteous, and seeketh to slay  him:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:33">37:33</a> Jehovah will not leave him in his hand, nor condemn him  when he is judged.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:34">37:34</a> Wait for Jehovah, and keep his way, and he will exalt thee  to possess the land: when the wicked are cut off, thou shalt  see [it].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:35">37:35</a> I have seen the wicked in great power, and spreading like  a green tree in its native soil:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:36">37:36</a> but he passed away, and behold, he was not; and I sought  him, but he was not found.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:37">37:37</a> Mark the perfect, and behold the upright, for the end of  [that] man is peace;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:38">37:38</a> but the transgressors shall be destroyed together; the  future of the wicked shall be cut off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:39">37:39</a> But the salvation of the righteous is of Jehovah: he is  their strength in the time of trouble.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:40">37:40</a> And Jehovah will help them and deliver them: he will  deliver them from the wicked, and save them; for they trust in  him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:1">38:1</a> {A Psalm of David, to bring to remembrance.} Jehovah,  rebuke me not in thy wrath; neither chasten me in thy hot  displeasure.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:2">38:2</a> For thine arrows stick fast in me, and thy hand cometh down  upon me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:3">38:3</a> There is no soundness in my flesh because of thine  indignation; no peace in my bones, because of my sin.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:4">38:4</a> For mine iniquities are gone over my head: as a heavy  burden they are too heavy for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:5">38:5</a> My wounds stink, they are corrupt, because of my  foolishness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:6">38:6</a> I am depressed; I am bowed down beyond measure; I go  mourning all the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:7">38:7</a> For my loins are full of burning, and there is no soundness  in my flesh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:8">38:8</a> I am faint and broken beyond measure; I roar by reason of  the agitation of my heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:9">38:9</a> Lord, all my desire is before thee, and my sighing is not  hid from thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:10">38:10</a> My heart throbbeth, my strength hath left me; and the  light of mine eyes, it also is no more with me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:11">38:11</a> My lovers and mine associates stand aloof from my stroke;  and my kinsmen stand afar off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:12">38:12</a> And they that seek after my life lay snares [for me]; and  they that seek my hurt speak mischievous things, and meditate  deceits all the day long.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:13">38:13</a> But I, as a deaf [man], hear not; and am as a dumb man  that openeth not his mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:14">38:14</a> Yea, I am as a man that heareth not, and in whose mouth  are no reproofs.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:15">38:15</a> For in thee, Jehovah, do I hope: *thou* wilt answer, O  Lord my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:16">38:16</a> For I said, Let them not rejoice over me! When my foot  slipped, they magnified [themselves] against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:17">38:17</a> For I am ready to halt, and my pain is continually before  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:18">38:18</a> For I will declare mine iniquity, I am grieved for my sin.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:19">38:19</a> But mine enemies are lively, they are strong; and they  that hate me wrongfully are multiplied:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:20">38:20</a> And they that render evil for good are adversaries unto  me; because I pursue what is good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:21">38:21</a> Forsake me not, Jehovah; O my God, be not far from me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:22">38:22</a> Make haste to help me, O Lord, my salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:1">39:1</a> {To the chief Musician, to Jeduthun. A Psalm of David.} I  said, I will take heed to my ways, that I sin not with my  tongue: I will keep my mouth with a muzzle, while the wicked is  before me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:2">39:2</a> I was dumb with silence, I held my peace from good; and my  sorrow was stirred.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:3">39:3</a> My heart burned within me; the fire was kindled in my  musing: I spoke with my tongue,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:4">39:4</a> Make me to know, Jehovah, mine end, and the measure of my  days, what it is: I shall know how frail I am.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:5">39:5</a> Behold, thou hast made my days [as] hand-breadths, and my  lifetime is as nothing before thee; verily, every man, [even]  the high placed, is altogether vanity. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:6">39:6</a> Verily, man walketh in a vain show; verily they are  disquieted in vain; he heapeth up [riches], and knoweth not who  shall gather them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:7">39:7</a> And now, what wait I for, Lord? my hope is in thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:8">39:8</a> Deliver me from all my transgressions; make me not the  reproach of the foolish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:9">39:9</a> I was dumb, I opened not my mouth; for *thou* hast done  [it].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:10">39:10</a> Remove thy stroke away from me: I am consumed by the blow  of thy hand.</p>
