 <p><a name="an_39:11">39:11</a> When thou with rebukes dost correct a man for iniquity,  thou makest his beauty to consume away like a moth: surely,  every man is vanity. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:12">39:12</a> Hear my prayer, Jehovah, and give ear unto my cry; be not  silent at my tears: for I am a stranger with thee, a sojourner,  like all my fathers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:13">39:13</a> Look away from me, and let me recover strength, before I  go hence and be no more.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:1">40:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Of David. A Psalm.} I waited  patiently for Jehovah; and he inclined unto me, and heard my  cry.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:2">40:2</a> And he brought me up out of the pit of destruction, out of  the miry clay, and set my feet upon a rock; he hath established  my goings:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:3">40:3</a> And he hath put a new song in my mouth, praise unto our  God. Many shall see it, and fear, and shall confide in Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:4">40:4</a> Blessed is the man that hath made Jehovah his confidence,  and turneth not to the proud, and to such as turn aside to  lies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:5">40:5</a> Thou, O Jehovah my God, hast multiplied thy marvellous  works, and thy thoughts toward us: they cannot be reckoned up  in order unto thee; would I declare and speak [them], they are  more than can be numbered.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:6">40:6</a> Sacrifice and oblation thou didst not desire: ears hast  thou prepared me. Burnt-offering and sin-offering hast thou not  demanded;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:7">40:7</a> Then said I, Behold, I come, in the volume of the book it  is written of me --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:8">40:8</a> To do thy good pleasure, my God, is my delight, and thy law  is within my heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:9">40:9</a> I have published righteousness in the great congregation:  behold, I have not withheld my lips, Jehovah, *thou* knowest.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:10">40:10</a> I have not hidden thy righteousness within my heart; I  have declared thy faithfulness and thy salvation: I have not  concealed thy loving-kindness and thy truth from the great  congregation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:11">40:11</a> Withhold not thou, Jehovah, thy tender mercies from me;  let thy loving-kindness and thy truth continually preserve me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:12">40:12</a> For innumerable evils have compassed me about: mine  iniquities have taken hold upon me, so that I cannot see; they  are more than the hairs of my head: and my heart hath failed  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:13">40:13</a> Be pleased, O Jehovah, to deliver me; Jehovah, make haste  to my help.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:14">40:14</a> Let them be ashamed and brought to confusion together that  seek after my soul to destroy it; let them be turned backward  and confounded that take pleasure in mine adversity;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:15">40:15</a> Let them be desolate, because of their shame, that say  unto me, Aha! Aha!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:16">40:16</a> Let all those that seek thee be glad and rejoice in thee;  let such as love thy salvation say continually, Jehovah be  magnified!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:17">40:17</a> But I am afflicted and needy: the Lord thinketh upon me.  Thou art my help and my deliverer: my God, make no delay.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:1">41:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David.} Blessed is he  that understandeth the poor: Jehovah will deliver him in the  day of evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:2">41:2</a> Jehovah will preserve him, and keep him alive; he shall be  made happy in the land; and thou wilt not deliver him to the  will of his enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:3">41:3</a> Jehovah will sustain him upon the bed of languishing: thou  turnest all his bed in his sickness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:4">41:4</a> As for me, I said, Jehovah, be gracious unto me: heal my  soul; for I have sinned against thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:5">41:5</a> Mine enemies wish me evil: When will he die, and his name  perish?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:6">41:6</a> And if one come to see [me], he speaketh falsehood; his  heart gathereth wickedness to itself: he goeth abroad, he  telleth [it].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:7">41:7</a> All that hate me whisper together against me; against me do  they devise my hurt.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:8">41:8</a> A thing of Belial cleaveth fast unto him; and now that he  is laid down, he will rise up no more.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:9">41:9</a> Yea, mine own familiar friend, in whom I confided, who did  eat of my bread, hath lifted up [his] heel against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:10">41:10</a> But thou, Jehovah, be gracious unto me, and raise me up,  that I may requite them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:11">41:11</a> By this I know that thou delightest in me, because mine  enemy doth not triumph over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:12">41:12</a> But as for me, thou upholdest me in mine integrity, and  settest me before thy face for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:13">41:13</a> Blessed be Jehovah, the God of Israel, from eternity to  eternity! Amen, and Amen.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:1">42:1</a> {To the chief Musician. An instruction; of the sons of  Korah.} As the hart panteth after the water-brooks, so panteth  my soul after thee, O God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:2">42:2</a> My soul thirsteth for God, for the living ùGod: when shall  I come and appear before God?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:3">42:3</a> My tears have been my bread day and night, while they say  unto me all the day, Where is thy God?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:4">42:4</a> These things I remember and have poured out my soul within  me: how I passed along with the multitude, how I went on with  them to the house of God, with the voice of joy and praise, a  festive multitude.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:5">42:5</a> Why art thou cast down, my soul, and art disquieted in me?  hope in God; for I shall yet praise him, [for] the health of  his countenance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:6">42:6</a> My God, my soul is cast down within me; therefore do I  remember thee from the land of the Jordan, and the Hermons,  from mount Mizar.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:7">42:7</a> Deep calleth unto deep at the noise of thy cataracts; all  thy breakers and thy billows are gone over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:8">42:8</a> In the day-time will Jehovah command his loving-kindness,  and in the night his song shall be with me, a prayer unto the  ùGod of my life.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:9">42:9</a> I will say unto ùGod my rock, Why hast thou forgotten me?  why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:10">42:10</a> As with a crushing in my bones mine adversaries reproach  me, while they say unto me all the day, Where is thy God?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:11">42:11</a> Why art thou cast down, my soul? and why art thou  disquieted within me? hope in God; for I shall yet praise him,  [who is] the health of my countenance, and my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:1">43:1</a> Judge me, O God, and plead my cause against an ungodly  nation; deliver me from the deceitful and unrighteous man.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:2">43:2</a> For thou art the God of my strength: why hast thou cast me  off? why go I about mourning because of the oppression of the  enemy?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:3">43:3</a> Send out thy light and thy truth: *they* shall lead me,  *they* shall bring me to thy holy mount, and unto thy  habitations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:4">43:4</a> Then will I go unto the altar of God, unto the ùGod of the  gladness of my joy: yea, upon the harp will I praise thee, O  God, my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:5">43:5</a> Why art thou cast down, my soul? and why art thou  disquieted within me? hope in God; for I shall yet praise him,  [who is] the health of my countenance, and my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:1">44:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Of the sons of Korah. An  instruction.} O God, with our ears have we heard, our fathers  have told us, the work thou wroughtest in their days, in the  days of old:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:2">44:2</a> Thou, by thy hand, didst dispossess the nations, but them  thou didst plant; thou didst afflict the peoples, but them  didst thou cause to spread out.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:3">44:3</a> For not by their own sword did they take possession of the  land, neither did their own arm save them; but thy right hand,  and thine arm, and the light of thy countenance, because thou  hadst delight in them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:4">44:4</a> Thou thyself art my king, O God: command deliverance for  Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:5">44:5</a> Through thee will we push down our adversaries; through thy  name will we tread them under that rise up against us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:6">44:6</a> For I will not put confidence in my bow, neither shall my  sword save me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:7">44:7</a> For thou hast saved us from our adversaries, and hast put  them to shame that hate us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:8">44:8</a> In God will we boast all the day, and we will praise thy  name for ever. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:9">44:9</a> But thou hast cast off, and put us to confusion, and dost  not go forth with our armies;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:10">44:10</a> Thou hast made us to turn back from the adversary, and  they that hate us spoil for themselves;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:11">44:11</a> Thou hast given us over like sheep [appointed] for meat,  and hast scattered us among the nations;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:12">44:12</a> Thou hast sold thy people for nought, and hast not  increased [thy wealth] by their price;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:13">44:13</a> Thou makest us a reproach to our neighbours, a mockery and  a derision for them that are round about us;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:14">44:14</a> Thou makest us a byword among the nations, a shaking of  the head among the peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:15">44:15</a> All the day my confusion is before me, and the shame of my  face hath covered me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:16">44:16</a> Because of the voice of him that reproacheth and  blasphemeth; by reason of the enemy and the avenger.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:17">44:17</a> All this is come upon us; yet have we not forgotten thee,  neither have we dealt falsely against thy covenant:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:18">44:18</a> Our heart is not turned back, neither have our steps  declined from thy path;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:19">44:19</a> Though thou hast crushed us in the place of jackals, and  covered us with the shadow of death.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:20">44:20</a> If we had forgotten the name of our God, and stretched out  our hands to a strange ùgod,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:21">44:21</a> Would not God search this out? for he knoweth the secrets  of the heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:22">44:22</a> But for thy sake are we killed all the day long; we are  reckoned as sheep for slaughter.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:23">44:23</a> Awake, why sleepest thou, Lord? arise, cast [us] not off  for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:24">44:24</a> Wherefore hidest thou thy face, [and] forgettest our  affliction and our oppression?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:25">44:25</a> For our soul is bowed down to the dust; our belly cleaveth  unto the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:26">44:26</a> Rise up for our help, and redeem us for thy  loving-kindness' sake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:1">45:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Upon Shoshannim. Of the sons of  Korah. An instruction; -- a song of the Beloved.} My heart is  welling forth [with] a good matter: I say what I have composed  touching the king. My tongue is the pen of a ready writer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:2">45:2</a> Thou art fairer than the sons of men; grace is poured into  thy lips: therefore God hath blessed thee for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:3">45:3</a> Gird thy sword upon [thy] thigh, O mighty one, [in] thy  majesty and thy splendour;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:4">45:4</a> And [in] thy splendour ride prosperously, because of truth  and meekness [and] righteousness: and thy right hand shall  teach thee terrible things.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:5">45:5</a> Thine arrows are sharp -- peoples fall under thee -- in the  heart of the king's enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:6">45:6</a> Thy throne, O God, is for ever and ever; a sceptre of  uprightness is the sceptre of thy kingdom:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:7">45:7</a> Thou hast loved righteousness, and hated wickedness;  therefore God, thy God, hath anointed thee with the oil of  gladness above thy companions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:8">45:8</a> Myrrh and aloes, cassia, are all thy garments; out of ivory  palaces stringed instruments have made thee glad.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:9">45:9</a> Kings' daughters are among thine honourable women; upon thy  right hand doth stand the queen in gold of Ophir.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:10">45:10</a> Hearken, daughter, and see, and incline thine ear; and  forget thine own people and thy father's house:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:11">45:11</a> And the king will desire thy beauty; for he is thy Lord,  and worship thou him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:12">45:12</a> And the daughter of Tyre with a gift, the rich ones among  the people, shall court thy favour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:13">45:13</a> All glorious is the king's daughter within; her clothing  is of wrought gold:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:14">45:14</a> She shall be brought unto the king in raiment of  embroidery; the virgins behind her, her companions, shall be  brought in unto thee:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:15">45:15</a> With joy and gladness shall they be brought; they shall  enter into the king's palace.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:16">45:16</a> Instead of thy fathers shall be thy sons; princes shalt  thou make them in all the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:17">45:17</a> I will make thy name to be remembered throughout all  generations; therefore shall the peoples praise thee for ever  and ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:1">46:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Of the sons of Korah. On Alamoth. A  song.} God is our refuge and strength, a help in distresses,  very readily found.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:2">46:2</a> Therefore will we not fear though the earth be removed, and  though the mountains be carried into the heart of the seas;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:3">46:3</a> Though the waters thereof roar [and] foam, though the  mountains shake with the swelling thereof. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:4">46:4</a> There is a river the streams whereof make glad the city of  God, the sanctuary of the habitations of the Most High.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:5">46:5</a> God is in the midst of her; she shall not be moved: God  shall help her at the dawn of the morning.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:6">46:6</a> The nations raged, the kingdoms were moved; he uttered his  voice, the earth melted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:7">46:7</a> Jehovah of hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our high  fortress. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:8">46:8</a> Come, behold the works of Jehovah, what desolations he hath  made in the earth:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:9">46:9</a> He hath made wars to cease unto the end of the earth; he  breaketh the bow, and cutteth the spear in sunder; he burneth  the chariots in the fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:10">46:10</a> Be still, and know that I am God: I will be exalted among  the nations, I will be exalted in the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:11">46:11</a> Jehovah of hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our high  fortress. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:1">47:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Of the sons of Korah. A Psalm.} All  ye peoples, clap your hands; shout unto God with the voice of  triumph!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:2">47:2</a> For Jehovah, the Most High, is terrible, a great king over  all the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:3">47:3</a> He subdueth the peoples under us, and the nations under our  feet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:4">47:4</a> He hath chosen our inheritance for us, the excellency of  Jacob whom he loved. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:5">47:5</a> God is gone up amid shouting, Jehovah amid the sound of the  trumpet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:6">47:6</a> Sing psalms of God, sing psalms; sing psalms unto our King,  sing psalms!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:7">47:7</a> For God is the King of all the earth; sing psalms with  understanding.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:8">47:8</a> God reigneth over the nations; God sitteth upon the throne  of his holiness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:9">47:9</a> The willing-hearted of the peoples have gathered together,  [with] the people of the God of Abraham. For unto God [belong]  the shields of the earth: he is greatly exalted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:1">48:1</a> {A Song; a Psalm. Of the sons of Korah.} Great is Jehovah,  and greatly to be praised in the city of our God, in the hill  of his holiness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:2">48:2</a> Beautiful in elevation, the joy of the whole earth, is  mount Zion, [on] the sides of the north, the city of the great  King.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:3">48:3</a> God is known in her palaces as a high fortress.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:4">48:4</a> For behold, the kings assembled themselves, they passed by  together;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:5">48:5</a> They saw, -- so they marvelled; they were troubled, they  fled in consternation:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:6">48:6</a> Trembling took hold upon them there; anguish, as of a woman  in travail.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:7">48:7</a> With an east wind thou hast broken the ships of Tarshish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:8">48:8</a> As we have heard, so have we seen, in the city of Jehovah  of hosts, in the city of our God: God doth establish it for  ever. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:9">48:9</a> We have thought, O God, of thy loving-kindness, in the  midst of thy temple.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:10">48:10</a> According to thy name, O God, so is thy praise unto the  ends of the earth: thy right hand is full of righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:11">48:11</a> Let mount Zion rejoice, let the daughters of Judah be  glad, because of thy judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:12">48:12</a> Walk about Zion, and go round about her: count the towers  thereof;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:13">48:13</a> Mark ye well her bulwarks, consider her palaces: that ye  may tell it to the generation following.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:14">48:14</a> For this God is our God for ever and ever; he will be our  guide until death.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:1">49:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Of the sons of Korah. A Psalm.}  Hear this, all ye peoples; give ear, all inhabitants of the  world:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:2">49:2</a> Both men of low and men of high degree, rich and poor  alike.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:3">49:3</a> My mouth shall speak wisdom, and the meditation of my heart  shall be of understanding:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:4">49:4</a> I will incline mine ear to a parable, I will open my riddle  upon the harp.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:5">49:5</a> Wherefore should I fear in the days of adversity, [when]  the iniquity of my supplanters encompasseth me? --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:6">49:6</a> They depend upon their wealth, and boast themselves in the  abundance of their riches. ...</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:7">49:7</a> None can by any means redeem his brother, nor give to God a  ransom for him,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:8">49:8</a> (For the redemption of their soul is costly, and must be  given up for ever,)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:9">49:9</a> That he should still live perpetually, [and] not see  corruption.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:10">49:10</a> For he seeth that wise men die; all alike, the fool and  the brutish perish, and they leave their wealth to others.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:11">49:11</a> Their inward thought is, that their houses are for ever,  their dwelling-places from generation to generation: they call  the lands after their own names.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:12">49:12</a> Nevertheless, man being in honour abideth not: he is like  the beasts that perish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:13">49:13</a> This their way is their folly, yet they that come after  them delight in their sayings. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:14">49:14</a> Like sheep are they laid in Sheol: Death feedeth on them;  and the upright shall have dominion over them in the morning;  and their comeliness shall be for Sheol to consume, that there  be no habitation for them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:15">49:15</a> But God will redeem my soul from the power of Sheol: for  he will receive me. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:16">49:16</a> Be not afraid when a man becometh rich, when the glory of  his house is increased:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:17">49:17</a> For when he dieth, he shall carry nothing away; his glory  shall not descend after him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:18">49:18</a> Though he blessed his soul in his lifetime, -- and men  will praise thee when thou doest well to thyself, --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:19">49:19</a> It shall go to the generation of his fathers: they shall  never see light.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:20">49:20</a> Man that is in honour, and understandeth not, is like the  beasts that perish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:1">50:1</a> {A Psalm. Of Asaph.} ùGod, Elohim-Jehovah, hath spoken, and  called the earth from the rising of the sun unto the going down  thereof.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:2">50:2</a> Out of Zion, the perfection of beauty, God hath shined  forth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:3">50:3</a> Our God will come, and will not keep silence: fire shall  devour before him, and it shall be very tempestuous round about  him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:4">50:4</a> He will call to the heavens from above, and to the earth,  that he may judge his people:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:5">50:5</a> Gather unto me my godly ones, those that have made a  covenant with me by sacrifice!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:6">50:6</a> And the heavens shall declare his righteousness; for God  executeth judgment himself. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:7">50:7</a> Hear, my people, and I will speak; O Israel, and I will  testify unto thee: I am God, thy God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:8">50:8</a> I will not reprove thee for thy sacrifices, or thy  burnt-offerings, continually before me;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:9">50:9</a> I will take no bullock out of thy house, [nor] he-goats out  of thy folds:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:10">50:10</a> For every beast of the forest is mine, the cattle upon a  thousand hills;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:11">50:11</a> I know all the fowl of the mountains, and the roaming  creatures of the field are mine:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:12">50:12</a> If I were hungry, I would not tell thee; for the world is  mine, and the fulness thereof.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:13">50:13</a> Should I eat the flesh of bulls, and drink the blood of  goats?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:14">50:14</a> Offer unto God thanksgiving, and perform thy vows unto the  Most High;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:15">50:15</a> And call upon me in the day of trouble; I will deliver  thee, and thou shalt glorify me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:16">50:16</a> But unto the wicked God saith, What hast thou to do to  declare my statutes, or that thou shouldest take my covenant  into thy mouth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:17">50:17</a> Seeing thou hast hated correction and hast cast my words  behind thee?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:18">50:18</a> When thou sawest a thief, thou didst take pleasure in him,  and thy portion was with adulterers;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:19">50:19</a> Thou lettest thy mouth loose to evil, and thy tongue  frameth deceit;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:20">50:20</a> Thou sittest [and] speakest against thy brother, thou  revilest thine own mother's son:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:21">50:21</a> These [things] hast thou done, and I kept silence; thou  thoughtest that I was altogether as thyself: [but] I will  reprove thee, and set [them] in order before thine eyes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:22">50:22</a> Now consider this, ye that forget +God, lest I tear in  pieces, and there be no deliverer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:23">50:23</a> Whoso offereth praise glorifieth me; and to him that  ordereth [his] way will I shew the salvation of God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:1">51:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David; when Nathan the  prophet came to him, after he had gone in to Bath-sheba.} Be  gracious unto me, O God, according to thy loving-kindness;  according to the abundance of thy tender mercies, blot out my  transgressions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:2">51:2</a> Wash me fully from mine iniquity, and cleanse me from my  sin.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:3">51:3</a> For I acknowledge my transgressions, and my sin is  continually before me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:4">51:4</a> Against thee, thee only, have I sinned, and done what is  evil in thy sight; that thou mayest be justified when thou  speakest, be clear when thou judgest.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:5">51:5</a> Behold, in iniquity was I brought forth, and in sin did my  mother conceive me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:6">51:6</a> Behold, thou wilt have truth in the inward parts; and in  the hidden [part] thou wilt make me to know wisdom.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:7">51:7</a> Purge me with hyssop, and I shall be clean; wash me, and I  shall be whiter than snow.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:8">51:8</a> Make me to hear gladness and joy; [that] the bones which  thou hast broken may rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:9">51:9</a> Hide thy face from my sins, and blot out all mine  iniquities.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:10">51:10</a> Create in me a clean heart, O God, and renew a steadfast  spirit within me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:11">51:11</a> Cast me not away from thy presence, and take not the  spirit of thy holiness from me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:12">51:12</a> Restore unto me the joy of thy salvation, and let a  willing spirit sustain me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:13">51:13</a> I will teach transgressors thy ways, and sinners shall  return unto thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:14">51:14</a> Deliver me from blood-guiltiness, O God, thou God of my  salvation: my tongue shall sing aloud of thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:15">51:15</a> Lord, open my lips, and my mouth shall declare thy praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:16">51:16</a> For thou desirest not sacrifice; else would I give it:  thou hast no pleasure in burnt-offering.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:17">51:17</a> The sacrifices of God are a broken spirit: a broken and a  contrite heart, O God, thou wilt not despise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:18">51:18</a> Do good in thy good pleasure unto Zion; build the walls of  Jerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:19">51:19</a> Then shalt thou have sacrifices of righteousness,  burnt-offering, and whole burnt-offering; then shall they offer  up bullocks upon thine altar.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:1">52:1</a> {To the chief Musician: an instruction. Of David; when Doeg  the Edomite came and told Saul, and said unto him, David came  to the house of Ahimelech.} Why boastest thou thyself in evil,  thou mighty man? The loving-kindness of ùGod [abideth]  continually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:2">52:2</a> Thy tongue deviseth mischievous things, like a sharp razor,  practising deceit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:3">52:3</a> Thou hast loved evil rather than good, lying rather than to  speak righteousness. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:4">52:4</a> Thou hast loved all devouring words, O deceitful tongue!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:5">52:5</a> ùGod shall likewise destroy thee for ever; he shall take  thee away, and pluck thee out of [thy] tent, and root thee out  of the land of the living. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:6">52:6</a> The righteous also shall see, and fear, and shall laugh at  him, [saying,]</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:7">52:7</a> Behold the man that made not God his strength, but put  confidence in the abundance of his riches, [and] strengthened  himself in his avarice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:8">52:8</a> But as for me, I am like a green olive-tree in the house of  God: I will confide in the loving-kindness of God for ever and  ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:9">52:9</a> I will praise thee for ever, because thou hast done [it];  and I will wait on thy name, before thy godly ones, for it is  good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:1">53:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On Mahalath: an instruction. Of  David.} The fool hath said in his heart, There is no God! They  have corrupted themselves, and have done abominable iniquity:  there is none that doeth good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:2">53:2</a> God looked down from the heavens upon the children of men,  to see if there were any that did understand, that did seek  God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:3">53:3</a> Every one of them is gone back, they are together become  corrupt: there is none that doeth good, not even one.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:4">53:4</a> Have the workers of iniquity no knowledge, eating up my  people [as] they eat bread? they call not upon God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:5">53:5</a> There were they in great fear, where no fear was; for God  scattereth the bones of him that encampeth against thee. Thou  hast put [them] to shame, for God hath despised them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:6">53:6</a> Oh that the salvation of Israel were come out of Zion! When  God turneth again the captivity of his people, Jacob shall be  glad, Israel shall rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:1">54:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On stringed instruments: an  instruction. Of David; when the Ziphites came, and said to  Saul, Is not David hiding himself with us?} O God, by thy name  save me, and by thy strength do me justice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:2">54:2</a> O God, hear my prayer; give ear to the words of my mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:3">54:3</a> For strangers are risen up against me, and the violent seek  after my life: they have not set God before them. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:4">54:4</a> Behold, God is my helper; the Lord is among them that  uphold my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:5">54:5</a> He will requite evil to mine enemies: in thy truth cut them  off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:6">54:6</a> I will freely sacrifice unto thee; I will praise thy name,  O Jehovah, because it is good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:7">54:7</a> For he hath delivered me out of all trouble; and mine eye  hath seen [its desire] upon mine enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:1">55:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On stringed instruments: an  instruction. Of David.} Give ear to my prayer, O God; and hide  not thyself from my supplication.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:2">55:2</a> Attend unto me, and answer me: I wander about in my plaint,  and I moan aloud,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:3">55:3</a> Because of the voice of the enemy; because of the  oppression of the wicked: for they cast iniquity upon me, and  in anger they persecute me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:4">55:4</a> My heart is writhing within me, and the terrors of death  are fallen upon me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:5">55:5</a> Fear and trembling are come upon me, and horror hath  overwhelmed me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:6">55:6</a> And I said, Oh that I had wings like a dove! I would fly  away, and be at rest;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:7">55:7</a> Behold, I would flee afar off, I would lodge in the  wilderness; Selah;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:8">55:8</a> I would hasten my escape from the stormy wind, from the  tempest.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:9">55:9</a> Swallow [them] up, Lord; divide their tongue: for I have  seen violence and strife in the city.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:10">55:10</a> Day and night they go about it upon the walls thereof; and  iniquity and mischief are in the midst of it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:11">55:11</a> Perversities are in the midst thereof; and oppression and  deceit depart not from its streets.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:12">55:12</a> For it is not an enemy that hath reproached me -- then  could I have borne it; neither is it he that hateth me that  hath magnified [himself] against me -- then would I have hidden  myself from him;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:13">55:13</a> But it was thou, a man mine equal, mine intimate, my  familiar friend. ...</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:14">55:14</a> We who held sweet intercourse together. To the house of  God we walked amid the throng.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:15">55:15</a> Let death seize upon them, let them go down alive into  Sheol. For wickedness is in their dwellings, in their midst.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:16">55:16</a> As for me, unto God will I call; and Jehovah will save me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:17">55:17</a> Evening, and morning, and at noon, will I pray and moan  aloud; and he will hear my voice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:18">55:18</a> He hath redeemed my soul in peace from the battle against  me: for there were many about me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:19">55:19</a> ùGod will hear, and afflict them: he that is seated of  old, (Selah) ... because there is no change in them, and they  fear not God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:20">55:20</a> He hath put forth his hands against such as are at peace  with him; he hath profaned his covenant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:21">55:21</a> Smooth were the milky [words] of his mouth, but his heart  was war; his words were softer than oil, yet are they drawn  swords.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:22">55:22</a> Cast thy burden upon Jehovah, and *he* will sustain thee:  he will never suffer the righteous to be moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:23">55:23</a> And thou, O God, wilt bring them down into the pit of  destruction: bloody and deceitful men shall not live out half  their days. But as for me, I will confide in thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:1">56:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On Jonathelem-rechokim. Of David.  Michtam; when the Philistines took him in Gath.} Be gracious  unto me, O God; for man would swallow me up: all the day long  fighting he oppresseth me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:2">56:2</a> Mine enemies would swallow [me] up all the day long; for  they are many that fight against me haughtily.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:3">56:3</a> In the day that I am afraid, I will confide in thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:4">56:4</a> In God will I praise his word, in God I put my confidence:  I will not fear; what can flesh do unto me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:5">56:5</a> All the day long they wrest my words; all their thoughts  are against me for evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:6">56:6</a> They gather themselves together, they hide themselves; they  mark my steps, because they wait for my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:7">56:7</a> Shall they escape by iniquity? In anger cast down the  peoples, O God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:8">56:8</a> *Thou* countest my wanderings; put my tears into thy  bottle: are they not in thy book?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:9">56:9</a> Then shall mine enemies return backward in the day when I  call: this I know, for God is for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:10">56:10</a> In God will I praise [his] word; in Jehovah will I praise  [his] word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:11">56:11</a> In God have I put my confidence: I will not fear; what can  man do unto me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:12">56:12</a> Thy vows are upon me, O God: I will render thanks unto  thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:13">56:13</a> For thou hast delivered my soul from death; [wilt thou]  not [keep] my feet from falling, that I may walk before God in  the light of the living?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:1">57:1</a> {To the chief Musician. 'Destroy not.' Of David. Michtam;  when he fled from Saul in the cave.} Be gracious unto me, O  God, be gracious unto me; for my soul taketh refuge in thee:  yea, in the shadow of thy wings do I take refuge, until the  calamities be overpast.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:2">57:2</a> I will call unto God, the Most High; unto ùGod that  performeth [all] for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:3">57:3</a> He will send from the heavens and save me; he hath covered  with reproach him that would swallow me up. Selah. God hath  sent forth his loving-kindness and his truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:4">57:4</a> My soul is in the midst of lions; I lie down [among] them  that breathe out flames, the sons of men, whose teeth are  spears and arrows, and their tongue a sharp sword.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:5">57:5</a> Be exalted above the heavens, O God; let thy glory be above  all the earth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:6">57:6</a> They have prepared a net for my steps; my soul was bowed  down: they have digged a pit before me; they are fallen into  the midst thereof. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:7">57:7</a> My heart is fixed, O God, my heart is fixed: I will sing,  yea, I will sing psalms.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:8">57:8</a> Awake, my glory; awake, lute and harp: I will wake the  dawn.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:9">57:9</a> I will give thee thanks among the peoples, O Lord; of thee  will I sing psalms among the nations:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:10">57:10</a> For thy loving-kindness is great unto the heavens, and thy  truth unto the clouds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:11">57:11</a> Be exalted above the heavens, O God; let thy glory be  above all the earth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:1">58:1</a> {To the chief Musician. 'Destroy not.' Of David. Michtam.}  Is righteousness indeed silent? Do ye speak it? Do ye judge  with equity, ye sons of men?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:2">58:2</a> Yea, in heart ye work wickedness; ye weigh out the violence  of your hands in the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:3">58:3</a> The wicked go astray from the womb; they err as soon as  they are born, speaking lies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:4">58:4</a> Their poison is like the poison of a serpent: [they are]  like the deaf adder which stoppeth her ear;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:5">58:5</a> Which doth not hearken to the voice of enchanters, of one  charming ever so wisely.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:6">58:6</a> O God, break their teeth in their mouth; break out the  great teeth of the young lions, O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:7">58:7</a> Let them melt away as waters that flow off; when he aimeth  his arrows, let them be as blunted:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:8">58:8</a> Let them be as a snail that melteth as it passeth away;  [like] the untimely birth of a woman, let them not see the sun.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:9">58:9</a> Before your pots feel the thorns, green or burning, -- they  shall be whirled away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:10">58:10</a> The righteous shall rejoice when he seeth the vengeance;  he shall wash his footsteps in the blood of the wicked:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:11">58:11</a> And men shall say, Verily there is fruit for the  righteous; verily there is a God that judgeth in the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:1">59:1</a> {To the chief Musician. 'Destroy not.' Of David. Michtam;  when Saul sent, and they watched the house to kill him.}  Deliver me from mine enemies, O my God; secure me on high from  them that rise up against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:2">59:2</a> Deliver me from the workers of iniquity, and save me from  men of blood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:3">59:3</a> For behold, they lie in wait for my soul; strong ones are  gathered against me: not for my transgression, nor for my sin,  O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:4">59:4</a> They run and prepare themselves without [my] fault: awake  to meet me, and behold.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:5">59:5</a> Yea, do thou, Jehovah, the God of hosts, the God of Israel,  arise to visit all the nations: be not gracious to any plotters  of iniquity. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:6">59:6</a> They return in the evening; they howl like a dog, and go  round about the city:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:7">59:7</a> Behold, they belch out with their mouth; swords are in  their lips: for who [say they] doth hear?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:8">59:8</a> But thou, Jehovah, wilt laugh at them; thou wilt have all  the nations in derision.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:9">59:9</a> Their strength! ... I will take heed to thee; for God is my  high fortress.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:10">59:10</a> God, whose loving-kindness will come to meet me, -- God  shall let me see [my desire] upon mine enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:11">59:11</a> Slay them not, lest my people forget; by thy power make  them wander, and bring them down, O Lord, our shield.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:12">59:12</a> [Because of] the sin of their mouth, the word of their  lips, let them even be taken in their pride; and because of  cursing and lying which they speak.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:13">59:13</a> Make an end in wrath, make an end, that they may be no  more; that they may know that God ruleth in Jacob, unto the  ends of the earth. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:14">59:14</a> And in the evening they shall return, they shall howl like  a dog, and go round about the city.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:15">59:15</a> They shall wander about for meat, and stay all night if  they be not satisfied.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:16">59:16</a> But as for me, I will sing of thy strength; yea, I will  sing aloud of thy loving-kindness in the morning; for thou hast  been to me a high fortress, and a refuge in the day of my  trouble.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:17">59:17</a> Unto thee, my strength, will I sing psalms; for God is my  high fortress, the God of my mercy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:1">60:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On Shushan. Testimony. Michtam of  David; to teach: when he strove with the Syrians of  Mesopotamia, and the Syrians of Zobah, and Joab returned, and  smote the Edomites in the valley of salt, twelve thousand.} O  God, thou hast cast us off, thou hast scattered us, thou hast  been displeased: restore us again.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:2">60:2</a> Thou hast made the earth to tremble, thou hast rent it:  heal the breaches thereof; for it shaketh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:3">60:3</a> Thou hast shewn thy people hard things; thou hast made us  to drink the wine of bewilderment.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:4">60:4</a> Thou hast given a banner to them that fear thee, that it  may be displayed because of the truth, (Selah,)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:5">60:5</a> That thy beloved ones may be delivered. Save with thy right  hand, and answer me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:6">60:6</a> God hath spoken in his holiness: I will exult, I will  divide Shechem, and mete out the valley of Succoth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:7">60:7</a> Gilead is mine, and Manasseh is mine, and Ephraim is the  strength of my head; Judah is my law-giver;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:8">60:8</a> Moab is my wash-pot; upon Edom will I cast my sandal;  Philistia, shout aloud because of me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:9">60:9</a> Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me  unto Edom?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:10">60:10</a> [Wilt] not thou, O God, who didst cast us off? and didst  not go forth, O God, with our armies?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:11">60:11</a> Give us help from trouble; for vain is man's deliverance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:12">60:12</a> Through God we shall do valiantly; and he it is that will  tread down our adversaries.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:1">61:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On a stringed instrument. [A Psalm]  of David.} Hear, O God, my cry; attend unto my prayer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:2">61:2</a> From the end of the earth will I call unto thee, when my  heart is overwhelmed: thou wilt lead me on to a rock which is  too high for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:3">61:3</a> For thou hast been a refuge for me, a strong tower from  before the enemy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:4">61:4</a> I will sojourn in thy tent for ever; I will take refuge in  the covert of thy wings. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:5">61:5</a> For thou, O God, hast heard my vows; thou hast given [me]  the inheritance of those that fear thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:6">61:6</a> Thou wilt add days to the days of the king: his years shall  be as many generations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:7">61:7</a> He shall abide before God for ever: bestow loving-kindness  and truth, that they may preserve him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:8">61:8</a> So will I sing forth thy name for ever, performing my vows  from day to day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:1">62:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On Jeduthun. A Psalm of David.}  Upon God alone doth my soul rest peacefully; from him is my  salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:2">62:2</a> He only is my rock and my salvation; my high fortress: I  shall not be greatly moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:3">62:3</a> How long will ye assail a man; will ye [seek], all of you,  to break him down as a bowing wall or a tottering fence?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:4">62:4</a> They only consult to thrust [him] down from his excellency;  they delight in lies; they bless with their mouth, but in their  inward part they curse. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:5">62:5</a> Upon God alone, O my soul, rest peacefully; for my  expectation is from him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:6">62:6</a> He only is my rock and my salvation; my high fortress: I  shall not be moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:7">62:7</a> With God is my salvation and my glory; the rock of my  strength, my refuge is in God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:8">62:8</a> Confide in him at all times, ye people; pour out your heart  before him: God is our refuge. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:9">62:9</a> Men of low degree are only vanity; men of high degree, a  lie: laid in the balance, they go up together [lighter] than  vanity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:10">62:10</a> Put not confidence in oppression, and become not vain in  robbery; if wealth increase, set not your heart upon it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:11">62:11</a> Once hath God spoken, twice have I heard this, that  strength [belongeth] unto God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:12">62:12</a> And unto thee, O Lord, [belongeth] loving-kindness; for  *thou* renderest to every man according to his work.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:1">63:1</a> {A Psalm of David; when he was in the wilderness of Judah.}  O God, thou art my ùGod; early will I seek thee. My soul  thirsteth for thee, my flesh languisheth for thee, in a dry and  weary land without water:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:2">63:2</a> To see thy power and thy glory, as I have beheld thee in  the sanctuary;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:3">63:3</a> For thy loving-kindness is better than life: my lips shall  praise thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:4">63:4</a> So will I bless thee while I live; I will lift up my hands  in thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:5">63:5</a> My soul is satisfied as with marrow and fatness, and my  mouth shall praise [thee] with joyful lips.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:6">63:6</a> When I remember thee upon my bed, I meditate on thee in the  night-watches:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:7">63:7</a> For thou hast been my help, and in the shadow of thy wings  will I sing for joy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:8">63:8</a> My soul followeth hard after thee: thy right hand upholdeth  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:9">63:9</a> But those that seek my soul, to destroy [it], shall go into  the lower parts of the earth;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:10">63:10</a> They shall be given over to the power of the sword; they  shall be the portion of foxes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:11">63:11</a> But the king shall rejoice in God; every one that sweareth  by him shall glory: for the mouth of them that speak lies shall  be stopped.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:1">64:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David.} Hear, O God, my  voice in my plaint; preserve my life from fear of the enemy:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:2">64:2</a> Hide me from the secret counsel of evil-doers, from the  tumultuous crowd of the workers of iniquity,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:3">64:3</a> Who have sharpened their tongue like a sword, [and] have  aimed their arrow, a bitter word;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:4">64:4</a> That they may shoot in secret at the perfect: suddenly do  they shoot at him, and fear not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:5">64:5</a> They encourage themselves in an evil matter, they concert  to hide snares; they say, Who will see them?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:6">64:6</a> They devise iniquities: We have it ready, the plan is  diligently sought out. And each one's inward [thought] and  heart is deep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:7">64:7</a> But God will shoot an arrow at them: suddenly are they  wounded;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:8">64:8</a> By their own tongue they are made to fall over one another:  all that see them shall flee away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:9">64:9</a> And all men shall fear, and shall declare God's doing; and  they shall wisely consider his work.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:10">64:10</a> The righteous shall rejoice in Jehovah, and trust in him;  and all the upright in heart shall glory.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:1">65:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David: a Song.} Praise  waiteth for thee in silence, O God, in Zion; and unto thee  shall the vow be performed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:2">65:2</a> O thou that hearest prayer, unto thee shall all flesh come.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:3">65:3</a> Iniquities have prevailed against me: our transgressions,  thou wilt forgive them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:4">65:4</a> Blessed is he whom thou choosest and causest to approach:  he shall dwell in thy courts. We shall be satisfied with the  goodness of thy house, of thy holy temple.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:5">65:5</a> By terrible things in righteousness wilt thou answer us, O  God of our salvation, thou confidence of all the ends of the  earth, and of the distant regions of the sea. ...</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:6">65:6</a> Who by his strength established the mountains, being girded  with power;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:7">65:7</a> Who stilleth the raging of the seas, the raging of their  waves, and the tumult of the peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:8">65:8</a> And they that dwell in the uttermost parts are afraid at  thy tokens; thou makest the outgoings of the morning and  evening to rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:9">65:9</a> Thou hast visited the earth, thou hast watered it; thou  greatly enrichest it: the river of God is full of water; thou  providest their corn, when thou hast so prepared it:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:10">65:10</a> Thou dost satiate its furrows, thou smoothest its clods,  thou makest it soft with showers; thou blessest the springing  thereof.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:11">65:11</a> Thou crownest the year with thy goodness, and thy paths  drop fatness:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:12">65:12</a> They drop upon the pastures of the wilderness, and the  hills are girded with gladness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:13">65:13</a> The meadows are clothed with flocks, and the valleys are  covered over with corn; they shout for joy, yea, they sing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:1">66:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Song: a Psalm.} Shout aloud unto  God, all the earth:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:2">66:2</a> Sing forth the glory of his name, make his praise glorious;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:3">66:3</a> Say unto God, How terrible are thy works! because of the  greatness of thy strength, thine enemies come cringing unto  thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:4">66:4</a> All the earth shall worship thee, and sing psalms unto  thee: they shall sing forth thy name. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:5">66:5</a> Come and see the works of God: he is terrible in [his]  doings toward the children of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:6">66:6</a> He turned the sea into dry [land]; they went through the  river on foot: there did we rejoice in him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:7">66:7</a> He ruleth by his power for ever; his eyes observe the  nations: let not the rebellious exalt themselves. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:8">66:8</a> Bless our God, ye peoples, and make the voice of his praise  to be heard;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:9">66:9</a> Who hath set our soul in life, and suffereth not our feet  to be moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:10">66:10</a> For thou, O God, hast proved us: thou hast tried us, as  silver is tried.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:11">66:11</a> Thou broughtest us into a net, thou didst lay a heavy  burden upon our loins;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:12">66:12</a> Thou didst cause men to ride over our head; we went  through fire and through water: but thou hast brought us out  into abundance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:13">66:13</a> I will go into thy house with burnt-offerings; I will  perform my vows to thee,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:14">66:14</a> Which my lips have uttered, and my mouth hath spoken, when  I was in trouble.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:15">66:15</a> I will offer up unto thee burnt-offerings of fatted  beasts, with the incense of rams; I will offer bullocks with  goats. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:16">66:16</a> Come, hear, all ye that fear God, and I will declare what  he hath done for my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:17">66:17</a> I called unto him with my mouth, and he was extolled with  my tongue.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:18">66:18</a> Had I regarded iniquity in my heart, the Lord would not  hear.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:19">66:19</a> But God hath heard; he hath attended to the voice of my  prayer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:20">66:20</a> Blessed be God, who hath not turned away my prayer, nor  his loving-kindness from me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:1">67:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A Psalm: a  Song.} God be gracious unto us, and bless us, [and] cause his  face to shine upon us; Selah,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:2">67:2</a> That thy way may be known upon earth, thy salvation among  all nations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:3">67:3</a> Let the peoples praise thee, O God, let all the peoples  praise thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:4">67:4</a> Let the nations rejoice and sing for joy: for thou wilt  judge the peoples equitably; and the nations upon earth, thou  wilt guide them. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:5">67:5</a> Let the peoples praise thee, O God; let all the peoples  praise thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:6">67:6</a> The earth will yield her increase; God, our God, will bless  us:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:7">67:7</a> God will bless us; and all the ends of the earth shall fear  him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:1">68:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Of David. A Psalm: a Song.} Let God  arise, let his enemies be scattered, and let them that hate him  flee before him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:2">68:2</a> As smoke is driven, thou wilt drive them away; as wax  melteth before the fire, the wicked shall perish at the  presence of God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:3">68:3</a> But the righteous shall rejoice: they shall exult before  God and be glad with joy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:4">68:4</a> Sing unto God, sing forth his name; cast up a way for him  that rideth in the deserts: his name is Jah; and rejoice before  him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:5">68:5</a> A father of the fatherless, and a judge of the widows, is  God in his holy habitation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:6">68:6</a> God maketh the solitary into families; those that were  bound he bringeth out into prosperity: but the rebellious dwell  in a parched [land].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:7">68:7</a> O God, when thou wentest forth before thy people, when thou  didst march through the wilderness -- (Selah) --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:8">68:8</a> The earth trembled, the heavens also dropped at the  presence of God, yon Sinai, at the presence of God, the God of  Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:9">68:9</a> Thou, O God, didst pour a plentiful rain upon thine  inheritance, and when it was weary thou strengthenedst it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:10">68:10</a> Thy flock hath dwelt therein: thou hast prepared in thy  goodness, for the afflicted, O God!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:11">68:11</a> The Lord gives the word: great the host of the publishers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:12">68:12</a> Kings of armies flee; they flee, and she that tarrieth at  home divideth the spoil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:13">68:13</a> Though ye have lain among the sheepfolds, [ye shall be as]  wings of a dove covered with silver, and her feathers with  green gold.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:14">68:14</a> When the Almighty scattered kings in it, it became  snow-white as Zalmon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:15">68:15</a> [As] mount Bashan is the mount of God, a many-peaked  mountain, [as] mount Bashan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:16">68:16</a> Why do ye look with envy, ye many-peaked mountains, upon  the mount that God hath desired for his abode? yea, Jehovah  will dwell [there] for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:17">68:17</a> The chariots of God are twenty thousand, thousands upon  thousands; the Lord is among them: it is a Sinai in holiness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:18">68:18</a> Thou hast ascended on high, thou hast led captivity  captive: thou hast received gifts in Man, and even [for] the  rebellious, for the dwelling [there] of Jah Elohim.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:19">68:19</a> Blessed be the Lord: day by day doth he load us [with  good], the ùGod who is our salvation. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:20">68:20</a> Our ùGod is the ùGod of salvation; and with Jehovah, the  Lord, are the goings forth [even] from death.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:21">68:21</a> Verily God will smite the head of his enemies, the hairy  scalp of him that goeth on still in his trespasses.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:22">68:22</a> The Lord said, I will bring again from Bashan, I will  bring [them] again from the depth of the sea;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:23">68:23</a> That thou mayest dip thy foot in blood: the tongue of thy  dogs has its portion from enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:24">68:24</a> They have seen thy goings, O God, the goings of my ùGod,  my King, in the sanctuary.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:25">68:25</a> The singers went before, the players on stringed  instruments after, in the midst of maidens playing on tabrets.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:26">68:26</a> In the congregations bless ye God, the Lord, -- [ye] from  the fountain of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:27">68:27</a> There is little Benjamin, their ruler; the princes of  Judah, their company; the princes of Zebulun, the princes of  Naphtali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:28">68:28</a> Thy God hath commanded thy strength: strengthen, O God,  that which thou hast wrought for us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:29">68:29</a> Because of thy temple at Jerusalem shall kings bring  presents unto thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:30">68:30</a> Rebuke the beast of the reeds, the assembly of the strong,  with the calves of the peoples: [every one] submitteth himself  with pieces of silver. Scatter the peoples that delight in war.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:31">68:31</a> Great ones shall come out of Egypt; Ethiopia shall quickly  stretch out her hands unto God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:32">68:32</a> Ye kingdoms of the earth, sing unto God; sing psalms of  the Lord, (Selah,)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:33">68:33</a> Of him that rideth upon the heavens, the heavens which are  of old: lo, he uttereth his voice, a mighty voice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:34">68:34</a> Ascribe ye strength unto God: his excellency is over  Israel, and his strength is in the clouds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:35">68:35</a> Terrible art thou, O God, out of thy sanctuaries, -- the  ùGod of Israel! He it is that giveth strength and might unto  the people. Blessed be God!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:1">69:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Upon Shoshannim. [A Psalm] of  David.} Save me, O God; for the waters are come in unto [my]  soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:2">69:2</a> I sink in deep mire, where there is no standing; I am come  into the depths of waters, and the flood overfloweth me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:3">69:3</a> I am weary with my crying, my throat is parched; mine eyes  fail while I wait for my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:4">69:4</a> They that hate me without a cause are more than the hairs  of my head; they that would destroy me, being mine enemies  wrongfully, are mighty: then I restored that which I took not  away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:5">69:5</a> Thou, O God, knowest my foolishness, and my trespasses are  not hidden from thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:6">69:6</a> Let not them that wait on thee, Lord, Jehovah of hosts, be  ashamed through me; let not those that seek thee be confounded  through me, O God of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:7">69:7</a> Because for thy sake I have borne reproach; confusion hath  covered my face.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:8">69:8</a> I am become a stranger unto my brethren, and an alien unto  my mother's sons;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:9">69:9</a> For the zeal of thy house hath devoured me, and the  reproaches of them that reproach thee have fallen upon me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:10">69:10</a> And I wept, my soul was fasting: that also was to my  reproach; --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:11">69:11</a> And I made sackcloth my garment: then I became a proverb  to them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:12">69:12</a> They that sit in the gate talk of me, and [I am] the song  of the drunkards.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:13">69:13</a> But as for me, my prayer is unto thee, Jehovah, in an  acceptable time: O God, in the abundance of thy loving-kindness  answer me, according to the truth of thy salvation:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:14">69:14</a> Deliver me out of the mire, let me not sink; let me be  delivered from them that hate me, and out of the depths of  waters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:15">69:15</a> Let not the flood of waters overflow me, neither let the  deep swallow me up; and let not the pit shut its mouth upon me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:16">69:16</a> Answer me, O Jehovah; for thy loving-kindness is good:  according to the abundance of thy tender mercies, turn toward  me;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:17">69:17</a> And hide not thy face from thy servant, for I am in  trouble: answer me speedily.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:18">69:18</a> Draw nigh unto my soul, be its redeemer; ransom me because  of mine enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:19">69:19</a> *Thou* knowest my reproach, and my shame, and my  dishonour: mine adversaries are all before thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:20">69:20</a> Reproach hath broken my heart, and I am overwhelmed: and I  looked for sympathy, but there was none; and for comforters,  but I found none.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:21">69:21</a> Yea, they gave me gall for my food, and in my thirst they  gave me vinegar to drink.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:22">69:22</a> Let their table become a snare before them, and their very  welfare a trap;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:23">69:23</a> Let their eyes be darkened, that they see not, and make  their loins continually to shake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:24">69:24</a> Pour out thine indignation upon them, and let the  fierceness of thine anger take hold of them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:25">69:25</a> Let their habitation be desolate; let there be no dweller  in their tents.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:26">69:26</a> For they persecute him whom *thou* hast smitten, and they  talk for the sorrow of those whom thou hast wounded.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:27">69:27</a> Add iniquity unto their iniquity, and let them not come  into thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:28">69:28</a> Let them be blotted out of the book of life, and not be  written with the righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:29">69:29</a> But I am afflicted and sorrowful: let thy salvation, O  God, set me secure on high.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:30">69:30</a> I will praise the name of God with a song, and will  magnify him with thanksgiving;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:31">69:31</a> And it shall please Jehovah more than an ox, -- a bullock  with horns and cloven hoofs.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:32">69:32</a> The meek shall see it, they shall be glad; ye that seek  God, your heart shall live.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:33">69:33</a> For Jehovah heareth the needy, and despiseth not his  prisoners.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:34">69:34</a> Let heavens and earth praise him; the seas, and everything  that moveth therein.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:35">69:35</a> For God will save Zion, and will build the cities of  Judah; and they shall dwell there, and possess it:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:36">69:36</a> And the seed of his servants shall inherit it, and they  that love his name shall dwell therein.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:1">70:1</a> {To the chief Musician. [A Psalm] of David: to bring to  remembrance.} Make haste, O God, to deliver me; Jehovah,  [hasten] to my help.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:2">70:2</a> Let them be ashamed and brought to confusion that seek  after my soul; let them be turned backward and confounded that  take pleasure in mine adversity;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:3">70:3</a> Let them turn back because of their shame that say, Aha!  Aha!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:4">70:4</a> Let all those that seek thee be glad and rejoice in thee,  and let such as love thy salvation say continually, Let God be  magnified!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:5">70:5</a> But I am afflicted and needy: make haste unto me, O God.  Thou art my help and my deliverer: O Jehovah, make no delay.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:1">71:1</a> In thee, Jehovah, do I trust: let me never be ashamed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:2">71:2</a> Deliver me in thy righteousness, and rescue me; incline  thine ear unto me, and save me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:3">71:3</a> Be to me a rock of habitation, whereunto I may continually  resort: thou hast given commandment to save me; for thou art my  rock and my fortress.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:4">71:4</a> My God, rescue me out of the hand of the wicked, out of the  hand of the unrighteous and cruel man.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:5">71:5</a> For thou art my hope, O Lord Jehovah, my confidence from my  youth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:6">71:6</a> On thee have I been stayed from the womb; from the bowels  of my mother thou didst draw me forth: my praise shall be  continually of thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:7">71:7</a> I have been as a wonder unto many; but thou art my strong  refuge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:8">71:8</a> My mouth shall be filled with thy praise, with thy glory,  all the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:9">71:9</a> Cast me not off in the time of old age; forsake me not when  my strength faileth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:10">71:10</a> For mine enemies speak against me, and they that watch for  my soul consult together,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:11">71:11</a> Saying, God hath forsaken him; pursue and seize him, for  there is none to deliver.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:12">71:12</a> O God, be not far from me; my God, hasten to my help.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:13">71:13</a> Let them be ashamed, let them be consumed, that are  adversaries to my soul; let them be covered with reproach and  dishonour that seek my hurt.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:14">71:14</a> But as for me, I will hope continually, and will praise  thee yet more and more.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:15">71:15</a> My mouth shall declare thy righteousness, [and] thy  salvation all the day: for I know not the numbers [thereof].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:16">71:16</a> I will go in the might of the Lord Jehovah; I will recall  thy righteousness, thine alone.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:17">71:17</a> O God, thou hast taught me from my youth, and hitherto  have I proclaimed thy marvellous works:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:18">71:18</a> Now also, when I am old and greyheaded, O God, forsake me  not, until I have proclaimed thine arm unto [this] generation,  thy might to every one that is to come.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:19">71:19</a> And thy righteousness, O God, reacheth on high, thou who  hast done great things: O God, who is like unto thee?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:20">71:20</a> Thou, who hast shewn us many and sore troubles, wilt  revive us again, and wilt bring us up again from the depths of  the earth;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:21">71:21</a> Thou wilt increase my greatness, and comfort me on every  side.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:22">71:22</a> I will also praise thee with the psaltery, even thy truth,  my God; unto thee will I sing psalms with the harp, thou holy  One of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:23">71:23</a> My lips shall exult when I sing psalms unto thee; and my  soul, which thou hast redeemed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:24">71:24</a> My tongue also shall talk of thy righteousness all the  day; for they shall be ashamed, for they shall be brought to  confusion, that seek my hurt.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:1">72:1</a> {For Solomon.} O God, give the king thy judgments, and thy  righteousness unto the king's son.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:2">72:2</a> He will judge thy people with righteousness, and thine  afflicted with judgment.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:3">72:3</a> The mountains shall bring peace to the people, and the  hills, by righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:4">72:4</a> He will do justice to the afflicted of the people; he will  save the children of the needy, and will break in pieces the  oppressor.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:5">72:5</a> They shall fear thee as long as sun and moon endure, from  generation to generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:6">72:6</a> He shall come down like rain on the mown grass, as showers  that water the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:7">72:7</a> In his days shall the righteous flourish, and abundance of  peace till the moon be no more.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:8">72:8</a> And he shall have dominion from sea to sea, and from the  river unto the ends of the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:9">72:9</a> The dwellers in the desert shall bow before him, and his  enemies shall lick the dust.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:10">72:10</a> The kings of Tarshish and of the isles shall render  presents; the kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer tribute:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:11">72:11</a> Yea, all kings shall bow down before him; all nations  shall serve him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:12">72:12</a> For he will deliver the needy who crieth, and the  afflicted, who hath no helper;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:13">72:13</a> He will have compassion on the poor and needy, and will  save the souls of the needy:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:14">72:14</a> He will redeem their souls from oppression and violence,  and precious shall their blood be in his sight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:15">72:15</a> And he shall live; and to him shall be given of the gold  of Sheba; and prayer shall be made for him continually: all the  day shall he be blessed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:16">72:16</a> There shall be abundance of corn in the earth, upon the  top of the mountains; the fruit thereof shall shake like  Lebanon; and they of the city shall bloom like the herb of the  earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:17">72:17</a> His name shall endure for ever; his name shall be  continued as long as the sun: and [men] shall bless themselves  in him; all nations shall call him blessed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:18">72:18</a> Blessed be Jehovah Elohim, the God of Israel, who alone  doeth wondrous things!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:19">72:19</a> And blessed be his glorious name for ever! and let the  whole earth be filled with his glory! Amen, and Amen.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:20">72:20</a> The prayers of David the son of Jesse are ended.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:1">73:1</a> {A Psalm of Asaph.} Truly God is good to Israel, to such as  are of a pure heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:2">73:2</a> But as for me, my feet were almost gone, my steps had well  nigh slipped;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:3">73:3</a> For I was envious at the arrogant, seeing the prosperity of  the wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:4">73:4</a> For they have no pangs in their death, and their body is  well nourished;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:5">73:5</a> They have not the hardships of mankind, neither are they  plagued like [other] men:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:6">73:6</a> Therefore pride encompasseth them as a neck-chain, violence  covereth them [as] a garment;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:7">73:7</a> Their eyes stand out from fatness, they exceed the  imaginations of their heart:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:8">73:8</a> They mock and speak wickedly of oppression, they speak  loftily:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:9">73:9</a> They set their mouth in the heavens, and their tongue  walketh through the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:10">73:10</a> Therefore his people turn hither, and waters in fulness  are wrung out to them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:11">73:11</a> And they say, How can ùGod know, and is there knowledge in  the Most High?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:12">73:12</a> Behold, these are the wicked, and they prosper in the  world: they heap up riches.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:13">73:13</a> Truly have I purified my heart in vain, and washed my  hands in innocency:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:14">73:14</a> For all the day have I been plagued, and chastened every  morning.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:15">73:15</a> If I said, I will speak thus, behold, I should be  faithless to the generation of thy children.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:16">73:16</a> When I thought to be able to know this, it was a grievous  task in mine eyes;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:17">73:17</a> Until I went into the sanctuaries of ùGod; [then]  understood I their end.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:18">73:18</a> Truly thou settest them in slippery places, thou castest  them down in ruins.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:19">73:19</a> How are they suddenly made desolate! they pass away,  consumed with terrors.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:20">73:20</a> As a dream, when one awaketh, wilt thou, Lord, on arising  despise their image.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:21">73:21</a> When my heart was in a ferment, and I was pricked in my  reins,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:22">73:22</a> Then I was brutish and knew nothing; I was [as] a beast  with thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:23">73:23</a> Nevertheless I am continually with thee: thou hast holden  my right hand;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:24">73:24</a> Thou wilt guide me by thy counsel, and after the glory,  thou wilt receive me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:25">73:25</a> Whom have I in the heavens? and there is none upon earth I  desire beside thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:26">73:26</a> My flesh and my heart faileth: God is the rock of my heart  and my portion for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:27">73:27</a> For behold, they that are far from thee shall perish; thou  destroyest every one that goeth a whoring from thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:28">73:28</a> But as for me, it is good for me to draw near to God: I  have put my trust in the Lord Jehovah, that I may declare all  thy works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:1">74:1</a> {An instruction: of Asaph.} Why, O God, hast thou cast off  for ever? [why] doth thine anger smoke against the sheep of thy  pasture?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:2">74:2</a> Remember thine assembly, which thou hast purchased of old,  which thou hast redeemed [to be] the portion of thine  inheritance, this mount Zion, wherein thou hast dwelt.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:3">74:3</a> Lift up thy steps unto the perpetual desolations:  everything in the sanctuary hath the enemy destroyed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:4">74:4</a> Thine adversaries roar in the midst of thy place of  assembly; they set up their signs [for] signs.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:5">74:5</a> [A man] was known as he could lift up axes in the thicket  of trees;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:6">74:6</a> And now they break down its carved work altogether, with  hatchets and hammers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:7">74:7</a> They have set on fire thy sanctuary, they have profaned the  habitation of thy name to the ground.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:8">74:8</a> They said in their heart, Let us destroy them together:  they have burned up all ùGod's places of assembly in the land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:9">74:9</a> We see not our signs; there is no more any prophet, neither  is there among us any that knoweth how long.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:10">74:10</a> How long, O God, shall the adversary reproach? Shall the  enemy contemn thy name for ever?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:11">74:11</a> Why withdrawest thou thy hand, and thy right hand? [pluck  it] out of thy bosom: consume [them].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:12">74:12</a> But God is my king of old, accomplishing deliverances in  the midst of the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:13">74:13</a> *Thou* didst divide the sea by thy strength; thou didst  break the heads of the monsters on the waters:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:14">74:14</a> *Thou* didst break in pieces the heads of leviathan, thou  gavest him to be meat to those that people the desert.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:15">74:15</a> *Thou* didst cleave fountain and torrent, *thou* driedst  up ever-flowing rivers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:16">74:16</a> The day is thine, the night also is thine; *thou* hast  prepared the moon and the sun:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:17">74:17</a> *Thou* hast set all the borders of the earth; summer and  winter -- *thou* didst form them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:18">74:18</a> Remember this, that an enemy hath reproached Jehovah, and  a foolish people have contemned thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:19">74:19</a> Give not up the soul of thy turtle-dove unto the wild  beast; forget not the troop of thine afflicted for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:20">74:20</a> Have respect unto the covenant; for the dark places of the  earth are full of the dwellings of violence.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:21">74:21</a> Oh let not the oppressed one return ashamed; let the  afflicted and needy praise thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:22">74:22</a> Rise up, O God, plead thine own cause: remember how the  foolish man reproacheth thee all the day;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:23">74:23</a> Forget not the voice of thine adversaries: the tumult of  those that rise up against thee ascendeth continually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:1">75:1</a> {To the chief Musician. 'Destroy not.' A Psalm of Asaph: a  Song.} Unto thee we give thanks, O God, we give thanks; and thy  name is near: thy marvellous works declare it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:2">75:2</a> When I shall receive the assembly, I will judge with  equity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:3">75:3</a> The earth and all the inhabitants thereof are dissolved: I  have established its pillars. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:4">75:4</a> I said unto the boastful, Boast not; and to the wicked,  Lift not up the horn:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:5">75:5</a> Lift not up your horn on high; speak not arrogantly with a  [stiff] neck.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:6">75:6</a> For not from the east nor from the west, nor yet from the  south doth exaltation [come]:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:7">75:7</a> For God is the judge; he putteth down one and exalteth  another.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:8">75:8</a> For in the hand of Jehovah there is a cup, and it foameth  with wine, it is full of mixture; and he poureth out of the  same; yea, the dregs thereof shall all the wicked of the earth  drain off, [and] drink.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:9">75:9</a> But as for me, I will declare for ever; I will sing psalms  to the God of Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:10">75:10</a> And all the horns of the wicked will I cut off; [but] the  horns of the righteous shall be exalted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:1">76:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A Psalm of  Asaph: a Song.} In Judah is God known, his name is great in  Israel;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:2">76:2</a> And in Salem is his tent, and his dwelling-place in Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:3">76:3</a> There broke he the flashings of the bow, shield and sword  and battle. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:4">76:4</a> More glorious art thou, more excellent, than the mountains  of prey.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:5">76:5</a> The stout-hearted are made a spoil, they have slept their  sleep; and none of the men of might have found their hands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:6">76:6</a> At thy rebuke, O God of Jacob, both chariot and horse are  cast into a dead sleep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:7">76:7</a> Thou, thou art to be feared, and who can stand before thee  when once thou art angry?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:8">76:8</a> Thou didst cause judgment to be heard from the heavens; the  earth feared, and was still,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:9">76:9</a> When God rose up to judgment, to save all the meek of the  earth. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:10">76:10</a> For the fury of man shall praise thee; the remainder of  fury wilt thou gird on thyself.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:11">76:11</a> Vow and pay unto Jehovah your God: let all that are round  about him bring presents unto him that is to be feared.</p>
