 <p><a name="an_76:12">76:12</a> He cutteth off the spirit of princes; [he] is terrible to  the kings of the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:1">77:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On Jeduthun. Of Asaph. A Psalm.} My  voice is unto God, and I will cry; my voice is unto God, and he  will give ear unto me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:2">77:2</a> In the day of my trouble, I sought the Lord: my hand was  stretched out in the night, and slacked not; my soul refused to  be comforted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:3">77:3</a> I remembered God, and I moaned; I complained, and my spirit  was overwhelmed. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:4">77:4</a> Thou holdest open mine eyelids; I am full of disquiet and  cannot speak.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:5">77:5</a> I consider the days of old, the years of ancient times.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:6">77:6</a> I remember my song in the night; I muse in mine own heart,  and my spirit maketh diligent search.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:7">77:7</a> Will the Lord cast off for ever? and will he be favourable  no more?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:8">77:8</a> Hath his loving-kindness ceased for ever? hath [his] word  come to an end from generation to generation?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:9">77:9</a> Hath ùGod forgotten to be gracious? or hath he in anger  shut up his tender mercies? Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:10">77:10</a> Then said I, This is my weakness: -- the years of the  right hand of the Most High</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:11">77:11</a> Will I remember, -- the works of Jah; for I will remember  thy wonders of old,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:12">77:12</a> And I will meditate upon all thy work, and muse upon thy  doings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:13">77:13</a> O God, thy way is in the sanctuary: who is so great a ùgod  as God?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:14">77:14</a> Thou art the ùGod that doest wonders; thou hast declared  thy strength among the peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:15">77:15</a> Thou hast with [thine] arm redeemed thy people, the sons  of Jacob and Joseph. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:16">77:16</a> The waters saw thee, O God, the waters saw thee; they  trembled, yea, the depths were troubled:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:17">77:17</a> The thick clouds poured out water; the skies sent out a  sound, yea, thine arrows went abroad:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:18">77:18</a> The voice of thy thunder was in the whirlwind, lightnings  lit up the world; the earth was troubled and it quaked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:19">77:19</a> Thy way is in the sea, and thy paths are in the great  waters; and thy footsteps are not known.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:20">77:20</a> Thou leddest thy people like a flock by the hand of Moses  and Aaron.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:1">78:1</a> {An instruction. Of Asaph.} Give ear, O my people, to my  law; incline your ears to the words of my mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:2">78:2</a> I will open my mouth in a parable; I will utter riddles  from of old,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:3">78:3</a> Which we have heard and known, and our fathers have told  us:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:4">78:4</a> We will not hide [them] from their sons, shewing forth to  the generation to come the praises of Jehovah, and his  strength, and his marvellous works which he hath done.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:5">78:5</a> For he established a testimony in Jacob, and appointed a  law in Israel, which he commanded our fathers, that they should  make them known to their children;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:6">78:6</a> That the generation to come might know [them], the children  that should be born; that they might rise up and tell [them] to  their children,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:7">78:7</a> And that they might set their hope in God, and not forget  the works of ùGod, but observe his commandments;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:8">78:8</a> And might not be as their fathers, a stubborn and  rebellious generation, a generation that prepared not their  heart, and whose spirit was not stedfast with ùGod.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:9">78:9</a> The sons of Ephraim, armed bowmen, turned back in the day  of battle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:10">78:10</a> They kept not the covenant of God, and refused to walk in  his law;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:11">78:11</a> And forgot his doings, and his marvellous works which he  had shewn them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:12">78:12</a> In the sight of their fathers had he done wonders, in the  land of Egypt, the field of Zoan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:13">78:13</a> He clave the sea, and caused them to pass through; and  made the waters to stand as a heap;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:14">78:14</a> And he led them with a cloud in the daytime, and all the  night with the light of fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:15">78:15</a> He clave rocks in the wilderness, and gave [them] drink as  out of the depths, abundantly;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:16">78:16</a> And he brought streams out of the rock, and caused waters  to run down like rivers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:17">78:17</a> Yet they still went on sinning against him, provoking the  Most High in the desert;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:18">78:18</a> And they tempted ùGod in their heart, by asking meat for  their lust;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:19">78:19</a> And they spoke against God: they said, Is ùGod able to  prepare a table in the wilderness?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:20">78:20</a> Behold, he smote the rock, and waters gushed out, and  streams overflowed; is he able to give bread also, or provide  flesh for his people?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:21">78:21</a> Therefore Jehovah heard, and was wroth; and fire was  kindled against Jacob, and anger also went up against Israel:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:22">78:22</a> Because they believed not in God, and confided not in his  salvation;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:23">78:23</a> Though he had commanded the clouds from above, and had  opened the doors of the heavens,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:24">78:24</a> And had rained down manna upon them to eat, and had given  them the corn of the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:25">78:25</a> Man did eat the bread of the mighty; he sent them  provision to the full.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:26">78:26</a> He caused the east wind to rise in the heavens, and by his  strength he brought the south wind;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:27">78:27</a> And he rained flesh upon them as dust, and feathered fowl  as the sand of the seas,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:28">78:28</a> And he let it fall in the midst of their camp, round about  their habitations:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:29">78:29</a> And they did eat, and were well filled; for that they  lusted after, he brought to them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:30">78:30</a> They were not alienated from their lust, their meat was  yet in their mouths,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:31">78:31</a> When the anger of God went up against them; and he slew  the fattest of them, and smote down the chosen men of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:32">78:32</a> For all this, they sinned still, and believed not in his  marvellous works;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:33">78:33</a> And he consumed their days in vanity, and their years in  terror.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:34">78:34</a> When he slew them, then they sought him, and returned and  sought early after ùGod;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:35">78:35</a> And they remembered that God was their rock, and ùGod, the  Most High, their redeemer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:36">78:36</a> But they flattered him with their mouth, and lied unto him  with their tongue;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:37">78:37</a> For their heart was not firm toward him, neither were they  stedfast in his covenant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:38">78:38</a> But he was merciful: he forgave the iniquity, and  destroyed [them] not; but many a time turned he his anger away,  and did not stir up all his fury:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:39">78:39</a> And he remembered that they were flesh, a breath that  passeth away and cometh not again.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:40">78:40</a> How oft did they provoke him in the wilderness, and grieve  him in the desert!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:41">78:41</a> And they turned again and tempted ùGod, and grieved the  Holy One of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:42">78:42</a> They remembered not his hand, the day when he delivered  them from the oppressor,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:43">78:43</a> How he set his signs in Egypt, and his miracles in the  field of Zoan;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:44">78:44</a> And turned their rivers into blood, and their streams,  that they could not drink;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:45">78:45</a> He sent dog-flies among them, which devoured them, and  frogs, which destroyed them;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:46">78:46</a> And he gave their increase unto the caterpillar, and their  labour unto the locust;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:47">78:47</a> He killed their vines with hail, and their sycamore trees  with hail-stones;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:48">78:48</a> And he delivered up their cattle to the hail, and their  flocks to thunderbolts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:49">78:49</a> He cast upon them the fierceness of his anger, wrath, and  indignation, and distress, -- a mission of angels of woes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:50">78:50</a> He made a way for his anger; he spared not their soul from  death, but gave their life over to the pestilence;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:51">78:51</a> And he smote all the firstborn in Egypt, the first-fruits  of their vigour in the tents of Ham.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:52">78:52</a> And he made his own people to go forth like sheep, and  guided them in the wilderness like a flock;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:53">78:53</a> And he led them safely, so that they were without fear;  and the sea covered their enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:54">78:54</a> And he brought them to his holy border, this mountain,  which his right hand purchased;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:55">78:55</a> And he drove out the nations before them, and allotted  them for an inheritance by line, and made the tribes of Israel  to dwell in their tents.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:56">78:56</a> But they tempted and provoked God, the Most High, and kept  not his testimonies,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:57">78:57</a> And they drew back and dealt treacherously like their  fathers: they turned like a deceitful bow.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:58">78:58</a> And they provoked him to anger with their high places, and  moved him to jealousy with their graven images.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:59">78:59</a> God heard, and was wroth, and greatly abhorred Israel:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:60">78:60</a> And he forsook the tabernacle at Shiloh, the tent where he  had dwelt among men,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:61">78:61</a> And gave his strength into captivity, and his glory into  the hand of the oppressor;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:62">78:62</a> And delivered up his people unto the sword, and was very  wroth with his inheritance:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:63">78:63</a> The fire consumed their young men, and their maidens were  not praised in [nuptial] song;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:64">78:64</a> Their priests fell by the sword, and their widows made no  lamentation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:65">78:65</a> Then the Lord awoke as one out of sleep, like a mighty man  that shouteth aloud by reason of wine;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:66">78:66</a> And he smote his adversaries in the hinder part, and put  them to everlasting reproach.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:67">78:67</a> And he rejected the tent of Joseph, and chose not the  tribe of Ephraim,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:68">78:68</a> But chose the tribe of Judah, the mount Zion which he  loved;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:69">78:69</a> And he built his sanctuary like the heights, like the  earth which he hath founded for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:70">78:70</a> And he chose David his servant, and took him from the  sheepfolds:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:71">78:71</a> From following the suckling-ewes, he brought him to feed  Jacob his people, and Israel his inheritance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:72">78:72</a> And he fed them according to the integrity of his heart,  and led them by the skilfulness of his hands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:1">79:1</a> {A Psalm of Asaph.} O God, the nations are come into thine  inheritance: thy holy temple have they defiled; they have laid  Jerusalem in heaps.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:2">79:2</a> The dead bodies of thy servants have they given to be meat  unto the fowl of the heavens, the flesh of thy saints unto the  beasts of the earth:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:3">79:3</a> Their blood have they shed like water round about  Jerusalem, and there was none to bury [them].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:4">79:4</a> We are become a reproach to our neighbours, a mockery and a  derision to them that are round about us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:5">79:5</a> How long, O Jehovah? wilt thou be angry for ever? Shall thy  jealousy burn like fire?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:6">79:6</a> Pour out thy fury upon the nations that have not known  thee, and upon the kingdoms that call not upon thy name:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:7">79:7</a> For they have devoured Jacob, and laid waste his  habitation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:8">79:8</a> Remember not against us the iniquities of [our]  forefathers; let thy tender mercies speedily come to meet us:  for we are brought very low.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:9">79:9</a> Help us, O God of our salvation, because of the glory of  thy name; and deliver us, and forgive our sins, for thy name's  sake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:10">79:10</a> Wherefore should the nations say, Where is their God? Let  the avenging of the blood of thy servants that is shed be known  among the nations in our sight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:11">79:11</a> Let the groaning of the prisoner come before thee;  according to the greatness of thine arm, preserve those that  are appointed to die;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:12">79:12</a> And render unto our neighbours, sevenfold into their  bosom, their reproach, wherewith they have reproached thee, O  Lord.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:13">79:13</a> And we, thy people and the sheep of thy pasture, will give  thanks unto thee for ever; we will shew forth thy praise from  generation to generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:1">80:1</a> {To the chief Musician. On Shoshannim-Eduth. Of Asaph. A  Psalm.} Give ear, O Shepherd of Israel, thou that leadest  Joseph like a flock; thou that sittest [between] the cherubim,  shine forth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:2">80:2</a> Before Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh, stir up thy  strength, and come to our deliverance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:3">80:3</a> O God, restore us; and cause thy face to shine, and we  shall be saved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:4">80:4</a> Jehovah, God of hosts, how long will thine anger smoke  against the prayer of thy people?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:5">80:5</a> Thou hast fed them with the bread of tears, and given them  tears to drink in large measure:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:6">80:6</a> Thou hast made us a strife unto our neighbours, and our  enemies mock among themselves.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:7">80:7</a> Restore us, O God of hosts; and cause thy face to shine,  and we shall be saved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:8">80:8</a> Thou broughtest a vine out of Egypt; thou didst cast out  the nations, and plant it:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:9">80:9</a> Thou preparedst space before it, and it took deep root, and  filled the land;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:10">80:10</a> The mountains were covered with its shadow, and the  branches thereof were [like] cedars of ùGod;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:11">80:11</a> It sent out its boughs unto the sea, and its shoots unto  the river.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:12">80:12</a> Why hast thou broken down its fences, so that all who pass  by the way do pluck it?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:13">80:13</a> The boar out of the forest doth waste it, and the beast of  the field doth feed off it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:14">80:14</a> O God of hosts, return, we beseech thee; look down from  the heavens, and behold, and visit this vine;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:15">80:15</a> Even the stock which thy right hand hath planted, and the  young plant thou madest strong for thyself.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:16">80:16</a> It is burned with fire, it is cut down; they perish at the  rebuke of thy countenance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:17">80:17</a> Let thy hand be upon the man of thy right hand, upon the  son of man whom thou hast made strong for thyself.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:18">80:18</a> So will we not go back from thee. Revive us, and we will  call upon thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:19">80:19</a> Restore us, O Jehovah, God of hosts; cause thy face to  shine, and we shall be saved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:1">81:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Upon the Gittith. [A Psalm] of  Asaph.} Sing ye joyously unto God our strength, shout aloud  unto the God of Jacob;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:2">81:2</a> Raise a song, and sound the tambour, the pleasant harp with  the lute.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:3">81:3</a> Blow the trumpet at the new moon, at the set time, on our  feast day:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:4">81:4</a> For this is a statute for Israel, an ordinance of the God  of Jacob;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:5">81:5</a> He ordained it in Joseph [for] a testimony, when he went  forth over the land of Egypt, [where] I heard a language that I  knew not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:6">81:6</a> I removed his shoulder from the burden; his hands were  freed from the basket.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:7">81:7</a> Thou calledst in trouble, and I delivered thee; I answered  thee in the secret place of thunder; I proved thee at the  waters of Meribah. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:8">81:8</a> Hear, my people, and I will testify unto thee; O Israel, if  thou wouldest hearken unto me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:9">81:9</a> There shall no strange ùgod be in thee, neither shalt thou  worship any foreign ùgod.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:10">81:10</a> I am Jehovah thy God, that brought thee up out of the land  of Egypt: open thy mouth wide, and I will fill it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:11">81:11</a> But my people hearkened not to my voice, and Israel would  none of me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:12">81:12</a> So I gave them up unto their own hearts' stubbornness:  they walked after their own counsels.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:13">81:13</a> Oh that my people had hearkened unto me, that Israel had  walked in my ways!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:14">81:14</a> I would soon have subdued their enemies, and turned my  hand against their adversaries.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:15">81:15</a> The haters of Jehovah would have come cringing unto him;  but their time would have been for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:16">81:16</a> And he would have fed them with the finest of wheat; yea,  with honey out of the rock would I have satisfied thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:1">82:1</a> {A Psalm of Asaph.} God standeth in the assembly of ùGod,  he judgeth among the gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:2">82:2</a> How long will ye judge unrighteously, and accept the person  of the wicked? Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:3">82:3</a> Judge the poor and the fatherless, do justice to the  afflicted and the destitute;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:4">82:4</a> Rescue the poor and needy, deliver them out of the hand of  the wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:5">82:5</a> They know not, neither do they understand; they walk on in  darkness: all the foundations of the earth are moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:6">82:6</a> I have said, Ye are gods, and all of you are children of  the Most High;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:7">82:7</a> But ye shall die like men, and fall like one of the  princes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:8">82:8</a> Arise, O God, judge the earth; for *thou* shalt inherit all  the nations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:1">83:1</a> {A Song; a Psalm of Asaph.} O God, keep not silence; hold  not thy peace, and be not still, O ùGod:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:2">83:2</a> For behold, thine enemies make a tumult; and they that hate  thee lift up the head.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:3">83:3</a> They take crafty counsel against thy people, and consult  against thy hidden ones:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:4">83:4</a> They say, Come, and let us cut them off from being a  nation, and let the name of Israel be mentioned no more.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:5">83:5</a> For they have consulted together with one heart: they have  made an alliance together against thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:6">83:6</a> The tents of Edom and the Ishmaelites, Moab and the  Hagarites;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:7">83:7</a> Gebal, and Ammon, and Amalek; Philistia, with the  inhabitants of Tyre;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:8">83:8</a> Asshur also is joined with them: they are an arm to the  sons of Lot. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:9">83:9</a> Do unto them as to Midian; as to Sisera, as to Jabin, at  the torrent of Kishon:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:10">83:10</a> Who were destroyed at Endor; they became as dung for the  ground.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:11">83:11</a> Make their nobles as Oreb and as Zeeb; and all their  chiefs as Zebah and as Zalmunna.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:12">83:12</a> For they have said, Let us take to ourselves God's  dwelling-places in possession.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:13">83:13</a> O my God, make them like a whirling thing, like stubble  before the wind.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:14">83:14</a> As fire burneth a forest, and as the flame setteth the  mountains on fire,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:15">83:15</a> So pursue them with thy tempest, and terrify them with thy  whirlwind.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:16">83:16</a> Fill their faces with shame, that they may seek thy name,  O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:17">83:17</a> Let them be put to shame and be dismayed for ever, and let  them be confounded and perish:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:18">83:18</a> That they may know that thou alone, whose name is Jehovah,  art the Most High over all the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:1">84:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Upon the Gittith. Of the sons of  Korah. A Psalm.} How amiable are thy tabernacles, O Jehovah of  hosts!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:2">84:2</a> My soul longeth, yea, even fainteth for the courts of  Jehovah; my heart and my flesh cry out for the living ùGod.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:3">84:3</a> Yea, the sparrow hath found a house, and the swallow a nest  for herself, where she layeth her young, thine altars, O  Jehovah of hosts, my King and my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:4">84:4</a> Blessed are they that dwell in thy house: they will be  constantly praising thee. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:5">84:5</a> Blessed is the man whose strength is in thee, -- they, in  whose heart are the highways.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:6">84:6</a> Passing through the valley of Baca, they make it a  well-spring; yea, the early rain covereth it with blessings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:7">84:7</a> They go from strength to strength: [each one] will appear  before God in Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:8">84:8</a> Jehovah, God of hosts, hear my prayer; give ear, O God of  Jacob. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:9">84:9</a> Behold, O God our shield, and look upon the face of thine  anointed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:10">84:10</a> For a day in thy courts is better than a thousand. I had  rather stand at the threshold of the house of my God, than  dwell in the tents of wickedness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:11">84:11</a> For Jehovah Elohim is a sun and shield: Jehovah will give  grace and glory; no good thing will he withhold from them that  walk uprightly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:12">84:12</a> Jehovah of hosts, blessed is the man that confideth in  thee!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:1">85:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Of the sons of Korah. A Psalm.}  Thou hast been favourable, Jehovah, unto thy land; thou hast  turned the captivity of Jacob:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:2">85:2</a> Thou hast forgiven the iniquity of thy people; thou hast  covered all their sin. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:3">85:3</a> Thou hast withdrawn all thy wrath; thou hast turned from  the fierceness of thine anger.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:4">85:4</a> Bring us back, O God of our salvation, and cause thine  indignation toward us to cease.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:5">85:5</a> Wilt thou be angry with us for ever? wilt thou draw out  thine anger from generation to generation?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:6">85:6</a> Wilt thou not revive us again, that thy people may rejoice  in thee?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:7">85:7</a> Shew us thy loving-kindness, O Jehovah, and grant us thy  salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:8">85:8</a> I will hear what ùGod, Jehovah, will speak; for he will  speak peace unto his people, and to his godly ones: but let  them not turn again to folly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:9">85:9</a> Surely his salvation is nigh them that fear him, that glory  may dwell in our land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:10">85:10</a> Loving-kindness and truth are met together; righteousness  and peace have kissed each other:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:11">85:11</a> Truth shall spring out of the earth, and righteousness  shall look down from the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:12">85:12</a> Jehovah also will give what is good, and our land shall  yield its increase.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:13">85:13</a> Righteousness shall go before him, and shall set his  footsteps on the way.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:1">86:1</a> {A Prayer of David.} Incline thine ear, Jehovah, answer me;  for I am afflicted and needy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:2">86:2</a> Keep my soul, for I am godly; O thou my God, save thy  servant who confideth in thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:3">86:3</a> Be gracious unto me, O Lord; for unto thee do I call all  the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:4">86:4</a> Rejoice the soul of thy servant; for unto thee, Lord, do I  lift up my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:5">86:5</a> For thou, Lord, art good, and ready to forgive, and art of  great loving-kindness unto all that call upon thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:6">86:6</a> Give ear, O Jehovah, unto my prayer, and attend to the  voice of my supplications.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:7">86:7</a> In the day of my distress I will call upon thee, for thou  wilt answer me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:8">86:8</a> Among the gods there is none like unto thee, Lord, and  there is nothing like unto thy works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:9">86:9</a> All nations whom thou hast made shall come and worship  before thee, O Lord, and shall glorify thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:10">86:10</a> For thou art great, and doest wondrous things: thou art  God, thou alone.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:11">86:11</a> Teach me thy way, Jehovah; I will walk in thy truth: unite  my heart to fear thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:12">86:12</a> I will praise thee, O Lord my God, with my whole heart;  and I will glorify thy name for evermore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:13">86:13</a> For great is thy loving-kindness toward me, and thou hast  delivered my soul from the lowest Sheol.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:14">86:14</a> O God, the proud are risen against me, and the assembly of  the violent seek after my soul, and they have not set thee  before them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:15">86:15</a> But thou, Lord, art a ùGod merciful and gracious, slow to  anger, and abundant in goodness and truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:16">86:16</a> Turn toward me, and be gracious unto me; give thy strength  unto thy servant, and save the son of thine handmaid.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:17">86:17</a> Shew me a token for good, that they which hate me may see  it, and be ashamed; for thou, Jehovah, hast helped me and  comforted me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:1">87:1</a> {Of the sons of Korah. A Psalm. A Song.} His foundation is  in the mountains of holiness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:2">87:2</a> Jehovah loveth the gates of Zion more than all the  habitations of Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:3">87:3</a> Glorious things are spoken of thee, O city of God. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:4">87:4</a> I will make mention of Rahab and Babylon among them that  know me; behold Philistia, and Tyre, with Ethiopia: this [man]  was born there.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:5">87:5</a> And of Zion it shall be said, This one and that one was  born in her; and the Most High himself shall establish her.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:6">87:6</a> Jehovah will count, when he inscribeth the peoples, This  [man] was born there. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:7">87:7</a> As well the singers as the dancers [shall say], All my  springs are in thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:1">88:1</a> {A Song, a Psalm for the sons of Korah. To the chief  Musician. Upon Mahalath Leannoth. An instruction. Of Heman the  Ezrahite.} Jehovah, God of my salvation, I have cried by day  [and] in the night before thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:2">88:2</a> Let my prayer come before thee; incline thine ear unto my  cry.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:3">88:3</a> For my soul is full of troubles, and my life draweth nigh  to Sheol.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:4">88:4</a> I am reckoned with them that go down into the pit; I am as  a man that hath no strength:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:5">88:5</a> Prostrate among the dead, like the slain that lie in the  grave; whom thou rememberest no more, and who are cut off from  thy hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:6">88:6</a> Thou hast laid me in the lowest pit, in dark places, in the  deeps.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:7">88:7</a> Thy fury lieth hard upon me, and thou hast afflicted [me]  with all thy waves. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:8">88:8</a> Thou hast put my familiar friends far from me; thou hast  made me an abomination unto them: I am shut up, and I cannot  come forth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:9">88:9</a> Mine eye consumeth by reason of affliction. Upon thee,  Jehovah, have I called every day; I have stretched out my hands  unto thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:10">88:10</a> Wilt thou do wonders to the dead? shall the shades arise  and praise thee? Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:11">88:11</a> Shall thy loving-kindness be declared in the grave? thy  faithfulness in Destruction?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:12">88:12</a> Shall thy wonders be known in the dark? and thy  righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:13">88:13</a> But as for me, Jehovah, I cry unto thee, and in the  morning my prayer cometh before thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:14">88:14</a> Why, O Jehovah, castest thou off my soul? [why] hidest  thou thy face from me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:15">88:15</a> I am afflicted and expiring from my youth up; I suffer thy  terrors, [and] I am distracted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:16">88:16</a> Thy fierce anger hath gone over me; thy terrors have  brought me to nought:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:17">88:17</a> They have surrounded me all the day like water; they have  compassed me about together.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:18">88:18</a> Lover and associate hast thou put far from me: my familiar  friends are darkness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:1">89:1</a> {An instruction. Of Ethan the Ezrahite.} I will sing of the  loving-kindness of Jehovah for ever; with my mouth will I make  known thy faithfulness from generation to generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:2">89:2</a> For I said, Loving-kindness shall be built up for ever; in  the very heavens wilt thou establish thy faithfulness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:3">89:3</a> I have made a covenant with mine elect, I have sworn unto  David my servant:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:4">89:4</a> Thy seed will I establish for ever, and build up thy throne  from generation to generation. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:5">89:5</a> And the heavens shall celebrate thy wonders, O Jehovah, and  thy faithfulness in the congregation of the saints.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:6">89:6</a> For who in the heaven can be compared to Jehovah? [who]  among the sons of the mighty shall be likened to Jehovah?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:7">89:7</a> ùGod is greatly to be feared in the council of the saints,  and terrible for all that are round about him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:8">89:8</a> Jehovah, God of hosts, who is like unto thee, the strong  Jah? And thy faithfulness is round about thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:9">89:9</a> *Thou* rulest the pride of the sea: when its waves arise,  *thou* stillest them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:10">89:10</a> Thou hast crushed Rahab as one that is slain; thou hast  scattered thine enemies with the arm of thy strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:11">89:11</a> Thine are the heavens, the earth also is thine; the world  and its fulness, *thou* hast founded them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:12">89:12</a> The north and the south, *thou* hast created them: Tabor  and Hermon triumph in thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:13">89:13</a> Thine is the arm of might: strong is thy hand, high is thy  right hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:14">89:14</a> Righteousness and judgment are the foundation of thy  throne; loving-kindness and truth go before thy face.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:15">89:15</a> Blessed is the people that know the shout of joy: they  walk, O Jehovah, in the light of thy countenance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:16">89:16</a> In thy name are they joyful all the day, and in thy  righteousness are they exalted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:17">89:17</a> For thou art the glory of their strength; and in thy  favour our horn shall be exalted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:18">89:18</a> For Jehovah is our shield, and the Holy One of Israel, our  king.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:19">89:19</a> Then thou spakest in vision of thy Holy One, and saidst, I  have laid help upon a mighty one; I have exalted one chosen out  of the people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:20">89:20</a> I have found David my servant; with my holy oil have I  anointed him:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:21">89:21</a> With whom my hand shall be established; and mine arm shall  strengthen him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:22">89:22</a> No enemy shall exact upon him, nor the son of wickedness  afflict him;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:23">89:23</a> But I will beat down his adversaries before his face, and  will smite them that hate him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:24">89:24</a> And my faithfulness and my loving-kindness shall be with  him, and by my name shall his horn be exalted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:25">89:25</a> And I will set his hand in the sea, and his right hand in  the rivers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:26">89:26</a> *He* shall call unto me, Thou art my father, my ùGod, and  the rock of my salvation;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:27">89:27</a> And as to me, I will make him firstborn, the highest of  the kings of the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:28">89:28</a> My loving-kindness will I keep for him for evermore, and  my covenant shall stand fast with him;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:29">89:29</a> And I will establish his seed for ever, and his throne as  the days of heaven.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:30">89:30</a> If his sons forsake my law, and walk not in mine  ordinances;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:31">89:31</a> If they profane my statutes, and keep not my commandments:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:32">89:32</a> Then will I visit their transgression with the rod, and  their iniquity with stripes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:33">89:33</a> Nevertheless my loving-kindness will I not utterly take  from him, nor belie my faithfulness;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:34">89:34</a> My covenant will I not profane, nor alter the thing that  is gone out of my lips.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:35">89:35</a> Once have I sworn by my holiness; I will not lie unto  David:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:36">89:36</a> His seed shall endure for ever, and his throne as the sun  before me;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:37">89:37</a> It shall be established for ever as the moon, and the  witness in the sky is firm. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:38">89:38</a> But thou hast rejected and cast off; thou hast been very  wroth with thine anointed:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:39">89:39</a> Thou hast made void the covenant of thy servant; thou hast  profaned his crown to the ground:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:40">89:40</a> Thou hast broken down all his hedges; thou hast brought  his strongholds to ruin.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:41">89:41</a> All that pass by the way plunder him; he is become a  reproach to his neighbours.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:42">89:42</a> Thou hast exalted the right hand of his oppressors; thou  hast made all his enemies to rejoice:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:43">89:43</a> Yea, thou hast turned back the edge of his sword, and hast  not made him stand in the battle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:44">89:44</a> Thou hast made his brightness to cease, and cast his  throne down to the ground;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:45">89:45</a> The days of his youth hast thou shortened; thou hast  covered him with shame. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:46">89:46</a> How long, Jehovah, wilt thou hide thyself for ever? shall  thy fury burn like fire?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:47">89:47</a> Remember, as regards me, what life is. Wherefore hast thou  created all the children of men to be vanity?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:48">89:48</a> What man liveth, and shall not see death? Shall he deliver  his soul from the power of Sheol? Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:49">89:49</a> Where, Lord, are thy former loving-kindnesses, [which]  thou swarest unto David in thy faithfulness?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:50">89:50</a> Remember, Lord, the reproach of thy servants -- that I  bear in my bosom [that of] all the mighty peoples --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:51">89:51</a> Wherewith thine enemies, O Jehovah, have reproached,  wherewith they have reproached the footsteps of thine anointed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:52">89:52</a> Blessed be Jehovah for evermore! Amen, and Amen.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:1">90:1</a> {A Prayer of Moses, the man of God.} Lord, *thou* hast been  our dwelling-place in all generations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:2">90:2</a> Before the mountains were brought forth, and thou hadst  formed the earth and the world, even from eternity to eternity  thou art ùGod.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:3">90:3</a> Thou makest [mortal] man to return to dust, and sayest,  Return, children of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:4">90:4</a> For a thousand years, in thy sight, are as yesterday when  it is past, and [as] a watch in the night.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:5">90:5</a> Thou carriest them away as with a flood; they are [as] a  sleep: in the morning they are like grass [that] groweth up:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:6">90:6</a> In the morning it flourisheth and groweth up; in the  evening it is cut down and withereth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:7">90:7</a> For we are consumed by thine anger, and by thy fury are we  troubled.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:8">90:8</a> Thou hast set our iniquities before thee, our secret [sins]  in the light of thy countenance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:9">90:9</a> For all our days pass away in thy wrath: we spend our years  as a [passing] thought.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:10">90:10</a> The days of our years are threescore years and ten; and  if, by reason of strength, they be fourscore years, yet their  pride is labour and vanity, for it is soon cut off, and we fly  away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:11">90:11</a> Who knoweth the power of thine anger? and thy wrath  according to the fear of thee?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:12">90:12</a> So teach [us] to number our days, that we may acquire a  wise heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:13">90:13</a> Return, Jehovah: how long? and let it repent thee  concerning thy servants.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:14">90:14</a> Satisfy us early with thy loving-kindness; that we may  sing for joy and be glad all our days.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:15">90:15</a> Make us glad according to the days [wherein] thou hast  afflicted us, according to the years [wherein] we have seen  evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:16">90:16</a> Let thy work appear unto thy servants, and thy majesty  unto their sons.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:17">90:17</a> And let the beauty of Jehovah our God be upon us; and  establish thou the work of our hands upon us: yea, the work of  our hands, establish thou it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:1">91:1</a> He that dwelleth in the secret place of the Most High shall  abide under the shadow of the Almighty.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:2">91:2</a> I say of Jehovah, My refuge and my fortress; my God, I will  confide in him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:3">91:3</a> Surely *he* shall deliver thee from the snare of the  fowler, [and] from the destructive pestilence.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:4">91:4</a> He shall cover thee with his feathers, and under his wings  shalt thou find refuge: his truth is a shield and buckler.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:5">91:5</a> Thou shalt not be afraid for the terror by night, for the  arrow that flieth by day,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:6">91:6</a> For the pestilence that walketh in darkness, for the  destruction that wasteth at noonday.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:7">91:7</a> A thousand shall fall at thy side, and ten thousand at thy  right hand; [but] it shall not come nigh thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:8">91:8</a> Only with thine eyes shalt thou behold, and see the reward  of the wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:9">91:9</a> Because *thou* hast made Jehovah, my refuge, the Most High,  thy dwelling-place,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:10">91:10</a> There shall no evil befall thee, neither shall any plague  come nigh thy tent.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:11">91:11</a> For he shall give his angels charge concerning thee, to  keep thee in all thy ways:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:12">91:12</a> They shall bear thee up in [their] hands, lest thou dash  thy foot against a stone.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:13">91:13</a> Thou shalt tread upon the lion and the adder; the young  lion and the dragon shalt thou trample under foot.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:14">91:14</a> Because he hath set his love upon me, therefore will I  deliver him; I will set him on high, because he hath known my  name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:15">91:15</a> He shall call upon me, and I will answer him; I will be  with him in trouble, I will deliver him and honour him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:16">91:16</a> With length of days will I satisfy him, and shew him my  salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:1">92:1</a> {A Psalm, a Song, for the Sabbath day.} It is good to give  thanks unto Jehovah, and to sing psalms unto thy name, O Most  High;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:2">92:2</a> To declare thy loving-kindness in the morning, and thy  faithfulness in the nights,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:3">92:3</a> Upon an instrument of ten strings and upon the lute; upon  the Higgaion with the harp.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:4">92:4</a> For thou, Jehovah, hast made me glad through thy work; I  will triumph in the works of thy hands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:5">92:5</a> Jehovah, how great are thy works! Thy thoughts are very  deep:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:6">92:6</a> A brutish man knoweth not, neither doth a fool understand  it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:7">92:7</a> When the wicked spring as the grass, and when all the  workers of iniquity flourish, it is that they may be destroyed  for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:8">92:8</a> And thou, Jehovah, art on high for evermore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:9">92:9</a> For lo, thine enemies, O Jehovah, for lo, thine enemies  shall perish; all the workers of iniquity shall be scattered.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:10">92:10</a> But my horn shalt thou exalt like a buffalo's: I shall be  anointed with fresh oil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:11">92:11</a> And mine eye shall see [its desire] on mine enemies; mine  ears shall hear [it] of the evil-doers that rise up against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:12">92:12</a> The righteous shall shoot forth like a palm-tree; he shall  grow like a cedar on Lebanon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:13">92:13</a> Those that are planted in the house of Jehovah shall  flourish in the courts of our God:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:14">92:14</a> They are still vigorous in old age, they are full of sap  and green;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:15">92:15</a> To shew that Jehovah is upright: [he is] my rock, and  there is no unrighteousness in him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:1">93:1</a> Jehovah reigneth, he hath clothed himself with majesty:  Jehovah hath clothed himself, he hath girded himself with  strength; yea, the world is established, it shall not be moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:2">93:2</a> Thy throne is established of old; thou art from eternity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:3">93:3</a> The floods lifted up, O Jehovah, the floods lifted up their  voice; the floods lifted up their roaring waves.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:4">93:4</a> Jehovah on high is mightier than the voices of many waters,  than the mighty breakers of the sea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:5">93:5</a> Thy testimonies are very sure: holiness becometh thy house,  O Jehovah, for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:1">94:1</a> O ùGod of vengeances, Jehovah, ùGod of vengeances, shine  forth;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:2">94:2</a> Lift up thyself, thou judge of the earth, render the reward  to the proud.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:3">94:3</a> How long shall the wicked, O Jehovah, how long shall the  wicked triumph?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:4">94:4</a> [How long] shall they utter [and] speak insolence -- all  the workers of iniquity boast themselves?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:5">94:5</a> They crush thy people, O Jehovah, and afflict thine  inheritance;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:6">94:6</a> They slay the widow and the stranger, and murder the  fatherless,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:7">94:7</a> And say, Jah will not see, neither will the God of Jacob  regard [it].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:8">94:8</a> Understand, ye brutish among the people; and ye fools, when  will ye be wise?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:9">94:9</a> He that planted the ear, shall he not hear? He that formed  the eye, shall he not see?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:10">94:10</a> He that instructeth the nations, shall not he correct --  he that teacheth man knowledge?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:11">94:11</a> Jehovah knoweth the thoughts of man, that they are vanity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:12">94:12</a> Blessed is the man whom thou chastenest, O Jah, and whom  thou teachest out of thy law;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:13">94:13</a> That thou mayest give him rest from the days of evil,  until the pit be digged for the wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:14">94:14</a> For Jehovah will not cast off his people, neither will he  forsake his inheritance;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:15">94:15</a> For judgment shall return unto righteousness, and all the  upright in heart shall follow it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:16">94:16</a> Who will rise up for me against the evil-doers? who will  stand for me against the workers of iniquity?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:17">94:17</a> If Jehovah had not been my help, my soul had almost dwelt  in silence.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:18">94:18</a> When I said, My foot slippeth, thy loving-kindness, O  Jehovah, held me up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:19">94:19</a> In the multitude of my anxious thoughts within me thy  comforts have delighted my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:20">94:20</a> Shall the throne of wickedness be united to thee, which  frameth mischief into a law?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:21">94:21</a> They band together against the soul of the righteous, and  condemn innocent blood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:22">94:22</a> But Jehovah will be my high tower; and my God the rock of  my refuge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:23">94:23</a> And he will bring upon them their iniquity, and will cut  them off in their own evil: Jehovah our God will cut them off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:1">95:1</a> Come, let us sing aloud to Jehovah, let us shout for joy to  the rock of our salvation;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:2">95:2</a> Let us come before his face with thanksgiving; let us shout  aloud unto him with psalms.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:3">95:3</a> For Jehovah is a great ùGod, and a great king above all  gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:4">95:4</a> In his hand are the deep places of the earth; the heights  of the mountains are his also:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:5">95:5</a> The sea is his, and he made it, and his hands formed the  dry [land].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:6">95:6</a> Come, let us worship and bow down; let us kneel before  Jehovah our Maker.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:7">95:7</a> For he is our God; and we are the people of his pasture and  the sheep of his hand. To-day if ye hear his voice,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:8">95:8</a> Harden not your heart, as at Meribah, as [in] the day of  Massah, in the wilderness;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:9">95:9</a> When your fathers tempted me, proved me, and saw my work.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:10">95:10</a> Forty years was I grieved with the generation, and said,  It is a people that do err in their heart, and they have not  known my ways;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:11">95:11</a> So that I swore in mine anger, that they should not enter  into my rest.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:1">96:1</a> Sing ye unto Jehovah a new song: sing unto Jehovah, all the  earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:2">96:2</a> Sing unto Jehovah, bless his name; publish his salvation  from day to day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:3">96:3</a> Declare his glory among the nations, his wondrous works  among all the peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:4">96:4</a> For Jehovah is great and exceedingly to be praised; he is  terrible above all gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:5">96:5</a> For all the gods of the peoples are idols; but Jehovah made  the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:6">96:6</a> Majesty and splendour are before him; strength and beauty  are in his sanctuary.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:7">96:7</a> Give unto Jehovah, ye families of peoples, give unto  Jehovah glory and strength;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:8">96:8</a> Give unto Jehovah the glory of his name; bring an oblation  and come into his courts;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:9">96:9</a> Worship Jehovah in holy splendour; tremble before him, all  the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:10">96:10</a> Say among the nations, Jehovah reigneth! yea, the world is  established, it shall not be moved; he will execute judgment  upon the peoples with equity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:11">96:11</a> Let the heavens rejoice, and let the earth be glad; let  the sea roar, and the fulness thereof;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:12">96:12</a> Let the field exult and all that is therein. Then shall  all the trees of the forest sing for joy,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:13">96:13</a> Before Jehovah, for he cometh; for he cometh to judge the  earth: he will judge the world with righteousness, and the  peoples in his faithfulness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:1">97:1</a> Jehovah reigneth: let the earth be glad, let the many isles  rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:2">97:2</a> Clouds and darkness are round about him; righteousness and  judgment are the foundation of his throne.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:3">97:3</a> A fire goeth before him, and burneth up his adversaries  round about.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:4">97:4</a> His lightnings lightened the world: the earth saw, and  trembled.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:5">97:5</a> The mountains melted like wax at the presence of Jehovah,  at the presence of the Lord of the whole earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:6">97:6</a> The heavens declare his righteousness, and all the peoples  see his glory.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:7">97:7</a> Ashamed be all they that serve graven images, that boast  themselves of idols. Worship him, all ye gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:8">97:8</a> Zion heard, and rejoiced; and the daughters of Judah were  glad, because of thy judgments, O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:9">97:9</a> For thou, Jehovah, art the Most High above all the earth;  thou art exalted exceedingly above all gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:10">97:10</a> Ye that love Jehovah, hate evil: he preserveth the souls  of his saints, he delivereth them out of the hand of the  wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:11">97:11</a> Light is sown for the righteous, and joy for the upright  in heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:12">97:12</a> Rejoice in Jehovah, ye righteous; and give thanks in  remembrance of his holiness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:1">98:1</a> {A Psalm.} Sing ye unto Jehovah a new song: for he hath  done wondrous things; his right hand and his holy arm hath  wrought salvation for him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:2">98:2</a> Jehovah hath made known his salvation: his righteousness  hath he openly shewed in the sight of the nations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:3">98:3</a> He hath remembered his loving-kindness and his faithfulness  toward the house of Israel: all the ends of the earth have seen  the salvation of our God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:4">98:4</a> Shout aloud unto Jehovah, all the earth; break forth and  shout for joy, and sing psalms.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:5">98:5</a> Sing psalms unto Jehovah with the harp: with the harp, and  the voice of a song;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:6">98:6</a> With trumpets and sound of cornet, make a joyful noise  before the King, Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:7">98:7</a> Let the sea roar, and the fulness thereof; the world, and  they that dwell therein;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:8">98:8</a> Let the floods clap [their] hands; let the mountains sing  for joy together,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:9">98:9</a> Before Jehovah, for he cometh to judge the earth: he will  judge the world with righteousness, and the peoples with  equity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:1">99:1</a> Jehovah reigneth: let the peoples tremble. He sitteth  [between the] cherubim: let the earth be moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:2">99:2</a> Jehovah is great in Zion, and he is high above all the  peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:3">99:3</a> They shall praise thy great and terrible name, -- it is  holy! --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:4">99:4</a> And the strength of the king that loveth justice. *Thou*  hast established equity: it is thou that executest judgment and  righteousness in Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:5">99:5</a> Exalt Jehovah our God, and worship at his footstool. He is  holy!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:6">99:6</a> Moses and Aaron among his priests, and Samuel among them  that call upon his name: they called unto Jehovah, and *he*  answered them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:7">99:7</a> He spoke unto them in the pillar of cloud: they kept his  testimonies, and the statute that he gave them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:8">99:8</a> Jehovah, our God, *thou* answeredst them: a forgiving ùGod  wast thou unto them, though thou tookest vengeance of their  doings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:9">99:9</a> Exalt Jehovah our God, and worship at the hill of his  holiness; for holy is Jehovah our God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:1">100:1</a> {A Psalm of thanksgiving.} Shout aloud unto Jehovah, all  the earth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:2">100:2</a> Serve Jehovah with joy: come before his presence with  exultation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:3">100:3</a> Know that Jehovah is God: it is he that hath made us, and  not we ourselves; [we are] his people, and the sheep of his  pasture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:4">100:4</a> Enter into his gates with thanksgiving [and] into his  courts with praise; give thanks unto him, bless his name:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:5">100:5</a> For Jehovah is good; his loving-kindness [endureth] for  ever; and his faithfulness from generation to generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:1">101:1</a> {A Psalm of David.} I will sing of loving-kindness and  judgment: unto thee, Jehovah, will I sing psalms.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:2">101:2</a> I will behave myself wisely in a perfect way. When wilt  thou come unto me? I will walk within my house in the integrity  of my heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:3">101:3</a> I will set no thing of Belial before mine eyes: I hate the  work of them that turn aside; it shall not cleave to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:4">101:4</a> A perverse heart shall depart from me; I will not know  evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:5">101:5</a> Whoso secretly slandereth his neighbour, him will I  destroy; him that hath a high look and a proud heart will I not  suffer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:6">101:6</a> Mine eyes shall be upon the faithful of the land, that  they may dwell with me; he that walketh in a perfect way, he  shall serve me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:7">101:7</a> He that practiseth deceit shall not dwell within my house;  he that speaketh falsehoods shall not subsist in my sight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:8">101:8</a> Every morning will I destroy all the wicked of the land:  to cut off all workers of iniquity from the city of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:1">102:1</a> {A Prayer of the afflicted, when he is overwhelmed, and  poureth out his complaint before Jehovah.} Jehovah, hear my  prayer, and let my cry come unto thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:2">102:2</a> Hide not thy face from me: in the day of my trouble,  incline thine ear unto me; in the day I call, answer me  speedily.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:3">102:3</a> For my days are consumed like smoke, and my bones are  burned as a firebrand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:4">102:4</a> My heart is smitten and withered like grass; yea, I have  forgotten to eat my bread.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:5">102:5</a> By reason of the voice of my groaning, my bones cleave to  my flesh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:6">102:6</a> I am become like the pelican of the wilderness, I am as an  owl in desolate places;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:7">102:7</a> I watch, and am like a sparrow alone upon the housetop.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:8">102:8</a> Mine enemies reproach me all the day; they that are mad  against me swear by me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:9">102:9</a> For I have eaten ashes like bread, and mingled my drink  with weeping,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:10">102:10</a> Because of thine indignation and thy wrath; for thou hast  lifted me up, and cast me down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:11">102:11</a> My days are like a lengthened-out shadow, and I, I am  withered like grass.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:12">102:12</a> But thou, Jehovah, abidest for ever, and thy memorial  from generation to generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:13">102:13</a> *Thou* wilt rise up, thou wilt have mercy upon Zion: for  it is the time to be gracious to her, for the set time is come.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:14">102:14</a> For thy servants take pleasure in her stones, and favour  her dust.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:15">102:15</a> And the nations shall fear the name of Jehovah, and all  the kings of the earth thy glory.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:16">102:16</a> When Jehovah shall build up Zion, he will appear in his  glory.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:17">102:17</a> He will regard the prayer of the destitute one, and not  despise their prayer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:18">102:18</a> This shall be written for the generation to come; and a  people that shall be created shall praise Jah:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:19">102:19</a> For he hath looked down from the height of his sanctuary;  from the heavens hath Jehovah beheld the earth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:20">102:20</a> To hear the groaning of the prisoner, to loose those that  are appointed to die;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:21">102:21</a> That the name of Jehovah may be declared in Zion, and his  praise in Jerusalem,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:22">102:22</a> When the peoples shall be gathered together, and the  kingdoms, to serve Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:23">102:23</a> He weakened my strength in the way, he shortened my days.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:24">102:24</a> I said, My ùGod, take me not away in the midst of my  days! ... Thy years are from generation to generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:25">102:25</a> Of old hast thou founded the earth, and the heavens are  the work of thy hands:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:26">102:26</a> *They* shall perish, but *thou* continuest; and all of  them shall grow old as a garment: as a vesture shalt thou  change them, and they shall be changed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:27">102:27</a> But thou art the Same, and thy years shall have no end.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:28">102:28</a> The children of thy servants shall abide, and their seed  shall be established before thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:1">103:1</a> {[A Psalm] of David.} Bless Jehovah, O my soul; and all  that is within me, [bless] his holy name!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:2">103:2</a> Bless Jehovah, O my soul, and forget not all his benefits:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:3">103:3</a> Who forgiveth all thine iniquities, who healeth all thy  diseases;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:4">103:4</a> Who redeemeth thy life from the pit, who crowneth thee  with loving-kindness and tender mercies;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:5">103:5</a> Who satisfieth thine old age with good [things]; thy youth  is renewed like the eagle's.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:6">103:6</a> Jehovah executeth righteousness and justice for all that  are oppressed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:7">103:7</a> He made known his ways unto Moses, his acts unto the  children of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:8">103:8</a> Jehovah is merciful and gracious, slow to anger, and  abundant in loving-kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:9">103:9</a> He will not always chide, neither will he keep [his anger]  for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:10">103:10</a> He hath not dealt with us according to our sins, nor  rewarded us according to our iniquities.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:11">103:11</a> For as the heavens are high above the earth, so great is  his loving-kindness toward them that fear him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:12">103:12</a> As far as the east is from the west, so far hath he  removed our transgressions from us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:13">103:13</a> As a father pitieth [his] children, so Jehovah pitieth  them that fear him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:14">103:14</a> For himself knoweth our frame; he remembereth that we are  dust.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:15">103:15</a> As for man, his days are as grass; as a flower of the  field, so he flourisheth:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:16">103:16</a> For the wind passeth over it, and it is gone, and the  place thereof knoweth it no more.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:17">103:17</a> But the loving-kindness of Jehovah is from everlasting  and to everlasting, upon them that fear him, and his  righteousness unto children's children,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:18">103:18</a> To such as keep his covenant and to those that remember  his precepts to do them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:19">103:19</a> Jehovah hath established his throne in the heavens, and  his kingdom ruleth over all.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:20">103:20</a> Bless Jehovah, ye his angels, mighty in strength, that  execute his word, hearkening unto the voice of his word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:21">103:21</a> Bless Jehovah, all ye his hosts; ye ministers of his that  do his will.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:22">103:22</a> Bless Jehovah, all his works, in all places of his  dominion. Bless Jehovah, O my soul!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:1">104:1</a> Bless Jehovah, O my soul! Jehovah my God, thou art very  great; thou art clothed with majesty and splendour;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:2">104:2</a> Covering thyself with light as with a garment, stretching  out the heavens like a tent-curtain; --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:3">104:3</a> Who layeth the beams of his upper chambers in the waters,  who maketh clouds his chariot, who walketh upon the wings of  the wind;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:4">104:4</a> Who maketh his angels spirits; his ministers a flame of  fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:5">104:5</a> He laid the earth upon its foundations: it shall not be  removed for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:6">104:6</a> Thou hadst covered it with the deep, as with a vesture;  the waters stood above the mountains:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:7">104:7</a> At thy rebuke they fled, at the voice of thy thunder they  hasted away; --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:8">104:8</a> The mountains rose, the valleys sank, unto the place which  thou hadst founded for them; --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:9">104:9</a> Thou hast set a bound which they may not pass over, that  they turn not again to cover the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:10">104:10</a> He sendeth the springs into the valleys: they run among  the mountains;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:11">104:11</a> They give drink to every beast of the field; the wild  asses quench their thirst.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:12">104:12</a> The birds of heaven dwell by them; they give forth their  voice from among the branches.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:13">104:13</a> He watereth the mountains from his upper-chambers: the  earth is satisfied with the fruit of thy works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:14">104:14</a> He maketh the grass to grow for the cattle, and herb for  the service of man; bringing forth bread out of the earth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:15">104:15</a> And wine which gladdeneth the heart of man; making [his]  face shine with oil; and with bread he strengtheneth man's  heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:16">104:16</a> The trees of Jehovah are satisfied, the cedars of  Lebanon, which he hath planted,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:17">104:17</a> Where the birds make their nests; [as for] the stork, the  fir trees are her house.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:18">104:18</a> The high mountains are for the wild goats; the cliffs, a  refuge for the rock-badgers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:19">104:19</a> He made the moon for seasons: the sun knoweth its going  down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:20">104:20</a> Thou makest darkness, and it is night, wherein all the  beasts of the forest creep forth:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:21">104:21</a> The young lions roar after the prey, and to seek their  food from ùGod.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:22">104:22</a> The sun ariseth, they retreat, and lay them down in their  dens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:23">104:23</a> Man goeth forth unto his work, and to his labour until  the evening.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:24">104:24</a> How manifold are thy works, O Jehovah! in wisdom hast  thou made them all: the earth is full of thy riches.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:25">104:25</a> Yonder is the great and wide sea: therein are moving  things innumerable, living creatures small and great.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:26">104:26</a> There go the ships; [there] that leviathan, which thou  hast formed to play therein.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:27">104:27</a> These all look unto thee, that thou mayest give their  food in its season:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:28">104:28</a> That thou givest unto them, they gather; thou openest thy  hand, they are filled with good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:29">104:29</a> Thou hidest thy face, they are troubled; thou takest away  their breath, they expire and return to their dust.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:30">104:30</a> Thou sendest forth thy spirit, they are created, and thou  renewest the face of the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:31">104:31</a> The glory of Jehovah will endure for ever; Jehovah will  rejoice in his works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:32">104:32</a> He looketh on the earth, and it trembleth; he toucheth  the mountains, and they smoke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:33">104:33</a> I will sing unto Jehovah as long as I live; I will sing  psalms to my God while I have my being.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:34">104:34</a> My meditation shall be pleasant unto him; I will rejoice  in Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:35">104:35</a> Sinners shall be consumed out of the earth, and the  wicked shall be no more. Bless Jehovah, O my soul. Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:1">105:1</a> Give ye thanks unto Jehovah, call upon his name; make  known his acts among the peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:2">105:2</a> Sing unto him, sing psalms unto him; meditate upon all his  wondrous works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:3">105:3</a> Glory ye in his holy name: let the heart of them rejoice  that seek Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:4">105:4</a> Seek Jehovah and his strength, seek his face continually;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:5">105:5</a> Remember his wondrous works which he hath done, his  miracles and the judgments of his mouth:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:6">105:6</a> Ye seed of Abraham his servant, ye sons of Jacob, his  chosen ones.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:7">105:7</a> He, Jehovah, is our God; his judgments are in all the  earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:8">105:8</a> He is ever mindful of his covenant, -- the word which he  commanded to a thousand generations, --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:9">105:9</a> Which he made with Abraham, and of his oath unto Isaac;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:10">105:10</a> And he confirmed it unto Jacob for a statute, unto Israel  for an everlasting covenant,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:11">105:11</a> Saying, Unto thee will I give the land of Canaan, the lot  of your inheritance;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:12">105:12</a> When they were a few men in number, of small account, and  strangers in it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:13">105:13</a> And they went from nation to nation, from one kingdom to  another people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:14">105:14</a> He suffered no man to oppress them, and reproved kings  for their sakes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:15">105:15</a> [Saying,] Touch not mine anointed ones, and do my  prophets no harm.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:16">105:16</a> And he called for a famine upon the land; he broke the  whole staff of bread.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:17">105:17</a> He sent a man before them: Joseph was sold for a bondman.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:18">105:18</a> They afflicted his feet with fetters; his soul came into  irons;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:19">105:19</a> Until the time when what he said came about: the word of  Jehovah tried him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:20">105:20</a> The king sent and loosed him -- the ruler of peoples --  and let him go free.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:21">105:21</a> He made him lord of his house, and ruler over all his  possessions:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:22">105:22</a> To bind his princes at his pleasure, and teach his elders  wisdom.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:23">105:23</a> And Israel came into Egypt, and Jacob sojourned in the  land of Ham.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:24">105:24</a> And he made his people exceeding fruitful, and made them  mightier than their oppressors.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:25">105:25</a> He turned their heart to hate his people, to deal  subtilly with his servants.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:26">105:26</a> He sent Moses his servant, [and] Aaron whom he had  chosen:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:27">105:27</a> They set his signs among them, and miracles in the land  of Ham.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:28">105:28</a> He sent darkness, and made it dark; and they rebelled not  against his word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:29">105:29</a> He turned their waters into blood, and caused their fish  to die.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:30">105:30</a> Their land swarmed with frogs, -- in the chambers of  their kings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:31">105:31</a> He spoke, and there came dog-flies, [and] gnats in all  their borders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:32">105:32</a> He gave them hail for rain, [and] flaming fire in their  land;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:33">105:33</a> And he smote their vines and their fig-trees, and broke  the trees of their borders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:34">105:34</a> He spoke, and the locust came, and the cankerworm, even  without number;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:35">105:35</a> And they devoured every herb in their land, and ate up  the fruit of their ground.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:36">105:36</a> And he smote every firstborn in their land, the  firstfruits of all their vigour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:37">105:37</a> And he brought them forth with silver and gold; and there  was not one feeble among their tribes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:38">105:38</a> Egypt rejoiced at their departure; for the fear of them  had fallen upon them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:39">105:39</a> He spread a cloud for a covering, and fire to give light  in the night.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:40">105:40</a> They asked, and he brought quails, and satisfied them  with the bread of heaven.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:41">105:41</a> He opened the rock, and waters gushed forth; they ran in  the dry places [like] a river.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:42">105:42</a> For he remembered his holy word, [and] Abraham his  servant;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:43">105:43</a> And he brought forth his people with gladness, his chosen  with rejoicing;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:44">105:44</a> And he gave them the lands of the nations, and they took  possession of the labour of the peoples:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:45">105:45</a> That they might keep his statutes, and observe his laws.  Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:1">106:1</a> Hallelujah! Give ye thanks unto Jehovah; for he is good;  for his loving-kindness [endureth] for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:2">106:2</a> Who can utter the mighty acts of Jehovah? [who] can shew  forth all his praise?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:3">106:3</a> Blessed are they that keep justice, [and] he that doeth  righteousness at all times.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:4">106:4</a> Remember me, O Jehovah, with [thy] favour toward thy  people; visit me with thy salvation:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:5">106:5</a> That I may see the prosperity of thy chosen ones, that I  may rejoice in the joy of thy nation, that I may glory with  thine inheritance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:6">106:6</a> We have sinned with our fathers, we have committed  iniquity, we have done wickedly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:7">106:7</a> Our fathers in Egypt considered not thy wondrous works;  they remembered not the multitude of thy loving-kindnesses; but  they rebelled at the sea, at the Red Sea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:8">106:8</a> Yet he saved them for his name's sake, that he might make  known his might.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:9">106:9</a> And he rebuked the Red Sea, and it dried up; and he led  them through the deeps as through a wilderness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:10">106:10</a> And he saved them from the hand of him that hated [them],  and redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:11">106:11</a> And the waters covered their oppressors: there was not  one of them left.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:12">106:12</a> Then believed they his words; they sang his praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:13">106:13</a> They soon forgot his works; they waited not for his  counsel:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:14">106:14</a> And they lusted exceedingly in the wilderness, and  tempted ùGod in the desert.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:15">106:15</a> Then he gave them their request, but sent leanness into  their soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:16">106:16</a> And they envied Moses in the camp, [and] Aaron, the saint  of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:17">106:17</a> The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan, and covered the  company of Abiram;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:18">106:18</a> And fire was kindled in their company; a flame burned up  the wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:19">106:19</a> They made a calf in Horeb, and did homage to a molten  image;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:20">106:20</a> And they changed their glory into the similitude of an ox  that eateth grass.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:21">106:21</a> They forgot ùGod their Saviour, who had done great things  in Egypt,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:22">106:22</a> Wondrous works in the land of Ham, terrible things by the  Red Sea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:23">106:23</a> And he said that he would destroy them, had not Moses,  his chosen, stood before him in the breach, to turn away his  fury, lest he should destroy [them].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:24">106:24</a> And they despised the pleasant land; they believed not  his word,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:25">106:25</a> But murmured in their tents: they hearkened not unto the  voice of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:26">106:26</a> And he lifted up his hand to them, that he would make  them fall in the wilderness;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:27">106:27</a> And that he would make their seed fall among the nations,  and disperse them through the countries.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:28">106:28</a> And they joined themselves unto Baal-Peor, and ate the  sacrifices of the dead;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:29">106:29</a> And they provoked [him] to anger with their doings; and a  plague broke out among them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:30">106:30</a> Then stood up Phinehas and executed judgment, and the  plague was stayed;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:31">106:31</a> And that was reckoned unto him for righteousness, from  generation to generation, for evermore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:32">106:32</a> And they moved him to wrath at the waters of Meribah, and  it went ill with Moses on their account;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:33">106:33</a> For they provoked his spirit, so that he spoke  unadvisedly with his lips.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:34">106:34</a> They did not destroy the peoples, as Jehovah commanded  them;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:35">106:35</a> But they mingled with the nations, and learned their  works;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:36">106:36</a> And they served their idols; and they were a snare unto  them:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:37">106:37</a> And they sacrificed their sons and their daughters unto  demons,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:38">106:38</a> And shed innocent blood, the blood of their sons and of  their daughters, whom they sacrificed unto the idols of Canaan;  and the land was polluted with blood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:39">106:39</a> And they were defiled with their works, and went  a-whoring in their doings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:40">106:40</a> Then was the anger of Jehovah kindled against his people,  and he abhorred his inheritance;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:41">106:41</a> And he gave them into the hand of the nations; and they  that hated them ruled over them:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:42">106:42</a> And their enemies oppressed them, and they were brought  into subjection under their hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:43">106:43</a> Often did he deliver them; but as for them they provoked  [him] by their counsel, and they were brought low by their  iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:44">106:44</a> But he regarded their distress, when he heard their cry;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:45">106:45</a> And he remembered for them his covenant, and repented  according to the multitude of his loving-kindnesses;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:46">106:46</a> And he caused them to find compassion of all those that  had carried them captives.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:47">106:47</a> Save us, Jehovah our God, and gather us from among the  nations, to give thanks unto thy holy name, [and] to triumph in  thy praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:48">106:48</a> Blessed be Jehovah the God of Israel, from eternity and  to eternity! And let all the people say, Amen! Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:1">107:1</a> Give ye thanks unto Jehovah; for he is good; for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:2">107:2</a> Let the redeemed of Jehovah say so, whom he hath redeemed  from the hand of the oppressor,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:3">107:3</a> And gathered out of the countries, from the east and from  the west, from the north and from the sea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:4">107:4</a> They wandered in the wilderness in a desert way, they  found no city of habitation;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:5">107:5</a> Hungry and thirsty, their soul fainted in them:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:6">107:6</a> Then they cried unto Jehovah in their trouble, [and] he  delivered them out of their distresses,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:7">107:7</a> And he led them forth by a right way, that they might go  to a city of habitation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:8">107:8</a> Let them give thanks unto Jehovah for his loving-kindness,  and for his wondrous works to the children of men;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:9">107:9</a> For he hath satisfied the longing soul and filled the  hungry soul with good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:10">107:10</a> Such as inhabit darkness and the shadow of death, bound  in affliction and iron,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:11">107:11</a> Because they had rebelled against the words of ùGod, and  had despised the counsel of the Most High; ...</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:12">107:12</a> And he bowed down their heart with labour; they stumbled,  and there was none to help:</p>
