 <p><a name="an_107:13">107:13</a> Then they cried unto Jehovah in their trouble, [and] he  saved them out of their distresses;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:14">107:14</a> He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death,  and broke their bands in sunder.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:15">107:15</a> Let them give thanks unto Jehovah for his  loving-kindness, and for his wondrous works to the children of  men;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:16">107:16</a> For he hath broken the gates of bronze, and cut asunder  the bars of iron.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:17">107:17</a> Fools, because of their way of transgression, and because  of their iniquities, are afflicted;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:18">107:18</a> Their soul abhorreth all manner of food, and they draw  near unto the gates of death:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:19">107:19</a> Then they cry unto Jehovah in their trouble, [and] he  saveth them out of their distresses;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:20">107:20</a> He sendeth his word, and healeth them, and delivereth  them from their destructions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:21">107:21</a> Let them give thanks unto Jehovah for his  loving-kindness, and for his wondrous works to the children of  men,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:22">107:22</a> And let them offer the sacrifices of thanksgiving, and  declare his works in joyful song.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:23">107:23</a> They that go down to the sea in ships, that do business  in great waters,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:24">107:24</a> These see the works of Jehovah, and his wonders in the  deep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:25">107:25</a> For he speaketh, and raiseth the stormy wind, which  lifteth up the waves thereof:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:26">107:26</a> They mount up to the heavens, they go down to the depths;  their soul is melted because of trouble;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:27">107:27</a> They reel to and fro, and stagger like a drunken man, and  they are at their wits' end:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:28">107:28</a> Then they cry unto Jehovah in their trouble, and he  bringeth them out of their distresses;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:29">107:29</a> He maketh the storm a calm, and the waves thereof are  still:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:30">107:30</a> And they rejoice because they are quiet; and he bringeth  them unto their desired haven.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:31">107:31</a> Let them give thanks unto Jehovah for his  loving-kindness, and for his wondrous works to the children of  men;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:32">107:32</a> Let them exalt him also in the congregation of the  people, and praise him in the session of the elders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:33">107:33</a> He maketh rivers into a wilderness, and water-springs  into dry ground;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:34">107:34</a> A fruitful land into a plain of salt, for the wickedness  of them that dwell therein.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:35">107:35</a> He maketh the wilderness into a pool of water, and the  dry land into water-springs;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:36">107:36</a> And there he maketh the hungry to dwell, and they  establish a city of habitation;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:37">107:37</a> And sow fields, and plant vineyards, which yield fruits  of increase;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:38">107:38</a> And he blesseth them, so that they are multiplied  greatly; and he suffereth not their cattle to decrease.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:39">107:39</a> And they are diminished and brought low, through  oppression, adversity, and sorrow:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:40">107:40</a> He poureth contempt upon nobles, and causeth them to  wander in a pathless waste;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:41">107:41</a> But he secureth the needy one on high from affliction,  and maketh [him] families like flocks.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:42">107:42</a> The upright shall see it, and rejoice; and all  unrighteousness shall stop its mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:43">107:43</a> Whoso is wise, let him observe these things, and let them  understand the loving-kindnesses of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:1">108:1</a> {A Song, a Psalm of David.} My heart is fixed, O God: I  will sing, yea, I will sing psalms, even [with] my glory.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:2">108:2</a> Awake, lute and harp: I will wake the dawn.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:3">108:3</a> I will give thee thanks among the peoples, O Jehovah; of  thee will I sing psalms among the nations:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:4">108:4</a> For thy loving-kindness is great above the heavens, and  thy truth is unto the clouds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:5">108:5</a> Be thou exalted above the heavens, O God, and thy glory  above all the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:6">108:6</a> That thy beloved ones may be delivered: save with thy  right hand, and answer me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:7">108:7</a> God hath spoken in his holiness: I will exult, I will  divide Shechem, and mete out the valley of Succoth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:8">108:8</a> Gilead is mine, Manasseh is mine, and Ephraim is the  strength of my head; Judah is my law-giver;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:9">108:9</a> Moab is my wash-pot; upon Edom will I cast my sandal; over  Philistia will I shout aloud.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:10">108:10</a> Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me  unto Edom?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:11">108:11</a> [Wilt] not [thou], O God, who didst cast us off? and  didst not go forth, O God, with our armies?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:12">108:12</a> Give us help from trouble; for vain is man's deliverance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:13">108:13</a> Through God we shall do valiantly; and he it is that will  tread down our adversaries.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:1">109:1</a> {To the chief Musician. Of David. A Psalm.} O God of my  praise, be not silent:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:2">109:2</a> For the mouth of the wicked [man] and the mouth of deceit  are opened against me: they have spoken against me with a lying  tongue,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:3">109:3</a> And with words of hatred have they encompassed me; and  they fight against me without a cause.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:4">109:4</a> For my love they are mine adversaries; but I [give myself  unto] prayer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:5">109:5</a> And they have rewarded me evil for good, and hatred for my  love.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:6">109:6</a> Set a wicked [man] over him, and let [the] adversary stand  at his right hand;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:7">109:7</a> When he shall be judged, let him go out guilty, and let  his prayer become sin;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:8">109:8</a> Let his days be few, let another take his office;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:9">109:9</a> Let his sons be fatherless, and his wife a widow;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:10">109:10</a> Let his sons be vagabonds and beg, and let them seek  [their bread] far from their desolate places;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:11">109:11</a> Let the usurer cast the net over all that he hath, and  let strangers despoil his labour;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:12">109:12</a> Let there be none to extend kindness unto him, neither  let there be any to favour his fatherless children;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:13">109:13</a> Let his posterity be cut off; in the generation following  let their name be blotted out:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:14">109:14</a> Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered with  Jehovah, and let not the sin of his mother be blotted out;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:15">109:15</a> Let them be before Jehovah continually, that he may cut  off the memory of them from the earth:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:16">109:16</a> Because he remembered not to shew kindness, but  persecuted the afflicted and needy man, and the broken in  heart, to slay him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:17">109:17</a> And he loved cursing; so let it come unto him. And he  delighted not in blessing; and let it be far from him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:18">109:18</a> And he clothed himself with cursing like his vestment; so  let it come into his bowels like water, and like oil into his  bones;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:19">109:19</a> Let it be unto him as a garment with which he covereth  himself, and for a girdle wherewith he is constantly girded.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:20">109:20</a> Let this be the reward of mine adversaries from Jehovah,  and of them that speak evil against my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:21">109:21</a> But do *thou* for me, Jehovah, Lord, for thy name's sake;  because thy loving-kindness is good, deliver me:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:22">109:22</a> For I am afflicted and needy, and my heart is wounded  within me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:23">109:23</a> I am gone like a shadow when it lengtheneth; I am tossed  about like the locust;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:24">109:24</a> My knees are failing through fasting, and my flesh hath  lost its fatness;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:25">109:25</a> And I am become a reproach unto them; [when] they look  upon me they shake their heads.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:26">109:26</a> Help me, Jehovah my God; save me according to thy  loving-kindness:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:27">109:27</a> That they may know that this is thy hand; that *thou*,  Jehovah, hast done it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:28">109:28</a> Let *them* curse, but bless *thou*; when they rise up,  let them be ashamed, and let thy servant rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:29">109:29</a> Let mine adversaries be clothed with confusion, and let  them cover themselves with their shame as with a mantle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:30">109:30</a> I will greatly celebrate Jehovah with my mouth; yea, I  will praise him among the multitude.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:31">109:31</a> For he standeth at the right hand of the needy, to save  him from those that judge his soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:1">110:1</a> {Psalm of David.} Jehovah said unto my Lord, Sit at my  right hand, until I put thine enemies [as] footstool of thy  feet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:2">110:2</a> Jehovah shall send the sceptre of thy might out of Zion:  rule in the midst of thine enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:3">110:3</a> Thy people shall be willing in the day of thy power, in  holy splendour: from the womb of the morning [shall come] to  thee the dew of thy youth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:4">110:4</a> Jehovah hath sworn, and will not repent, Thou art priest  for ever after the order of Melchisedek.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:5">110:5</a> The Lord at thy right hand will smite through kings in the  day of his anger.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:6">110:6</a> He shall judge among the nations; he shall fill [all  places] with dead bodies; he shall smite through the head over  a great country.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:7">110:7</a> He shall drink of the brook in the way; therefore shall he  lift up the head.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:1">111:1</a> Hallelujah! I will celebrate Jehovah with [my] whole  heart, in the council of the upright, and in the assembly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:2">111:2</a> Great are the works of Jehovah; sought out of all that  delight in them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:3">111:3</a> His work is majesty and splendour, and his righteousness  abideth for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:4">111:4</a> He hath made his wonders to be remembered: Jehovah is  gracious and merciful.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:5">111:5</a> He hath given meat unto them that fear him; he is ever  mindful of his covenant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:6">111:6</a> He hath shewn his people the power of his works, to give  them the heritage of the nations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:7">111:7</a> The works of his hands are truth and judgment; all his  precepts are faithful:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:8">111:8</a> Maintained for ever and ever, done in truth and  uprightness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:9">111:9</a> He sent deliverance unto his people; he hath commanded his  covenant for ever: holy and terrible is his name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:10">111:10</a> The fear of Jehovah is the beginning of wisdom; a good  understanding have all they that do [his precepts]: his praise  abideth for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:1">112:1</a> Hallelujah! Blessed is the man that feareth Jehovah, that  delighteth greatly in his commandments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:2">112:2</a> His seed shall be mighty in the land; the generation of  the upright shall be blessed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:3">112:3</a> Wealth and riches [shall be] in his house; and his  righteousness abideth for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:4">112:4</a> Unto the upright there ariseth light in the darkness; he  is gracious, and merciful, and righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:5">112:5</a> It is well with the man that is gracious and lendeth; he  will sustain his cause in judgment.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:6">112:6</a> For he shall not be moved for ever: the righteous shall be  in everlasting remembrance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:7">112:7</a> He shall not be afraid of evil tidings; his heart is fixed  confiding in Jehovah;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:8">112:8</a> His heart is maintained, he is not afraid, until he see  [his desire] upon his oppressors.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:9">112:9</a> He scattereth abroad, he giveth to the needy; his  righteousness abideth for ever: his horn shall be exalted with  honour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:10">112:10</a> The wicked [man] shall see [it] and be vexed; he shall  gnash with his teeth, and melt away: the desire of the wicked  shall perish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:1">113:1</a> Hallelujah! Praise, ye servants of Jehovah, praise the  name of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:2">113:2</a> Blessed be the name of Jehovah, from this time forth and  for evermore!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:3">113:3</a> From the rising of the sun unto the going down of the  same, let Jehovah's name be praised.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:4">113:4</a> Jehovah is high above all nations, his glory above the  heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:5">113:5</a> Who is like unto Jehovah our God, who hath placed his  dwelling on high;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:6">113:6</a> Who humbleth himself to look on the heavens and on the  earth?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:7">113:7</a> He raiseth up the poor out of the dust; from the dung-hill  he lifteth up the needy,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:8">113:8</a> To set [him] among nobles, among the nobles of his people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:9">113:9</a> He maketh the barren woman to keep house, [as] a joyful  mother of sons. Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:1">114:1</a> When Israel went out of Egypt, the house of Jacob from a  people of strange language,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:2">114:2</a> Judah was his sanctuary, Israel his dominion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:3">114:3</a> The sea saw it and fled, the Jordan turned back;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:4">114:4</a> The mountains skipped like rams, the hills like lambs.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:5">114:5</a> What ailed thee, thou sea, that thou fleddest? thou  Jordan, that thou turnedst back?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:6">114:6</a> Ye mountains, that ye skipped like rams? ye hills, like  lambs?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:7">114:7</a> Tremble, thou earth, at the presence of the Lord, at the  presence of the +God of Jacob,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:8">114:8</a> Who turned the rock into a pool of water, the flint into a  fountain of waters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:1">115:1</a> Not unto us, O Jehovah, not unto us, but unto thy name  give glory, for thy loving-kindness and for thy truth's sake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:2">115:2</a> Wherefore should the nations say, Where then is their God?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:3">115:3</a> But our God is in the heavens: he hath done whatsoever he  pleased.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:4">115:4</a> Their idols are silver and gold, the work of men's hands:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:5">115:5</a> They have a mouth, and they speak not; eyes have they, and  they see not;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:6">115:6</a> They have ears, and they hear not; a nose have they, and  they smell not;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:7">115:7</a> They have hands, and they handle not; feet have they, and  they walk not; they give no sound through their throat.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:8">115:8</a> They that make them are like unto them, -- every one that  confideth in them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:9">115:9</a> O Israel, confide thou in Jehovah: he is their help and  their shield.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:10">115:10</a> House of Aaron, confide in Jehovah: he is their help and  their shield.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:11">115:11</a> Ye that fear Jehovah, confide in Jehovah: he is their  help and their shield.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:12">115:12</a> Jehovah hath been mindful of us: he will bless, he will  bless the house of Israel; he will bless the house of Aaron;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:13">115:13</a> He will bless them that fear Jehovah, both the small and  the great.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:14">115:14</a> Jehovah will add unto you more, unto you and unto your  children.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:15">115:15</a> Ye are blessed of Jehovah, who made the heavens and the  earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:16">115:16</a> The heavens are the heavens of Jehovah, but the earth  hath he given to the children of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:17">115:17</a> The dead praise not Jah, neither any that go down into  silence;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:18">115:18</a> But *we* will bless Jah from this time forth and for  evermore. Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:1">116:1</a> I love Jehovah, for he hath heard my voice [and] my  supplications;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:2">116:2</a> For he hath inclined his ear unto me, and I will call upon  him during [all] my days.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:3">116:3</a> The bands of death encompassed me, and the anguish of  Sheol took hold of me; I found trouble and sorrow:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:4">116:4</a> Then called I upon the name of Jehovah: I beseech thee,  Jehovah, deliver my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:5">116:5</a> Gracious is Jehovah and righteous; and our God is  merciful.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:6">116:6</a> Jehovah keepeth the simple: I was brought low, and he  saved me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:7">116:7</a> Return unto thy rest, O my soul; for Jehovah hath dealt  bountifully with thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:8">116:8</a> For thou hast delivered my soul from death, mine eyes from  tears, my feet from falling.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:9">116:9</a> I will walk before Jehovah in the land of the living.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:10">116:10</a> I believed, therefore have I spoken. As for me, I was  greatly afflicted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:11">116:11</a> I said in my haste, All men are liars.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:12">116:12</a> What shall I render unto Jehovah, [for] all his benefits  toward me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:13">116:13</a> I will take the cup of salvation, and call upon the name  of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:14">116:14</a> I will perform my vows unto Jehovah, yea, before all his  people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:15">116:15</a> Precious in the sight of Jehovah is the death of his  saints.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:16">116:16</a> Yea, Jehovah! for I am thy servant; I am thy servant, the  son of thy handmaid: thou hast loosed my bonds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:17">116:17</a> I will offer to thee the sacrifice of thanksgiving, and  will call upon the name of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:18">116:18</a> I will perform my vows unto Jehovah, yea, before all his  people,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:19">116:19</a> In the courts of Jehovah's house, in the midst of thee, O  Jerusalem. Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:1">117:1</a> Praise Jehovah, all ye nations; laud him, all ye peoples;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:2">117:2</a> For his loving-kindness is great toward us, and the truth  of Jehovah [endureth] for ever. Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:1">118:1</a> Give ye thanks unto Jehovah; for he is good; for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:2">118:2</a> Oh let Israel say, that his loving-kindness [endureth] for  ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:3">118:3</a> Oh let the house of Aaron say, that his loving-kindness  [endureth] for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:4">118:4</a> Oh let them that fear Jehovah say, that his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:5">118:5</a> I called upon Jah in distress; Jah answered me [and set  me] in a large place.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:6">118:6</a> Jehovah is for me, I will not fear; what can man do unto  me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:7">118:7</a> Jehovah is for me among them that help me; and I shall see  [my desire] upon them that hate me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:8">118:8</a> It is better to trust in Jehovah than to put confidence in  man;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:9">118:9</a> It is better to trust in Jehovah than to put confidence in  nobles.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:10">118:10</a> All nations encompassed me; but in the name of Jehovah  have I destroyed them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:11">118:11</a> They encompassed me, yea, encompassed me; but in the name  of Jehovah have I destroyed them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:12">118:12</a> They encompassed me like bees; they are quenched as the  fire of thorns: for in the name of Jehovah have I destroyed  them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:13">118:13</a> Thou hast thrust hard at me that I might fall; but  Jehovah helped me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:14">118:14</a> My strength and song is Jah, and he is become my  salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:15">118:15</a> The voice of triumph and salvation is in the tents of the  righteous: the right hand of Jehovah doeth valiantly;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:16">118:16</a> The right hand of Jehovah is exalted, the right hand of  Jehovah doeth valiantly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:17">118:17</a> I shall not die, but live, and declare the works of Jah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:18">118:18</a> Jah hath chastened me sore; but he hath not given me over  unto death.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:19">118:19</a> Open to me the gates of righteousness: I will enter into  them; Jah will I praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:20">118:20</a> This is the gate of Jehovah: the righteous shall enter  therein.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:21">118:21</a> I will give thee thanks, for thou hast answered me, and  art become my salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:22">118:22</a> [The] stone which the builders rejected hath become the  head of the corner:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:23">118:23</a> This is of Jehovah; it is wonderful in our eyes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:24">118:24</a> This is the day that Jehovah hath made; we will rejoice  and be glad in it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:25">118:25</a> Oh save, Jehovah, I beseech thee; Jehovah, I beseech  thee, oh send prosperity!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:26">118:26</a> Blessed be he that cometh in the name of Jehovah. We have  blessed you out of the house of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:27">118:27</a> Jehovah is ùGod, and he hath given us light: bind the  sacrifice with cords, -- up to the horns of the altar.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:28">118:28</a> Thou art my ùGod, and I will give thee thanks; my God, I  will exalt thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:29">118:29</a> Give ye thanks unto Jehovah; for he is good; for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:1">119:1</a> ALEPH. Blessed are the perfect in the way, who walk in the  law of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:2">119:2</a> Blessed are they that observe his testimonies, that seek  him with the whole heart;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:3">119:3</a> Who also do no unrighteousness: they walk in his ways.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:4">119:4</a> Thou hast enjoined thy precepts, to be kept diligently.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:5">119:5</a> Oh that my ways were directed to keep thy statutes!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:6">119:6</a> Then shall I not be ashamed, when I have respect unto all  thy commandments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:7">119:7</a> I will give thee thanks with uprightness of heart, when I  shall have learned thy righteous judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:8">119:8</a> I will keep thy statutes: forsake me not utterly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:9">119:9</a> BETH. Wherewithal shall a young man cleanse his path? by  taking heed according to thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:10">119:10</a> With my whole heart have I sought thee: let me not wander  from thy commandments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:11">119:11</a> Thy ùword have I hid in my heart, that I might not sin  against thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:12">119:12</a> Blessed art thou, Jehovah! teach me thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:13">119:13</a> With my lips have I declared all the judgments of thy  mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:14">119:14</a> I have rejoiced in the way of thy testimonies, as [much  as] in all wealth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:15">119:15</a> I will meditate upon thy precepts, and have respect unto  thy paths.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:16">119:16</a> I delight myself in thy statutes; I will not forget thy  word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:17">119:17</a> GIMEL. Deal bountifully with thy servant [and] I shall  live; and I will keep thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:18">119:18</a> Open mine eyes, and I shall behold wondrous things out of  thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:19">119:19</a> I am a stranger in the land; hide not thy commandments  from me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:20">119:20</a> My soul breaketh for longing after thy judgments at all  times.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:21">119:21</a> Thou hast rebuked the proud [that are] cursed, who wander  from thy commandments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:22">119:22</a> Roll off from me reproach and contempt; for I observe thy  testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:23">119:23</a> Princes also did sit [and] talk together against me: thy  servant doth meditate in thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:24">119:24</a> Thy testimonies also are my delight [and] my counsellors.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:25">119:25</a> DALETH. My soul cleaveth unto the dust: quicken me  according to thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:26">119:26</a> I have declared my ways, and thou hast answered me: teach  me thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:27">119:27</a> Make me to understand the way of thy precepts, and I will  meditate upon thy wondrous works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:28">119:28</a> My soul melteth for sadness: strengthen me according to  thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:29">119:29</a> Remove from me the way of falsehood, and graciously grant  me thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:30">119:30</a> I have chosen the way of faithfulness; thy judgments have  I set [before me].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:31">119:31</a> I cleave unto thy testimonies; Jehovah, let me not be  ashamed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:32">119:32</a> I will run the way of thy commandments when thou shalt  enlarge my heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:33">119:33</a> HE. Teach me, O Jehovah, the way of thy statutes, and I  will observe it [unto] the end.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:34">119:34</a> Give me understanding, and I will observe thy law; and I  will keep it with [my] whole heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:35">119:35</a> Make me to walk in the path of thy commandments; for  therein do I delight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:36">119:36</a> Incline my heart unto thy testimonies, and not to gain.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:37">119:37</a> Turn away mine eyes from beholding vanity; quicken me in  thy way.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:38">119:38</a> Establish thy ùword unto thy servant, who is [devoted] to  thy fear.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:39">119:39</a> Turn away my reproach which I fear; for thy judgments are  good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:40">119:40</a> Behold, I have longed after thy precepts: quicken me in  thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:41">119:41</a> VAU. And let thy loving-kindness come unto me, O Jehovah,  -- thy salvation according to thy ùword.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:42">119:42</a> So shall I have wherewith to answer him that reproacheth  me; for I confide in thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:43">119:43</a> And take not the word of truth utterly out of my mouth;  because I have hoped in thy judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:44">119:44</a> Then will I keep thy law continually, for ever and ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:45">119:45</a> And I will walk at liberty, for I have sought thy  precepts;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:46">119:46</a> And I will speak of thy testimonies before kings, and  will not be ashamed;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:47">119:47</a> And I will delight myself in thy commandments, which I  have loved;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:48">119:48</a> And I will lift up my hands unto thy commandments, which  I have loved, and I will meditate in thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:49">119:49</a> ZAIN. Remember the word for thy servant, upon which thou  hast caused me to hope.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:50">119:50</a> This is my comfort in mine affliction; for thy ùword hath  quickened me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:51">119:51</a> The proud have derided me beyond measure: I have not  declined from thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:52">119:52</a> I remembered thy judgments of old, O Jehovah, and have  comforted myself.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:53">119:53</a> Burning indignation hath taken hold upon me because of  the wicked who forsake thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:54">119:54</a> Thy statutes have been my songs in the house of my  pilgrimage.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:55">119:55</a> I have remembered thy name, O Jehovah, in the night, and  have kept thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:56">119:56</a> This I have had, because I have observed thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:57">119:57</a> CHETH. My portion, O Jehovah, I have said, is to keep thy  words.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:58">119:58</a> I have sought thy favour with [my] whole heart: be  gracious unto me according to thy ùword.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:59">119:59</a> I have thought on my ways, and turned my feet unto thy  testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:60">119:60</a> I have made haste, and not delayed, to keep thy  commandments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:61">119:61</a> The bands of the wicked have wrapped me round: I have not  forgotten thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:62">119:62</a> At midnight I rise up to give thanks unto thee, because  of thy righteous judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:63">119:63</a> I am the companion of all that fear thee, and of them  that keep thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:64">119:64</a> The earth, O Jehovah, is full of thy loving-kindness:  teach me thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:65">119:65</a> TETH. Thou hast dealt well with thy servant, O Jehovah,  according to thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:66">119:66</a> Teach me good discernment and knowledge; for I have  believed in thy commandments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:67">119:67</a> Before I was afflicted I went astray, but now I keep thy  ùword.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:68">119:68</a> Thou art good, and doest good; teach me thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:69">119:69</a> The proud have forged falsehood against me: I will  observe thy precepts with [my] whole heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:70">119:70</a> Their heart is as fat as grease: as for me, I delight in  thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:71">119:71</a> It is good for me that I have been afflicted, that I  might learn thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:72">119:72</a> The law of thy mouth is better unto me than thousands of  gold and silver.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:73">119:73</a> YOD. Thy hands have made me and fashioned me: give me  understanding, and I will learn thy commandments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:74">119:74</a> They that fear thee will see me, and rejoice; because I  have hoped in thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:75">119:75</a> I know, Jehovah, that thy Judgments are righteousness,  and that in faithfulness thou hast afflicted me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:76">119:76</a> Oh let thy loving-kindness be for my comfort, according  to thy ùword unto thy servant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:77">119:77</a> Let thy tender mercies come unto me, that I may live; for  thy law is my delight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:78">119:78</a> Let the proud be ashamed; for they have acted perversely  towards me with falsehood: as for me, I meditate in thy  precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:79">119:79</a> Let those that fear thee turn unto me, and those that  know thy testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:80">119:80</a> Let my heart be perfect in thy statutes, that I be not  ashamed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:81">119:81</a> CAPH. My soul fainteth for thy salvation; I hope in thy  word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:82">119:82</a> Mine eyes fail for thy ùword, saying, When wilt thou  comfort me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:83">119:83</a> For I am become like a bottle in the smoke; I do not  forget thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:84">119:84</a> How many shall be the days of thy servant? when wilt thou  execute judgment on them that persecute me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:85">119:85</a> The proud have digged pits for me, which is not according  to thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:86">119:86</a> All thy commandments are faithfulness. They persecute me  wrongfully: help thou me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:87">119:87</a> They had almost consumed me upon the earth; but as for  me, I forsook not thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:88">119:88</a> Quicken me according to thy loving-kindness, and I will  keep the testimony of thy mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:89">119:89</a> LAMED. For ever, O Jehovah, thy word is settled in the  heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:90">119:90</a> Thy faithfulness is from generation to generation: thou  hast established the earth, and it standeth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:91">119:91</a> By thine ordinances they stand this day; for all things  are thy servants.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:92">119:92</a> Unless thy law had been my delight, I should then have  perished in mine affliction.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:93">119:93</a> I will never forget thy precepts; for by them thou hast  quickened me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:94">119:94</a> I am thine, save me; for I have sought thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:95">119:95</a> The wicked have awaited me to destroy me; [but] I attend  unto thy testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:96">119:96</a> I have seen an end of all perfection: thy commandment is  exceeding broad.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:97">119:97</a> MEM. Oh how I love thy law! it is my meditation all the  day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:98">119:98</a> Thy commandments make me wiser than mine enemies; for  they are ever with me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:99">119:99</a> I have more understanding than all my teachers; for thy  testimonies are my meditation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:100">119:100</a> I understand more than the aged, because I have observed  thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:101">119:101</a> I have refrained my feet from every evil path, that I  might keep thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:102">119:102</a> I have not departed from thy judgments; for it is thou  that hast taught me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:103">119:103</a> How sweet are thy ùwords unto my taste! more than honey  to my mouth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:104">119:104</a> From thy precepts I get understanding; therefore I hate  every false path.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:105">119:105</a> NUN. Thy word is a lamp unto my feet, and a light unto  my path.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:106">119:106</a> I have sworn, and I will perform it, that I will keep  thy righteous judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:107">119:107</a> I am afflicted very much; O Jehovah, quicken me  according to thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:108">119:108</a> Accept, I beseech thee, Jehovah, the voluntary-offerings  of my mouth, and teach me thy judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:109">119:109</a> My life is continually in my hand; but I do not forget  thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:110">119:110</a> The wicked have laid a snare for me; but I have not  wandered from thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:111">119:111</a> Thy testimonies have I taken as a heritage for ever; for  they are the rejoicing of my heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:112">119:112</a> I have inclined my heart to perform thy statutes for  ever, unto the end.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:113">119:113</a> SAMECH. The double-minded have I hated; but thy law do I  love.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:114">119:114</a> Thou art my hiding-place and my shield: I hope in thy  word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:115">119:115</a> Depart from me, ye evil-doers; and I will observe the  commandments of my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:116">119:116</a> Uphold me according to thy ùword, that I may live; and  let me not be ashamed of my hope.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:117">119:117</a> Hold thou me up, and I shall be safe; and I will have  respect unto thy statutes continually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:118">119:118</a> Thou hast set at nought all them that wander from thy  statutes; for their deceit is falsehood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:119">119:119</a> Thou puttest away all the wicked of the earth [like]  dross; therefore I love thy testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:120">119:120</a> My flesh shuddereth for fear of thee; and I am afraid of  thy judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:121">119:121</a> AIN. I have done judgment and justice: leave me not to  mine oppressors.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:122">119:122</a> Be surety for thy servant for good; let not the proud  oppress me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:123">119:123</a> Mine eyes fail for thy salvation, and for the ùword of  thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:124">119:124</a> Deal with thy servant according to thy loving-kindness,  and teach me thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:125">119:125</a> I am thy servant; give me understanding that I may know  thy testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:126">119:126</a> It is time for Jehovah to work: they have made void thy  law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:127">119:127</a> Therefore I love thy commandments above gold, yea, above  fine gold.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:128">119:128</a> Therefore I regard all [thy] precepts concerning all  things to be right: I hate every false path.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:129">119:129</a> PE. Thy testimonies are wonderful; therefore doth my  soul observe them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:130">119:130</a> The entrance of thy words giveth light, giving  understanding unto the simple.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:131">119:131</a> I opened my mouth wide and panted; for I longed for thy  commandments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:132">119:132</a> Turn unto me, and be gracious unto me, as thou art wont  to do unto those that love thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:133">119:133</a> Establish my steps in thy ùword; and let not any  iniquity have dominion over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:134">119:134</a> Deliver me from the oppression of man; and I will keep  thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:135">119:135</a> Make thy face to shine upon thy servant, and teach me  thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:136">119:136</a> Mine eyes run down with streams of water, because they  keep not thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:137">119:137</a> TZADE. Righteous art thou, Jehovah, and upright are thy  judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:138">119:138</a> Thou hast commanded thy testimonies in righteousness and  exceeding faithfulness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:139">119:139</a> My zeal destroyeth me, because mine oppressors have  forgotten thy words.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:140">119:140</a> Thy ùword is exceeding pure, and thy servant loveth it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:141">119:141</a> I am little and despised: thy precepts have I not  forgotten.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:142">119:142</a> Thy righteousness is an everlasting righteousness, and  thy law is truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:143">119:143</a> Trouble and anguish have taken hold upon me: thy  commandments are my delights.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:144">119:144</a> The righteousness of thy testimonies is for ever: give  me understanding, and I shall live.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:145">119:145</a> KOPH. I have called with [my] whole heart; answer me, O  Jehovah: I will observe thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:146">119:146</a> I call upon thee; save me, and I will keep thy  testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:147">119:147</a> I anticipate the morning-dawn and I cry: I hope in thy  word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:148">119:148</a> Mine eyes anticipate the night-watches, that I may  meditate in thy ùword.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:149">119:149</a> Hear my voice according to thy loving-kindness: O  Jehovah, quicken me according to thy judgment.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:150">119:150</a> They have drawn nigh that follow after mischief: they  are far from thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:151">119:151</a> Thou, Jehovah, art near, and all thy commandments are  truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:152">119:152</a> From thy testimonies, I have known of old that thou hast  founded them for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:153">119:153</a> RESH. See mine affliction, and deliver me; for I have  not forgotten thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:154">119:154</a> Plead my cause, and redeem me: quicken me according to  thy ùword.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:155">119:155</a> Salvation is far from the wicked; for they seek not thy  statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:156">119:156</a> Many are thy tender mercies, O Jehovah; quicken me  according to thy judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:157">119:157</a> Many are my persecutors and mine oppressors; I have not  declined from thy testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:158">119:158</a> I beheld them that deal treacherously, and was grieved;  because they kept not thy ùword.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:159">119:159</a> See how I have loved thy precepts: quicken me, O  Jehovah, according to thy loving-kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:160">119:160</a> The sum of thy word is truth, and every righteous  judgment of thine is for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:161">119:161</a> SHIN. Princes have persecuted me without a cause; but my  heart standeth in awe of thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:162">119:162</a> I have joy in thy ùword, as one that findeth great  spoil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:163">119:163</a> I hate and abhor falsehood; thy law do I love.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:164">119:164</a> Seven times a day do I praise thee because of thy  righteous judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:165">119:165</a> Great peace have they that love thy law, and nothing  doth stumble them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:166">119:166</a> I have hoped for thy salvation, O Jehovah, and have done  thy commandments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:167">119:167</a> My soul hath kept thy testimonies, and I love them  exceedingly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:168">119:168</a> I have kept thy precepts and thy testimonies; for all my  ways are before thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:169">119:169</a> TAU. Let my cry come near before thee, Jehovah: give me  understanding according to thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:170">119:170</a> Let my supplication come before thee: deliver me  according to thy ùword.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:171">119:171</a> My lips shall pour forth praise when thou hast taught me  thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:172">119:172</a> My tongue shall speak aloud of thy ùword; for all thy  commandments are righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:173">119:173</a> Let thy hand be for my help; for I have chosen thy  precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:174">119:174</a> I have longed for thy salvation, O Jehovah, and thy law  is my delight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:175">119:175</a> Let my soul live, and it shall praise thee; and let thy  judgments help me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:176">119:176</a> I have gone astray like a lost sheep: seek thy servant;  for I have not forgotten thy commandments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:1">120:1</a> {A Song of degrees.} In my trouble I called unto Jehovah,  and he answered me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:2">120:2</a> Jehovah, deliver my soul from the lying lip, from the  deceitful tongue.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:3">120:3</a> What shall be given unto thee, what shall be added unto  thee, thou deceitful tongue?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:4">120:4</a> Sharp arrows of a mighty one, with burning coals of  broom-wood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:5">120:5</a> Woe is me, that I sojourn in Meshech, that I dwell among  the tents of Kedar!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:6">120:6</a> My soul hath long dwelt with them that hate peace.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:7">120:7</a> I [am for] peace; but when I speak, *they* [are] for war.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:1">121:1</a> {A Song of degrees.} I lift up mine eyes unto the  mountains: whence shall my help come?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:2">121:2</a> My help [cometh] from Jehovah, who made the heavens and  the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:3">121:3</a> He will not suffer thy foot to be moved; he that keepeth  thee will not slumber.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:4">121:4</a> Behold, he that keepeth Israel will neither slumber nor  sleep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:5">121:5</a> Jehovah is thy keeper, Jehovah is thy shade upon thy right  hand;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:6">121:6</a> The sun shall not smite thee by day, nor the moon by  night.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:7">121:7</a> Jehovah will keep thee from all evil; he will keep thy  soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:8">121:8</a> Jehovah will keep thy going out and thy coming in, from  henceforth and for evermore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:1">122:1</a> {A Song of degrees. Of David.} I rejoiced when they said  unto me, Let us go into the house of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:2">122:2</a> Our feet shall stand within thy gates, O Jerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:3">122:3</a> Jerusalem, which art built as a city that is compact  together,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:4">122:4</a> Whither the tribes go up, the tribes of Jah, a testimony  to Israel, to give thanks unto the name of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:5">122:5</a> For there are set thrones for judgment, the thrones of the  house of David.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:6">122:6</a> Pray for the peace of Jerusalem: they shall prosper that  love thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:7">122:7</a> Peace be within thy bulwarks, prosperity within thy  palaces.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:8">122:8</a> For my brethren and companions' sakes I will say, Peace be  within thee!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:9">122:9</a> Because of the house of Jehovah our God I will seek thy  good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:1">123:1</a> {A Song of degrees.} Unto thee do I lift up mine eyes, O  thou that dwellest in the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:2">123:2</a> Behold, as the eyes of servants [look] unto the hand of  their masters, as the eyes of a maiden unto the hand of her  mistress, so our eyes [are directed] to Jehovah our God, until  he be gracious unto us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:3">123:3</a> Be gracious unto us, O Jehovah, be gracious unto us; for  we are exceedingly filled with contempt.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:4">123:4</a> Our soul is exceedingly filled with the scorning of those  that are at ease, with the contempt of the proud.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:1">124:1</a> {A Song of degrees. Of David.} If it had not been Jehovah  who was for us -- oh let Israel say --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:2">124:2</a> If it had not been Jehovah who was for us, when men rose  up against us,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:3">124:3</a> Then they had swallowed us up alive, when their anger was  kindled against us;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:4">124:4</a> Then the waters had overwhelmed us, a torrent had gone  over our soul;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:5">124:5</a> Then the proud waters had gone over our soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:6">124:6</a> Blessed be Jehovah, who gave us not up a prey to their  teeth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:7">124:7</a> Our soul is escaped as a bird out of the snare of the  fowlers: the snare is broken, and we have escaped.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:8">124:8</a> Our help is in the name of Jehovah, the maker of heavens  and earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:1">125:1</a> {A Song of degrees.} They that confide in Jehovah are as  mount Zion, which cannot be moved; it abideth for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:2">125:2</a> Jerusalem! -- mountains are round about her, and Jehovah  is round about his people, from henceforth and for evermore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:3">125:3</a> For the sceptre of wickedness shall not rest upon the lot  of the righteous; lest the righteous put forth their hands unto  iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:4">125:4</a> Do good, O Jehovah, unto the good, and to them that are  upright in their hearts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:5">125:5</a> But as for such as turn aside unto their crooked ways,  Jehovah will lead them forth with the workers of iniquity.  Peace be upon Israel!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:1">126:1</a> {A Song of degrees.} When Jehovah turned the captivity of  Zion, we were like them that dream.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:2">126:2</a> Then was our mouth filled with laughter, and our tongue  with rejoicing: then said they among the nations, Jehovah hath  done great things for them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:3">126:3</a> Jehovah hath done great things for us; [and] we are  joyful.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:4">126:4</a> Turn our captivity, O Jehovah, as the streams in the  south.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:5">126:5</a> They that sow in tears shall reap with rejoicing:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:6">126:6</a> He goeth forth and weepeth, bearing seed for scattering;  he cometh again with rejoicing, bearing his sheaves.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:1">127:1</a> {A Song of degrees. Of Solomon.} Unless Jehovah build the  house, in vain do its builders labour in it; unless Jehovah  keep the city, the keeper watcheth in vain:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:2">127:2</a> It is vain for you to rise up early, to lie down late, to  eat the bread of sorrows: so to his beloved one he giveth  sleep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:3">127:3</a> Lo, children are an inheritance from Jehovah, [and] the  fruit of the womb a reward.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:4">127:4</a> As arrows in the hand of a mighty man, so are the children  of youth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:5">127:5</a> Happy is the man that hath filled his quiver with them.  They shall not be ashamed when they speak with enemies in the  gate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:1">128:1</a> {A Song of degrees.} Blessed is every one that feareth  Jehovah, that walketh in his ways.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:2">128:2</a> For thou shalt eat the labour of thy hands; happy shalt  thou be, and it shall be well with thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:3">128:3</a> Thy wife shall be as a fruitful vine in the inner part of  thy house; thy children like olive-plants round about thy  table.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:4">128:4</a> Behold, thus shall the man be blessed that feareth  Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:5">128:5</a> Jehovah will bless thee out of Zion; and mayest thou see  the good of Jerusalem all the days of thy life,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:6">128:6</a> And see thy children's children. Peace be upon Israel!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:1">129:1</a> {A Song of degrees.} Many a time have they afflicted me  from my youth -- oh let Israel say --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:2">129:2</a> Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth; yet they  have not prevailed against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:3">129:3</a> The ploughers ploughed upon my back; they made long their  furrows.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:4">129:4</a> Jehovah is righteous: he hath cut asunder the cords of the  wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:5">129:5</a> Let them be ashamed and turned backward, all that hate  Zion;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:6">129:6</a> Let them be as the grass upon the house-tops, which  withereth before it is plucked up,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:7">129:7</a> Wherewith the mower filleth not his hand, nor he that  bindeth sheaves his bosom;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:8">129:8</a> Neither do the passers-by say, The blessing of Jehovah be  upon you; we bless you in the name of Jehovah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:1">130:1</a> {A Song of degrees.} Out of the depths do I call upon  thee, Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:2">130:2</a> Lord, hear my voice; let thine ears be attentive to the  voice of my supplication.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:3">130:3</a> If thou, Jah, shouldest mark iniquities, Lord, who shall  stand?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:4">130:4</a> But there is forgiveness with thee, that thou mayest be  feared.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:5">130:5</a> I wait for Jehovah; my soul doth wait, and in his word do  I hope.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:6">130:6</a> My soul [waiteth] for the Lord more than the watchers  [wait] for the morning, [more than] the watchers for the  morning.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:7">130:7</a> Let Israel hope in Jehovah, because with Jehovah there is  loving-kindness, and with him is plenteous redemption;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:8">130:8</a> And he will redeem Israel from all his iniquities.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:1">131:1</a> {A Song of degrees. Of David.} Jehovah, my heart is not  haughty, nor mine eyes lofty; neither do I exercise myself in  great matters, and in things too wonderful for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:2">131:2</a> Surely I have restrained and composed my soul, like a  weaned child with its mother: my soul within me is as a weaned  child.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:3">131:3</a> Let Israel hope in Jehovah, from henceforth and for  evermore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:1">132:1</a> {A Song of degrees.} Jehovah, remember for David all his  affliction;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:2">132:2</a> How he swore unto Jehovah, vowed unto the Mighty One of  Jacob:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:3">132:3</a> I will not come into the tent of my house, I will not go  up to the couch of my bed;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:4">132:4</a> I will not give sleep to mine eyes, slumber to mine  eyelids,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:5">132:5</a> Until I find out a place for Jehovah, habitations for the  Mighty One of Jacob. ...</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:6">132:6</a> Behold, we heard of it at Ephratah, we found it in the  fields of the wood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:7">132:7</a> Let us go into his habitations, let us worship at his  footstool.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:8">132:8</a> Arise, Jehovah, into thy rest, thou and the ark of thy  strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:9">132:9</a> Let thy priests be clothed with righteousness, and let thy  saints shout for joy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:10">132:10</a> For thy servant David's sake, turn not away the face of  thine anointed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:11">132:11</a> Jehovah hath sworn [in] truth unto David; he will not  turn from it: Of the fruit of thy body will I set upon thy  throne;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:12">132:12</a> If thy children keep my covenant, and my testimonies  which I will teach them, their children also for evermore shall  sit upon thy throne.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:13">132:13</a> For Jehovah hath chosen Zion; he hath desired it for his  dwelling:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:14">132:14</a> This is my rest for ever; here will I dwell, for I have  desired it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:15">132:15</a> I will abundantly bless her provision; I will satisfy her  needy ones with bread;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:16">132:16</a> And I will clothe her priests with salvation, and her  saints shall shout aloud for joy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:17">132:17</a> There will I cause the horn of David to bud forth; I have  ordained a lamp for mine anointed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:18">132:18</a> His enemies will I clothe with shame; but upon himself  shall his crown flourish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:1">133:1</a> {A Song of degrees. Of David.} Behold, how good and how  pleasant it is for brethren to dwell together in unity!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:2">133:2</a> Like the precious oil upon the head, that ran down upon  the beard, upon Aaron's beard, that ran down to the hem of his  garments;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:3">133:3</a> As the dew of Hermon that descendeth on the mountains of  Zion; for there hath Jehovah commanded the blessing, life for  evermore.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:1">134:1</a> {A Song of degrees.} Behold, bless Jehovah, all ye  servants of Jehovah, who by night stand in the house of  Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:2">134:2</a> Lift up your hands in the sanctuary, and bless Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:3">134:3</a> Jehovah, the maker of heavens and earth, bless thee out of  Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:1">135:1</a> Hallelujah! Praise the name of Jehovah; praise, ye  servants of Jehovah,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:2">135:2</a> Ye that stand in the house of Jehovah, in the courts of  the house of our God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:3">135:3</a> Praise ye Jah; for Jehovah is good: sing psalms unto his  name; for it is pleasant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:4">135:4</a> For Jah hath chosen Jacob unto himself, Israel for his own  possession.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:5">135:5</a> For *I* know that Jehovah is great, and our Lord is above  all gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:6">135:6</a> Whatsoever Jehovah pleased, he hath done in the heavens  and on the earth, in the seas and all deeps;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:7">135:7</a> Who causeth the vapours to ascend from the ends of the  earth; who maketh lightnings for the rain; who bringeth the  wind out of his treasuries:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:8">135:8</a> Who smote the firstborn of Egypt, both of man and beast;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:9">135:9</a> Who sent signs and miracles into the midst of thee, O  Egypt, upon Pharaoh and upon all his servants;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:10">135:10</a> Who smote great nations, and slew mighty kings,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:11">135:11</a> Sihon king of the Amorites, and Og king of Bashan, and  all the kingdoms of Canaan;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:12">135:12</a> And gave their land for an inheritance, an inheritance  unto Israel his people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:13">135:13</a> Thy name, O Jehovah, is for ever; thy memorial, O  Jehovah, from generation to generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:14">135:14</a> For Jehovah will judge his people, and will repent in  favour of his servants.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:15">135:15</a> The idols of the nations are silver and gold, the work of  men's hands:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:16">135:16</a> They have a mouth, and they speak not; eyes have they,  and they see not;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:17">135:17</a> They have ears, and they hear not; neither is there any  breath in their mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:18">135:18</a> They that make them are like unto them, -- every one that  confideth in them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:19">135:19</a> House of Israel, bless ye Jehovah; house of Aaron, bless  ye Jehovah;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:20">135:20</a> House of Levi, bless ye Jehovah; ye that fear Jehovah,  bless Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:21">135:21</a> Blessed be Jehovah out of Zion, who dwelleth at  Jerusalem! Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:1">136:1</a> Give ye thanks unto Jehovah, for he is good; for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:2">136:2</a> Give thanks unto the God of gods, for his loving-kindness  [endureth] for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:3">136:3</a> Give thanks unto the Lord of lords, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:4">136:4</a> To him who alone doeth great wonders, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:5">136:5</a> To him that by understanding made the heavens, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:6">136:6</a> To him that stretched out the earth above the waters, for  his loving-kindness [endureth] for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:7">136:7</a> To him that made great lights, for his loving-kindness  [endureth] for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:8">136:8</a> The sun for rule over the day, for his loving-kindness  [endureth] for ever,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:9">136:9</a> The moon and stars for rule over the night, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:10">136:10</a> To him that smote Egypt in their firstborn, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:11">136:11</a> And brought out Israel from among them, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:12">136:12</a> With a powerful hand and with a stretched-out arm, for  his loving-kindness [endureth] for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:13">136:13</a> To him that divided the Red sea into parts, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:14">136:14</a> And made Israel to pass through the midst of it, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:15">136:15</a> And overturned Pharaoh and his host in the Red sea, for  his loving-kindness [endureth] for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:16">136:16</a> To him that led his people through the wilderness, for  his loving-kindness [endureth] for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:17">136:17</a> To him that smote great kings, for his loving-kindness  [endureth] for ever,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:18">136:18</a> And slew famous kings, for his loving-kindness [endureth]  for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:19">136:19</a> Sihon king of the Amorites, for his loving-kindness  [endureth] for ever,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:20">136:20</a> And Og king of Bashan, for his loving-kindness [endureth]  for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:21">136:21</a> And gave their land for an inheritance, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:22">136:22</a> An inheritance unto Israel his servant, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:23">136:23</a> Who hath remembered us in our low estate, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:24">136:24</a> And hath delivered us from our oppressors, for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:25">136:25</a> Who giveth food to all flesh, for his loving-kindness  [endureth] for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:26">136:26</a> Give ye thanks unto the ùGod of the heavens; for his  loving-kindness [endureth] for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:1">137:1</a> By the rivers of Babylon, there we sat down; yea, we wept  when we remembered Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:2">137:2</a> We hanged our harps upon the willows in the midst thereof.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:3">137:3</a> For there they that carried us away captive required of us  a song; and they that made us wail [required] mirth, [saying,]  Sing us [one] of the songs of Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:4">137:4</a> How should we sing a song of Jehovah's upon a foreign  soil?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:5">137:5</a> If I forget thee, Jerusalem, let my right hand forget [its  skill];</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:6">137:6</a> If I do not remember thee, let my tongue cleave to my  palate: if I prefer not Jerusalem above my chief joy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:7">137:7</a> Remember, O Jehovah, against the sons of Edom, the day of  Jerusalem; who said, Lay [it] bare, Lay [it] bare, down to its  foundation!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:8">137:8</a> Daughter of Babylon, who art to be laid waste, happy he  that rendereth unto thee that which thou hast meted out to us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:9">137:9</a> Happy he that taketh and dasheth thy little ones against  the rock.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:1">138:1</a> {[A Psalm] of David.} I will give thee thanks with my  whole heart; before the gods will I sing psalms of thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:2">138:2</a> I will bow down toward the temple of thy holiness, and  celebrate thy name for thy loving-kindness and for thy truth;  for thou hast magnified thy word above all thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:3">138:3</a> In the day when I called thou answeredst me; thou didst  encourage me with strength in my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:4">138:4</a> All the kings of the earth shall celebrate thee, Jehovah,  when they have heard the words of thy mouth;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:5">138:5</a> And they shall sing in the ways of Jehovah, for great is  the glory of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:6">138:6</a> For Jehovah is high; but he looketh upon the lowly, and  the proud he knoweth afar off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:7">138:7</a> Though I walk in the midst of trouble, thou wilt revive  me: thou wilt stretch forth thy hand against the anger of mine  enemies, and thy right hand shall save me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:8">138:8</a> Jehovah will perfect what concerneth me: thy  loving-kindness, O Jehovah, [endureth] for ever; forsake not  the works of thine own hands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:1">139:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David.} Jehovah, thou  hast searched me, and known [me].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:2">139:2</a> *Thou* knowest my down-sitting and mine uprising, thou  understandest my thought afar off;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:3">139:3</a> Thou searchest out my path and my lying down, and art  acquainted with all my ways;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:4">139:4</a> For there is not yet a word on my tongue, [but] lo, O  Jehovah, thou knowest it altogether.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:5">139:5</a> Thou hast beset me behind and before, and laid thy hand  upon me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:6">139:6</a> O knowledge too wonderful for me! it is high, I cannot  [attain] unto it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:7">139:7</a> Whither shall I go from thy Spirit? and whither flee from  thy presence?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:8">139:8</a> If I ascend up into the heavens thou art there; or if I  make my bed in Sheol, behold, thou [art there];</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:9">139:9</a> [If] I take the wings of the dawn [and] dwell in the  uttermost parts of the sea,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:10">139:10</a> Even there shall thy hand lead me, and thy right hand  shall hold me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:11">139:11</a> And if I say, Surely darkness shall cover me, and the  light about me be night;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:12">139:12</a> Even darkness hideth not from thee, and the night shineth  as the day: the darkness is as the light.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:13">139:13</a> For thou hast possessed my reins; thou didst cover me in  my mother's womb.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:14">139:14</a> I will praise thee, for I am fearfully, wonderfully made.  Marvellous are thy works; and [that] my soul knoweth right  well.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:15">139:15</a> My bones were not hidden from thee when I was made in  secret, curiously wrought in the lower parts of the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:16">139:16</a> Thine eyes did see my unformed substance, and in thy book  all [my members] were written; [during many] days were they  fashioned, when [as yet] there was none of them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:17">139:17</a> But how precious are thy thoughts unto me, O ùGod! how  great is the sum of them!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:18">139:18</a> [If] I would count them, they are more in number than the  sand. When I awake, I am still with thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:19">139:19</a> Oh that thou wouldest slay the wicked, O +God! And ye men  of blood, depart from me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:20">139:20</a> For they speak of thee wickedly, they take [thy name] in  vain, thine enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:21">139:21</a> Do not I hate them, O Jehovah, that hate thee? and do not  I loathe them that rise up against thee?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:22">139:22</a> I hate them with perfect hatred; I account them mine  enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:23">139:23</a> Search me, O ùGod, and know my heart; prove me, and know  my thoughts;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:24">139:24</a> And see if there be any grievous way in me; and lead me  in the way everlasting.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:1">140:1</a> {To the chief Musician. A Psalm of David.} Free me, O  Jehovah, from the evil man; preserve me from the violent man:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:2">140:2</a> Who devise mischiefs in [their] heart; every day are they  banded together for war.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:3">140:3</a> They sharpen their tongues like a serpent; adders' poison  is under their lips. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:4">140:4</a> Keep me, O Jehovah, from the hands of the wicked [man],  preserve me from the violent man, who devise to overthrow my  steps.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:5">140:5</a> The proud have hidden a snare for me, and cords; they have  spread a net by the way-side; they have set traps for me.  Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:6">140:6</a> I have said unto Jehovah, Thou art my ùGod: give ear, O  Jehovah, to the voice of my supplications.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:7">140:7</a> Jehovah, the Lord, is the strength of my salvation: thou  hast covered my head in the day of battle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:8">140:8</a> Grant not, O Jehovah, the desire of the wicked; further  not his device: they would exalt themselves. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:9">140:9</a> [As for] the head of those that encompass me, let the  mischief of their own lips cover them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:10">140:10</a> Let burning coals fall on them; let them be cast into the  fire; into deep waters, that they rise not up again.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:11">140:11</a> Let not the man of [evil] tongue be established in the  earth: evil shall hunt the man of violence to [his] ruin.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:12">140:12</a> I know that Jehovah will maintain the cause of the  afflicted one, the right of the needy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:13">140:13</a> Yea, the righteous shall give thanks unto thy name; the  upright shall dwell in thy presence.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:1">141:1</a> {A Psalm of David.} Jehovah, I have called upon thee: make  haste unto me; give ear unto my voice, when I call unto thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:2">141:2</a> Let my prayer be set forth before thee as incense, the  lifting up of my hands as the evening oblation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:3">141:3</a> Set a watch, O Jehovah, before my mouth; keep the door of  my lips.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:4">141:4</a> Incline not my heart to any evil thing, to practise deeds  of wickedness with men that are workers of iniquity; and let me  not eat of their dainties.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:5">141:5</a> Let the righteous smite me, it is kindness; and let him  reprove me, it is an excellent oil which my head shall not  refuse: for yet my prayer also is [for them] in their  calamities.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:6">141:6</a> When their judges are thrown down from the rocks, they  shall hear my words, for they are sweet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:7">141:7</a> Our bones are scattered at the mouth of Sheol, as when one  cutteth and cleaveth [wood] upon the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:8">141:8</a> For unto thee, Jehovah, Lord, are mine eyes; in thee do I  trust: leave not my soul destitute.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:9">141:9</a> Keep me from the snare which they have laid for me, and  from the traps of the workers of iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:10">141:10</a> Let the wicked fall into their own nets, whilst that *I*  withal pass over.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:1">142:1</a> {An instruction of David; when he was in the cave: a  prayer.} I cry unto Jehovah with my voice: with my voice unto  Jehovah do I make supplication.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:2">142:2</a> I pour out my plaint before him; I shew before him my  trouble.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:3">142:3</a> When my spirit was overwhelmed within me, then *thou*  knewest my path. In the way wherein I walked have they hidden a  snare for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:4">142:4</a> Look on the right hand and see; there is no man that  knoweth me: refuge hath failed me; no man careth for my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:5">142:5</a> I cried unto thee, Jehovah; I said, Thou art my refuge, my  portion in the land of the living.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:6">142:6</a> Attend unto my cry, for I am brought very low; deliver me  from my persecutors, for they are stronger than I.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:7">142:7</a> Bring my soul out of prison, that I may celebrate thy  name. The righteous shall surround me, because thou dealest  bountifully with me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:1">143:1</a> {A Psalm of David.} Jehovah, hear my prayer; give ear to  my supplications: in thy faithfulness answer me, in thy  righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:2">143:2</a> And enter not into judgment with thy servant; for in thy  sight no man living shall be justified.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:3">143:3</a> For the enemy persecuteth my soul: he hath crushed my life  down to the earth; he hath made me to dwell in dark places, as  those that have been long dead.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:4">143:4</a> And my spirit is overwhelmed within me; my heart within me  is desolate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:5">143:5</a> I remember the days of old: I meditate on all thy doing; I  muse on the work of thy hands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:6">143:6</a> I stretch forth my hands unto thee: my soul, as a parched  land, [thirsteth] after thee. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:7">143:7</a> Answer me speedily, O Jehovah; my spirit faileth: hide not  thy face from me, or I shall be like unto them that go down  into the pit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:8">143:8</a> Cause me to hear thy loving-kindness in the morning, for  in thee do I confide; make me to know the way wherein I should  walk, for unto thee do I lift up my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:9">143:9</a> Deliver me, O Jehovah, from mine enemies: unto thee do I  flee for refuge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:10">143:10</a> Teach me to do thy will; for thou art my God: let thy  good Spirit lead me in a plain country.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:11">143:11</a> Revive me, O Jehovah, for thy name's sake; in thy  righteousness bring my soul out of trouble;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:12">143:12</a> And in thy loving-kindness cut off mine enemies, and  destroy all them that oppress my soul: for I am thy servant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:1">144:1</a> {[A Psalm] of David.} Blessed be Jehovah my rock, who  teacheth my hands to war, my fingers to fight;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:2">144:2</a> My mercy and my fortress, my high tower and my deliverer,  my shield and he in whom I trust, who subdueth my people under  me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:3">144:3</a> Jehovah, what is man, that thou takest knowledge of him,  the son of man, that thou takest thought of him?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:4">144:4</a> Man is like to vanity; his days are as a shadow that  passeth away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:5">144:5</a> Jehovah, bow thy heavens, and come down; touch the  mountains, that they smoke;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:6">144:6</a> Cast forth lightnings, and scatter them; send forth thine  arrows, and discomfit them:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:7">144:7</a> Stretch out thy hands from above; rescue me, and deliver  me out of great waters, from the hand of aliens,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:8">144:8</a> Whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a  right hand of falsehood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:9">144:9</a> O God, I will sing a new song unto thee; with the  ten-stringed lute will I sing psalms unto thee:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:10">144:10</a> Who givest salvation unto kings; who rescuest David thy  servant from the hurtful sword.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:11">144:11</a> Rescue me, and deliver me from the hand of aliens, whose  mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a right hand of  falsehood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:12">144:12</a> That our sons may be as plants grown up in their youth;  our daughters as corner-columns, sculptured after the fashion  of a palace:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:13">144:13</a> Our granaries full, affording all manner of store; our  sheep bringing forth thousands, ten thousands in our pastures;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:14">144:14</a> Our kine laden [with young]; no breaking in and no going  forth, and no outcry in our streets.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:15">144:15</a> Blessed the people that is in such a case! Blessed the  people whose God is Jehovah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:1">145:1</a> {A Psalm of praise. Of David.} I will extol thee, my God,  O King, and I will bless thy name for ever and ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:2">145:2</a> Every day will I bless thee, and I will praise thy name  for ever and ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:3">145:3</a> Great is Jehovah, and exceedingly to be praised; and his  greatness is unsearchable.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:4">145:4</a> One generation shall laud thy works to another, and shall  declare thy mighty acts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:5">145:5</a> I will speak of the glorious splendour of thy majesty, and  of thy wondrous works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:6">145:6</a> And they shall tell of the might of thy terrible acts; and  thy great deeds will I declare.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:7">145:7</a> They shall abundantly utter the memory of thy great  goodness, and shall sing aloud of thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:8">145:8</a> Jehovah is gracious and merciful; slow to anger, and of  great loving-kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:9">145:9</a> Jehovah is good to all; and his tender mercies are over  all his works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:10">145:10</a> All thy works shall praise thee, Jehovah, and thy saints  shall bless thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:11">145:11</a> They shall tell of the glory of thy kingdom, and speak of  thy power;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:12">145:12</a> To make known to the children of men his mighty acts, and  the glorious splendour of his kingdom.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:13">145:13</a> Thy kingdom is a kingdom of all ages, and thy dominion is  throughout all generations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:14">145:14</a> Jehovah upholdeth all that fall, and raiseth up all that  are bowed down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:15">145:15</a> The eyes of all wait upon thee; and thou givest them  their food in its season.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:16">145:16</a> Thou openest thy hand, and satisfiest the desire of every  living thing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:17">145:17</a> Jehovah is righteous in all his ways, and kind in all his  works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:18">145:18</a> Jehovah is nigh unto all that call upon him, unto all  that call upon him in truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:19">145:19</a> He fulfilleth the desire of them that fear him; he  heareth their cry, and saveth them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:20">145:20</a> Jehovah keepeth all that love him, and all the wicked  will he destroy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:21">145:21</a> My mouth shall speak the praise of Jehovah; and let all  flesh bless his holy name for ever and ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:1">146:1</a> Hallelujah! Praise Jehovah, O my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:2">146:2</a> As long as I live will I praise Jehovah; I will sing  psalms unto my God while I have my being.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:3">146:3</a> Put not confidence in nobles, in a son of man, in whom  there is no salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:4">146:4</a> His breath goeth forth, he returneth to his earth; in that  very day his purposes perish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:5">146:5</a> Blessed is he who hath the ùGod of Jacob for his help,  whose hope is in Jehovah his God,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:6">146:6</a> Who made the heavens and the earth, the sea and all that  is therein; who keepeth truth for ever;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:7">146:7</a> Who executeth judgment for the oppressed, who giveth bread  to the hungry. Jehovah looseth the prisoners;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:8">146:8</a> Jehovah openeth [the eyes of] the blind; Jehovah raiseth  up them that are bowed down; Jehovah loveth the righteous;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:9">146:9</a> Jehovah preserveth the strangers; he lifteth up the  fatherless and the widow; but the way of the wicked doth he  subvert.</p>
