 <p><a name="an_146:10">146:10</a> Jehovah will reign for ever, [even] thy God, O Zion, from  generation to generation. Halleluiah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:1">147:1</a> Praise ye Jah! for it is good. Sing psalms of our God; for  it is pleasant: praise is comely.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:2">147:2</a> Jehovah doth build up Jerusalem: he gathereth the outcasts  of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:3">147:3</a> He healeth the broken in heart, and bindeth up their  wounds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:4">147:4</a> He counteth the number of the stars; he giveth names to  them all.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:5">147:5</a> Great is our Lord, and of great power: his understanding  is infinite.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:6">147:6</a> Jehovah lifteth up the meek; he abaseth the wicked to the  earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:7">147:7</a> Sing unto Jehovah with thanksgiving; sing psalms upon the  harp unto our God:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:8">147:8</a> Who covereth the heavens with clouds, who prepareth rain  for the earth, who maketh grass to grow upon the mountains;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:9">147:9</a> Who giveth to the cattle their food, to the young ravens  which cry.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:10">147:10</a> He delighteth not in the strength of the horse, he taketh  not pleasure in the legs of a man;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:11">147:11</a> Jehovah taketh pleasure in those that fear him, in those  that hope in his loving-kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:12">147:12</a> Laud Jehovah, O Jerusalem; praise thy God, O Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:13">147:13</a> For he hath strengthened the bars of thy gates; he hath  blessed thy children within thee;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:14">147:14</a> He maketh peace in thy borders; he satisfieth thee with  the finest of the wheat.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:15">147:15</a> He sendeth forth his oracles to the earth: his word  runneth very swiftly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:16">147:16</a> He giveth snow like wool, scattereth the hoar frost like  ashes;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:17">147:17</a> He casteth forth his ice like morsels: who can stand  before his cold?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:18">147:18</a> He sendeth his word, and melteth them; he causeth his  wind to blow -- the waters flow.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:19">147:19</a> He sheweth his word unto Jacob, his statutes and his  judgments unto Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:20">147:20</a> He hath not dealt thus with any nation; and as for [his]  judgments, they have not known them. Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:1">148:1</a> Hallelujah! Praise Jehovah from the heavens; praise him in  the heights.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:2">148:2</a> Praise ye him, all his angels; praise ye him, all his  hosts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:3">148:3</a> Praise him, sun and moon; praise him, all ye stars of  light.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:4">148:4</a> Praise him, ye heavens of heavens, and ye waters that are  above the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:5">148:5</a> Let them praise the name of Jehovah, for he it is that  commanded, and they were created:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:6">148:6</a> And he established them for ever and ever; he made [for  them] a statute which shall not pass.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:7">148:7</a> Praise Jehovah from the earth, ye sea-monsters, and all  deeps;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:8">148:8</a> Fire and hail, snow and vapour, stormy wind fulfilling his  word;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:9">148:9</a> Mountains and all hills, fruit-trees and all cedars;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:10">148:10</a> Beasts and all cattle, creeping things and winged fowl;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:11">148:11</a> Kings of the earth and all peoples, princes and all  judges of the earth;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:12">148:12</a> Both young men and maidens, old men with youths, --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:13">148:13</a> Let them praise the name of Jehovah: for his name alone  is exalted; his majesty is above the earth and the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:14">148:14</a> And he hath lifted up the horn of his people, the praise  of all his saints, [even] of the children of Israel, a people  near unto him. Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:1">149:1</a> Hallelujah! Sing unto Jehovah a new song; [sing] his  praise in the congregation of the godly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:2">149:2</a> Let Israel rejoice in his Maker; let the sons of Zion be  joyful in their King.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:3">149:3</a> Let them praise his name in the dance; let them sing  psalms unto him with the tambour and harp.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:4">149:4</a> For Jehovah taketh pleasure in his people; he beautifieth  the meek with salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:5">149:5</a> Let the godly exult in glory; let them shout for joy upon  their beds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:6">149:6</a> Let the high praises of ùGod be in their mouth, and a  two-edged sword in their hand:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:7">149:7</a> To execute vengeance against the nations, [and] punishment  among the peoples;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:8">149:8</a> To bind their kings with chains, and their nobles with  fetters of iron;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:9">149:9</a> To execute upon them the judgment written. This honour  have all his saints. Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:1">150:1</a> Hallelujah! Praise ùGod in his sanctuary; praise him in  the firmament of his power.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:2">150:2</a> Praise him in his mighty acts; praise him according to the  abundance of his greatness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:3">150:3</a> Praise him with the sound of the trumpet; praise him with  lute and harp;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:4">150:4</a> Praise him with the tambour and dance; praise him with  stringed instruments and the pipe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:5">150:5</a> Praise him with loud cymbals; praise him with high  sounding cymbals.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:6">150:6</a> Let everything that hath breath praise Jah. Hallelujah!</p> 
 <p></p><hr>
